*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Spain](/images/thumb/5/58/Spain.png/20px-Spain.png)](/Spain "Spain") [Spain](/Spain "Spain")
*   [![Global settler increase.png](/images/thumb/2/2b/Global_settler_increase.png/28px-Global_settler_increase.png)](/Global_settler_increase "Global settler increase") Have colonial nations in Mexico, Panama, Havana, and Cuzco.

In the Name of the Father

It's all about luck

Just Resting In My Account

[1.16](/1.16 "1.16")

E

[![Kow-Tow icon](/images/0/0a/Kow-Tow.png)](/File:Kow-Tow.png "Kow-Tow icon")

[Kow-Tow](/Kow-Tow "Kow-Tow")

As Ming, have a subject from each religion group.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Ming](/images/thumb/a/a5/Ming.png/20px-Ming.png)](/Ming "Ming") [Ming](/Ming "Ming")

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Vassal.png](/images/thumb/4/47/Vassal.png/28px-Vassal.png)](/Vassal "Vassal") Have a subject nation in the 5 [religious groups](/Religious_group "Religious group") Christian, Muslim, Eastern, Dharmic and Pagan

*   The Jewish and Zoroastrian groups are _not_ needed.
*   No CB War against [Mikhlaf](/Mikhlaf "Mikhlaf") in Arabia, vassalize them in the peace deal. Ally a neighbour (Yemen or Hormuz can be a good choice), ask for maps of the horn of Africa and then establish one of the Coptic minors as a tributary or vassal. Medri Bahri can be a good choice. Proclaim a Guarantee to protect them while you improve relations.

[1.9](/1.9 "1.9")

E

[![Land of Eastern Jade icon](/images/2/28/Land_of_Eastern_Jade.jpg)](/File:Land_of_Eastern_Jade.jpg "Land of Eastern Jade icon")

Land of Eastern Jade

Own a core province in Central America as a Buddhist country.

[![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World").

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Be [![Theravada.png](/images/thumb/5/52/Theravada.png/28px-Theravada.png)](/Theravada "Theravada") Theravada, [![Vajrayana.png](/images/thumb/f/f1/Vajrayana.png/28px-Vajrayana.png)](/Vajrayana "Vajrayana") Vajrayana, or [![Mahayana.png](/images/thumb/2/2f/Mahayana.png/28px-Mahayana.png)](/Mahayana "Mahayana") Mahayana.
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own a core province in the region [Mexico](/North_American_regions#Mexico "North American regions").

Contrary to the Steam description of the achievement, a province in the region Mexico is necessary and not a province in the region Central America.

An interesting choice is Ayutthaya. Start by choosing exploration ideas, colonize the islands in Indonesia, followed by the Marshall Islands, and Midway. Then focus on North America, and most likely you can colonize Sinaloa, which is the easiest path for this achievement.

[1.8](/1.8 "1.8")

E

[![Let It Go! icon](/images/0/08/Let_It_Go%21.png)](/File:Let_It_Go!.png "Let It Go! icon")

Let It Go!

Starting as Norway, have your capital in the Canada region while not owning any province in Scandinavia and not playing as a released subject.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Norway](/images/thumb/0/0f/Norway.png/20px-Norway.png)](/Norway "Norway") [Norway](/Norway "Norway")

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Capital.png](/images/thumb/6/6e/Capital.png/28px-Capital.png)](/Capital "Capital") Capital is in the [Canada region](/Canada_(region) "Canada (region)")
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") Owns no province in the [Scandinavia region](/Scandinavia_(region) "Scandinavia (region)")

Forming countries is allowed, but playing as a released colonial nation or switching to a different country is not allowed. The easiest way to be rid of provinces in Europe is to release Sápmi and Iceland as subjects, giving them all other provinces in Europe other than your capital. At that point, moving your capital into America is allowed, and then giving away the last European province should complete the achievement.

[1.34](/1.34 "1.34")

E

[![Made in Japan icon](/images/3/3d/Made_in_Japan.png)](/File:Made_in_Japan.png "Made in Japan icon")

Made in Japan

Embrace "manufactories" institution as Japan by 1655.

[![Culture icon.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Culture_icon.png/28px-Culture_icon.png)](/Culture "Culture") Culture group is _Japanese_

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") The year is before 1655
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Japan](/images/thumb/f/fc/Japan.png/20px-Japan.png)](/Japan "Japan") [Japan](/Japan "Japan")
*   [![Institutions.png](/images/thumb/4/43/Institutions.png/28px-Institutions.png)](/Institutions "Institutions") Has embraced the [![Manufactories](/images/thumb/c/c4/Manufactories.png/28px-Manufactories.png)](/Institutions#Manufactories "Manufactories") Manufactories institution

Colonize the west coast of America as soon as possible to gain Colonialism. Do not enforce Sakoku when the option presents itself, since that will make it harder to get Global Trade.

[1.20](/1.20 "1.20")

E

[![Magellan’s Voyage icon](/images/b/be/Magellan%E2%80%99s_Voyage.jpg)](/File:Magellan%E2%80%99s_Voyage.jpg "Magellan’s Voyage icon")

Magellan’s Voyage

Make the first circumnavigation.

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is the first to circumnavigate the World.

Colonize along the route as much as possible, or get fleet basing rights. Fully-repaired ships can be stationed along the way to join the explorer's fleet before he moves to the next sea tile. If the fleet stops to repair, ships can also be sent to augment it while it is in port. How long the AI takes to circumnavigate varies from game to game.

[![El Dorado.png](/images/thumb/1/16/El_Dorado.png/28px-El_Dorado.png)](/El_Dorado "El Dorado")

[1.10](/1.10 "1.10")

E

[![Maharana Pratap icon](/images/7/71/Maharana_Pratap.png)](/File:Maharana_Pratap.png "Maharana Pratap icon")

Maharana Pratap

Start as Mewar and field an army of 20 Rajput regiments.

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Mewar](/images/thumb/7/7d/Mewar.png/20px-Mewar.png)](/Mewar "Mewar") [Mewar](/Mewar "Mewar")

[![Infantry.png](/images/thumb/9/9f/Infantry.png/28px-Infantry.png)](/Infantry "Infantry") Has at least 20 Rajput regiments

See [Rajput regiment](/Rajput_regiment "Rajput regiment") and [Special unit force limit](/Special_unit_force_limit "Special unit force limit") for ways to get more Rajput regiments. Forming another country such as Rajputana does not prevent the achievement, but the formed country will still need to have access to the [![Rajputs.png](/images/thumb/5/56/Rajputs.png/28px-Rajputs.png)](/Rajputs "Rajputs") Rajputs estate.

[![Dharma.png](/images/thumb/f/fc/Dharma.png/28px-Dharma.png)](/Dharma "Dharma")

[1.26](/1.26 "1.26")

E

[![Multiculturalism icon](/images/7/7e/Multiculturalism.png)](/File:Multiculturalism.png "Multiculturalism icon")

Multiculturalism

Have 4 different Cultures and 4 different religions represented in your court.

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") No more than 1 custom nation exists in the world
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") Used no more than 201 nation designer points if playing as a custom nation

*   [![Advisor.png](/images/thumb/6/6a/Advisor.png/28px-Advisor.png)](/Advisor "Advisor") Four different religions in court
*   [![Culture icon.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Culture_icon.png/28px-Culture_icon.png)](/Culture "Culture") Four different cultures in court

Spawned advisors take the culture and religion of a random held province. Easy as [![Flag of Ming](/images/thumb/a/a5/Ming.png/20px-Ming.png)](/Ming "Ming") [Ming](/Ming "Ming"): dismiss advisors until you have one Theravada, one Animist, and one Vajrayana advisor. Release nations to increase the proportion of your provinces which have one of the remaining religions.

[![Nation designer.png](/images/a/ab/Nation_designer.png)](/Nation_designer "Nation designer")

[![My True Friend icon](/images/f/fd/My_True_Friend.jpg)](/File:My_True_Friend.jpg "My True Friend icon")

My True Friend

Go to war in support of a rebel faction and win, enforcing their demands.

[![Rebel support efficiency.png](/images/thumb/d/d7/Rebel_support_efficiency.png/28px-Rebel_support_efficiency.png)](/Rebel_support_efficiency "Rebel support efficiency") Help a [rebel faction](/Rebel_faction "Rebel faction") win a war against another country

Can be completed at the same time as the Viva la Revolución! achievement.

[![Art of War.png](/images/thumb/0/0f/Art_of_War.png/28px-Art_of_War.png)](/Art_of_War "Art of War")

[1.8](/1.8 "1.8")

E

[![Networking icon](/images/c/c0/Networking.jpg)](/File:Networking.jpg "Networking icon")

Networking

Have 100 point spy networks in 3 Rival nations.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Have 100 point spy networks in 3 rival nations

Hard to get with [![Mare Nostrum.png](/images/thumb/f/ff/Mare_Nostrum.png/28px-Mare_Nostrum.png)](/Mare_Nostrum "Mare Nostrum") Mare Nostrum enabled since AI will use [counter-espionage](/Espionage#Counter-espionage "Espionage") against rivals.

A slow but easy method involves starting as a nation with at least 3 diplomats, building the spy networks in your rival nations and waiting until you get the achievement or annexed.

[![Nation designer.png](/images/a/ab/Nation_designer.png)](/Nation_designer "Nation designer")

[1.16](/1.16 "1.16")

E

[![Nobody wants to die icon](/images/f/fd/Nobody_wants_to_die.jpg)](/File:Nobody_wants_to_die.jpg "Nobody wants to die icon")

Nobody wants to die

Own Timbuktu as Songhai

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Songhai](/images/thumb/2/24/Songhai.png/20px-Songhai.png)](/Songhai "Songhai") [Songhai](/Songhai "Songhai")

[![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own and core the province of Timbuktu

Can be done swiftly by declaring a no-[casus belli](/Casus_belli "Casus belli") war a month from the start of the game, before any alliances are made. Hiring a handful of mercenaries will help with the conquest, whereas hiring an administrative advisor and changing the [national focus](/National_focus "National focus") to administrative will help to core the province sooner.

[1.3](/1.3 "1.3")

E

[![On the Edge of Madness icon](/images/5/53/On_the_Edge_of_Madness.jpg)](/File:On_the_Edge_of_Madness.jpg "On the Edge of Madness icon")

[On the Edge of Madness](/On_the_Edge_of_Madness "On the Edge of Madness")

As Aztecs, reach 95 Doom, then go 20 years without Doom hitting 100.

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Aztec](/images/thumb/e/ef/Aztec.png/20px-Aztec.png)](/Aztec "Aztec") [Aztec](/Aztec "Aztec")
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World")

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Reach 95 Doom, then survive for 20 years without hitting 100 Doom. Had the flag _doom\_reached\_95_ for 20 years _and_ do not have flag _doom\_reached\_100_

It is not required to keep doom between 95 and 100 for 20 years, but make sure you are at 95 doom at least once when a month tick happens so the countdown actually starts. Doom may drop below 95 at any time. Passing religious reforms (except the Reform Religion button, which disables doom) will also not prevent the achievement.

[![El Dorado.png](/images/thumb/1/16/El_Dorado.png/28px-El_Dorado.png)](/El_Dorado "El Dorado")

[1.10](/1.10 "1.10")

E

[![One Family to Rule them All icon](/images/7/78/One_Family_to_Rule_them_All.jpg)](/File:One_Family_to_Rule_them_All.jpg "One Family to Rule them All icon")

One Family to Rule them All

Have your dynasty on 8 thrones at the same time. Client states do not count.

*   [![Government monarchy.png](/images/thumb/4/4d/Government_monarchy.png/28px-Government_monarchy.png)](/Monarchy "Monarchy") Is monarchy
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") Is _not_ in a regency
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Have the same [dynasty](/Dynasty "Dynasty") as 8 other non-client state nations

Can be easily done as [![Flag of Ming](/images/thumb/a/a5/Ming.png/20px-Ming.png)](/Ming "Ming") [Ming](/Ming "Ming"). Release 8 nations as vassals (make sure you pick nations that will have an eastern religion) and use the _Place Relative on Throne_ [Subject interaction](/Subject_nation#Subject_interactions "Subject nation"). This requires the [![Common Sense.png](/images/thumb/e/e4/Common_Sense.png/28px-Common_Sense.png)](/Common_Sense "Common Sense") Common Sense DLC.

[1.12](/1.12 "1.12")

E

[![One King to Rule! icon](/images/d/d2/One_King_to_Rule%21.jpg)](/File:One_King_to_Rule!.jpg "One King to Rule! icon")

[One King to Rule!](/One_King_to_Rule! "One King to Rule!")

As Poland, become an absolutist monarchy, abolishing the Sejm.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Poland](/images/thumb/9/99/Poland.png/20px-Poland.png)](/Poland "Poland") [Poland](/Poland "Poland")

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Government monarchy.png](/images/thumb/4/4d/Government_monarchy.png/28px-Government_monarchy.png)](/Monarchy "Monarchy") Is a monarchy
*   [![Absolutism.png](/images/thumb/c/c2/Absolutism.png/28px-Absolutism.png)](/Absolutism "Absolutism") Have 50 [absolutism](/Absolutism "Absolutism")
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") Has _not_ enacted one of the following government reforms:
    *   ‘[Elective Monarchy](/Monarchy#Elective_Monarchy "Monarchy")’
    *   ‘[Great Sejm](/Great_Sejm "Great Sejm")’
    *   ‘[Polish Elective Monarchy](/Polish_Elective_Monarchy "Polish Elective Monarchy")’

[![One Night in Paris icon](/images/e/e9/One_Night_in_Paris.jpg)](/File:One_Night_in_Paris.jpg "One Night in Paris icon")

[One Night in Paris](/One_Night_in_Paris "One Night in Paris")

Start as England, own and have a core on Paris (do not form another country unless it's Great Britain).

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of England](/images/thumb/2/21/England.png/20px-England.png)](/England "England") [England](/England "England")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of England](/images/thumb/2/21/England.png/20px-England.png)](/England "England") [England](/England "England"), [![Flag of Great Britain](/images/thumb/2/2b/Great_Britain.png/20px-Great_Britain.png)](/Great_Britain "Great Britain") [Great Britain](/Great_Britain "Great Britain"), _or_ the [![Flag of Angevin Kingdom](/images/thumb/b/be/Angevin_Kingdom.png/20px-Angevin_Kingdom.png)](/Angevin_Kingdom "Angevin Kingdom") [Angevin Kingdom](/Angevin_Kingdom "Angevin Kingdom")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own and core Paris

Despite the Steam description, forming the [![Flag of Angevin Kingdom](/images/thumb/b/be/Angevin_Kingdom.png/20px-Angevin_Kingdom.png)](/Angevin_Kingdom "Angevin Kingdom") [Angevin Kingdom](/Angevin_Kingdom "Angevin Kingdom") is allowed (and will complete the achievement provided France owns Paris).

Pirate Bay of Janjira

E

[![Purify the Temple icon](/images/b/ba/Purify_the_Temple.png)](/File:Purify_the_Temple.png "Purify the Temple icon")

Purify the Temple

Starting as Riga, enact the Salvific Plutocracy government reform and raid the heretic church of Rome.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Riga](/images/thumb/4/4c/Riga.png/20px-Riga.png)](/Riga "Riga") [Riga](/Riga "Riga")

*   [![Government theocracy.png](/images/thumb/8/81/Government_theocracy.png/28px-Government_theocracy.png)](/Theocracy "Theocracy") Has enacted the [Salvific Plutocracy](/Salvific_Plutocracy "Salvific Plutocracy") government reform
*   Raided the province Roma (118) with the peace term _“Raid Heretic Churches”_

_“Raid Heretic Churches”_ always selects Roma (118) as long as it has a Church or Cathedral. You need to convert to another Christian religion to enact [Salvific Plutocracy](/Salvific_Plutocracy "Salvific Plutocracy"). _“Raid Heretic Churches”_ can also be chosen for secondary war participants.

[![Lions of the North.png](/images/thumb/c/cd/Lions_of_the_North.png/28px-Lions_of_the_North.png)](/Lions_of_the_North "Lions of the North")

[1.34](/1.34 "1.34")

E

[![Queen of Mercury icon](/images/5/5c/Queen_of_Mercury.jpg)](/File:Queen_of_Mercury.jpg "Queen of Mercury icon")

Queen of Mercury

As Kilwa, own and have cores on Zanzibar and Bombay (Thana).

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Kilwa](/images/thumb/c/cb/Kilwa.png/20px-Kilwa.png)](/Kilwa "Kilwa") [Kilwa](/Kilwa "Kilwa")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Kilwa](/images/thumb/c/cb/Kilwa.png/20px-Kilwa.png)](/Kilwa "Kilwa") [Kilwa](/Kilwa "Kilwa")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own and core Zanzibar and Thana.

*   Since Kilwa starts with Zanzibar, essentially the goal is to expand to Thana on the west coast of India which is owned by Gujarat at the start of the game. If you form any nation, you will be ineligible for the achievement.
*   Much easier with the [![Dharma.png](/images/thumb/f/fc/Dharma.png/28px-Dharma.png)](/Dharma "Dharma") Dharma expansion, as you can simply charter Thana off its owner.
*   Freddie Mercury, the lead singer of Queen, was born in Zanzibar and raised in Zanzibar and Bombay. He and his family were Zoroastrian.

[1.6](/1.6 "1.6")

E

[![Relentless Push East icon](/images/7/79/Relentless_Push_East.png)](/File:Relentless_Push_East.png "Relentless Push East icon")

Relentless Push East

Starting as a Russian nation, By 1600 own the East Siberian Coastline.

[![Culture icon.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Culture_icon.png/28px-Culture_icon.png)](/Culture "Culture") Culture group is _East Slavic_

*   [![Time Icon.png](/images/7/70/Time_Icon.png)](/Time "Time") Year is before 1601
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own all port provinces in the _[East Siberia](/East_Siberia "East Siberia")_ region

Expand

[![Relentless Push East map.png](/images/thumb/e/e0/Relentless_Push_East_map.png/140px-Relentless_Push_East_map.png)](/File:Relentless_Push_East_map.png)

[](/File:Relentless_Push_East_map.png "Enlarge")

These provinces are Kamchatka, Penzhina, Kagyrgyn, Gizhiga, Tauisk, Okhotsk and Jugjur.

*   Note that it is not necessary to core the provinces. Even unfinished colonies count.
*   This achievement is pretty easy to reach as [![Flag of Muscovy](/images/thumb/4/41/Muscovy.png/20px-Muscovy.png)](/Muscovy "Muscovy") [Muscovy](/Muscovy "Muscovy") and you can finish it 40 to 50 years before the deadline. It is recommended to form [![Flag of Russia](/images/thumb/e/ee/Russia.png/20px-Russia.png)](/Russia "Russia") [Russia](/Russia "Russia") and take advantage of their Siberian Frontier idea, helping idea groups like exploration and expansion will then be optional. But a colonist from these groups can be used to start colonies if the time runs out and one of the Siberian ports has already been cored or fully colonized.

[1.22](/1.22 "1.22")

E

[![Respected icon](/images/3/33/Respected.jpg)](/File:Respected.jpg "Respected icon")

Respected

Have 100 prestige, 100 legitimacy and three stability.

*   [![Yearly prestige.png](/images/thumb/f/f3/Yearly_prestige.png/28px-Yearly_prestige.png)](/Prestige "Prestige") Have **100** prestige
*   [![Legitimacy.png](/images/2/25/Legitimacy.png)](/Legitimacy "Legitimacy") Have **100** legitimacy
*   [![Stability.png](/images/a/ae/Stability.png)](/Stability "Stability") Have **+3** stability

*   Fight battles and explore terra incognita to increase prestige.
*   Maintain positive stability, have heirs with strong claim and control the amount of royal marriages to increase legitimacy.
*   Wait for stability improving events and invest administrative points to increase stability.
*   Easy to achieve as [![Flag of Russia](/images/thumb/e/ee/Russia.png/20px-Russia.png)](/Russia "Russia") [Russia](/Russia "Russia"). The decision _“[Make St. Petersburg the Capital](/Russia#Make_St._Petersburg_the_Capital "Russia")”_ gives the player [![Yearly prestige.png](/images/thumb/f/f3/Yearly_prestige.png/28px-Yearly_prestige.png)](/Prestige "Prestige") **100** prestige, which fulfills the most difficult requirement if the player had non-negative prestige.
*   Having a level 3 advisor or higher will eventually cause an event to trigger that will let the player choose to gain [![Yearly prestige.png](/images/thumb/f/f3/Yearly_prestige.png/28px-Yearly_prestige.png)](/Prestige "Prestige") **50** prestige.

[![Nation designer.png](/images/a/ab/Nation_designer.png)](/Nation_designer "Nation designer")

[1.1](/Patch_1.1.X "Patch 1.1.X")

E

[![Royal Authority icon](/images/c/ce/Royal_Authority.jpg)](/File:Royal_Authority.jpg "Royal Authority icon")

[Royal Authority](/Royal_Authority "Royal Authority")

Install a union through a succession war.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Have installed a union in a succession war.

*   Win a war with the "Claim on Throne" or "Restore Union" [casus belli](/Casus_belli "Casus belli"). The former is used in succession wars. Only requires winning a war with the right CB; the peace deal does not actually need to force a union.
*   Easily done as [![Flag of Muscovy](/images/thumb/4/41/Muscovy.png/20px-Muscovy.png)](/Muscovy "Muscovy") [Muscovy](/Muscovy "Muscovy") against [![Flag of Ryazan](/images/thumb/7/7b/Ryazan.png/20px-Ryazan.png)](/Ryazan "Ryazan") [Ryazan](/Ryazan "Ryazan"), or against [![Flag of Tver](/images/thumb/3/35/Tver.png/20px-Tver.png)](/Tver "Tver") [Tver](/Tver "Tver") with a claim on throne.

[1.1](/Patch_1.1.X "Patch 1.1.X")

[![Rozwi Empire icon](/images/7/7b/Rozwi_Empire.jpg)](/File:Rozwi_Empire.jpg "Rozwi Empire icon")

Rozwi Empire

Starting as Butua, conquer Mutapa (Zimbabwe and Lower Zambezi areas).

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Butua](/images/thumb/9/92/Butua.png/20px-Butua.png)](/Butua "Butua") [Butua](/Butua "Butua")

*   Own all provinces in the following areas:
    *   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") [Butua](/African_regions#Butua "African regions")
    *   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") [Lower Zambezi](/African_regions#Lower_Zambezi "African regions")
    *   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") [Zimbabwe](/African_regions#Zimbabwe "African regions")

Expand

[![Rozwi Empire map.png](/images/thumb/3/32/Rozwi_Empire_map.png/140px-Rozwi_Empire_map.png)](/File:Rozwi_Empire_map.png)

[](/File:Rozwi_Empire_map.png "Enlarge")

Easy only with [![Conquest of Paradise.png](/images/thumb/3/31/Conquest_of_Paradise.png/28px-Conquest_of_Paradise.png)](/Conquest_of_Paradise "Conquest of Paradise") Conquest of Paradise or [![El Dorado.png](/images/thumb/1/16/El_Dorado.png/28px-El_Dorado.png)](/El_Dorado "El Dorado") El Dorado DLC. Starting in 1444 you can always get Kilwa (and at least one of these: Tumbuka, Maravi, Makua) to support your independence. Declare war ASAP and boost your gold production.

Without either of these DLCs, you're on your own. Save up money and build an army when Mutapa has started integrating you.

[![Shemot is Not icon](/images/c/cd/Shemot_is_Not.png)](/File:Shemot_is_Not.png "Shemot is Not icon")

Shemot is Not

As a Jewish nation, convert all of Egypt to Jewish while having the Jewish Community Aspect active.

*   [![Tolerance of the true faith.png](/images/thumb/d/d9/Tolerance_of_the_true_faith.png/28px-Tolerance_of_the_true_faith.png)](/Tolerance_of_the_true_faith "Tolerance of the true faith") Religion is [![Jewish.png](/images/thumb/c/cd/Jewish.png/28px-Jewish.png)](/Jewish "Jewish") Jewish
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") The church aspect “_Jewish Community_” is active
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") All provinces in the Egypt region are [![Jewish.png](/images/thumb/c/cd/Jewish.png/28px-Jewish.png)](/Jewish "Jewish") Jewish

Expand

[![Shemot is Not map.png](/images/thumb/c/cf/Shemot_is_Not_map.png/140px-Shemot_is_Not_map.png)](/File:Shemot_is_Not_map.png)

[](/File:Shemot_is_Not_map.png "Enlarge")

Easiest to do as [![Flag of Mamluks](/images/thumb/c/ca/The_Mamluks.png/20px-The_Mamluks.png)](/Mamluks "Mamluks") [Mamluks](/Mamluks "Mamluks"). Conquer Semien (and Dembiya) in [![Flag of Ethiopia](/images/thumb/0/06/Ethiopia.png/20px-Ethiopia.png)](/Ethiopia "Ethiopia") [Ethiopia](/Ethiopia "Ethiopia") and immediately send a missionary with 0 maintenance to switch the rebels to Jewish Zealots (before the previous rebel type in the province has reached 30% progress). Let the rebels spawn and let them convert the country. Once Jewish has become the [dominant religion](/Dominant_religion "Dominant religion"), the rebel demands will also include to change the state religion. Then the demands can be accepted, but it might be beneficial to let them convert more provinces. After becoming Jewish, finish converting Egypt and choose Jewish Community as your first aspect.

[![Origins.png](/images/thumb/8/8e/Origins.png/28px-Origins.png)](/Origins "Origins")

Sikh Pun

[![Strait Talk icon](/images/d/d1/Strait_Talk.jpg)](/File:Strait_Talk.jpg "Strait Talk icon")

[Strait Talk](/Strait_Talk "Strait Talk")

As Hormuz, have at least 10 diplomatic reputation

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Hormuz](/images/thumb/f/fa/Hormuz.png/20px-Hormuz.png)](/Hormuz "Hormuz") [Hormuz](/Hormuz "Hormuz")

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Hormuz](/images/thumb/f/fa/Hormuz.png/20px-Hormuz.png)](/Hormuz "Hormuz") [Hormuz](/Hormuz "Hormuz")
*   [![Diplomatic reputation.png](/images/thumb/2/21/Diplomatic_reputation.png/28px-Diplomatic_reputation.png)](/Diplomatic_reputation "Diplomatic reputation") Has at least 10 diplomatic reputation

Diplomatic reputation is gained from Hormuz ideas and completing missions. Easier since 1.24 since one of Islam's taxation policies gives +1 Diplomatic reputation.

Forming other nations _will_ prevent this achievement.

[![Surfing USA icon](/images/9/97/Surfing_USA.png)](/File:Surfing_USA.png "Surfing USA icon")

Surfing USA

Form the USA as Hawaii.

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World")
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Hawai'i](/images/thumb/8/8b/HAW.png/20px-HAW.png)](/Oceanian_super-region#Hawai.27i "Hawai'i")[Hawai'i](/Oceanian_super-region#Hawai.27i "Oceanian super-region"), [![Flag of Maui](/images/thumb/4/40/Maui.png/20px-Maui.png)](/Maui "Maui") [Maui](/Maui "Maui"), [![Flag of O'ahu](/images/thumb/9/9c/O%27ahu.png/20px-O%27ahu.png)](/O%27ahu "O'ahu") [O'ahu](/O%27ahu "O'ahu") _or_ [![Flag of Kaua'i](/images/thumb/3/32/Kaua%27i.png/20px-Kaua%27i.png)](/Kaua%27i "Kaua'i") [Kaua'i](/Kaua%27i "Kaua'i")

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of USA](/images/thumb/3/32/United_States.png/20px-United_States.png)](/USA "USA") [USA](/USA "USA")

It is advised to not colonise the nearby islands in your region. To form [![Flag of USA](/images/thumb/3/32/United_States.png/20px-United_States.png)](/USA "USA") [USA](/USA "USA") you need to move your capital to the Colonial Eastern America region, and to be able to do that you will need to move your capital. This can be done if it's the only province in a state, i,e, Hawaii. Consider releasing vassals in your home islands to achieve this.

[1.32](/1.32 "1.32")

E

[![Sweet Home Qaraqorum icon](/images/d/d6/Sweet_Home_Qaraqorum.png)](/File:Sweet_Home_Qaraqorum.png "Sweet Home Qaraqorum icon")

Sweet Home Qaraqorum

As the Mughals assimilate Mongolian culture.

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Mughals](/images/thumb/e/e6/Mughals.png/20px-Mughals.png)](/Mughals "Mughals") [Mughals](/Mughals "Mughals")
*   [![Government monarchy.png](/images/thumb/4/4d/Government_monarchy.png/28px-Government_monarchy.png)](/Monarchy "Monarchy") Has the [Mughal Diwan](/Mughal_Diwan "Mughal Diwan") government reform
*   [![Max promoted cultures.png](/images/thumb/8/8b/Max_promoted_cultures.png/28px-Max_promoted_cultures.png)](/Max_promoted_cultures "Max promoted cultures") Have Mongol as accepted culture

Easiest by starting as the [![Flag of Timurids](/images/thumb/6/6a/Timurids.png/20px-Timurids.png)](/Timurids "Timurids") [Timurids](/Timurids "Timurids"). Forming the Mughals should not be a problem as long as you keep your vassals loyal and conquer Delhi. After that you should carve your way up to the Mongolian culture area. Fabricate claims along the way and conquer the provinces needed to reach that area. Usually you can start by declaring war on Uzbek, followed by Oirat. The factions controlling those provinces differ from campaign to campaign. In order to assimilate you need to conquer ALL Mongolian culture provinces.

[![Dharma.png](/images/thumb/f/fc/Dharma.png/28px-Dharma.png)](/Dharma "Dharma")

[1.26](/1.26 "1.26")

E

[![The Coin is Stronger than the Sword icon](/images/f/fc/The_Coin_is_Stronger_than_the_Sword.png)](/File:The_Coin_is_Stronger_than_the_Sword.png "The Coin is Stronger than the Sword icon")

The Coin is Stronger than the Sword

Charter Company from an Indian nation.

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") No more than 1 custom nation exists in the world
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") Used no more than 201 nation designer points

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Has successfully used the Charter Trade Company diplomatic interaction to buy a province in India.

Chartering a province from outside India proper will _not_ grant the achievement (e.g. buying the Maldives from [![Flag of Vijayanagar](/images/thumb/3/31/Vijayanagar.png/20px-Vijayanagar.png)](/Vijayanagar "Vijayanagar") [Vijayanagar](/Vijayanagar "Vijayanagar")), but chartering a province in India from a country which has it's capital somewhere else works.

[![Dharma.png](/images/thumb/f/fc/Dharma.png/28px-Dharma.png)](/Dharma "Dharma")

*   [![Nation designer.png](/images/a/ab/Nation_designer.png)](/Nation_designer "Nation designer")

[1.26](/1.26 "1.26")

E

[![The Emperors new clothes icon](/images/c/c3/The_Emperor%27s_new_clothes.jpg)](/File:The_Emperor%27s_new_clothes.jpg "The Emperors new clothes icon")

The Emperors new clothes

Overthrow Austria and become the Emperor of the Holy Roman Empire.

[![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") Not playing as [![Flag of Austria](/images/thumb/7/7f/Austria.png/20px-Austria.png)](/Austria "Austria") [Austria](/Austria "Austria")

[![Imperial authority.png](/images/thumb/4/46/Imperial_authority.png/28px-Imperial_authority.png)](/Imperial_authority "Imperial authority") Is emperor of the [Holy Roman Empire](/Holy_Roman_Empire "Holy Roman Empire")

Become emperor of the Holy Roman Empire. Austrian players already start as the emperor so they won't get the achievement. Easiest to do as Bohemia.

[1.1](/Patch_1.1.X "Patch 1.1.X")

E

[![The Five Colonies icon](/images/1/16/The_Five_Colonies.jpg)](/File:The_Five_Colonies.jpg "The Five Colonies icon")

The Five Colonies

Have five colonial nations.

[![Subject colony icon.png](/images/thumb/d/de/Subject_colony_icon.png/28px-Subject_colony_icon.png)](/Colonial_nation "Colonial nation") have 5 colonial nations

*   Is an Age Objective in the Age of Reformation.

[![The Power of Three icon](/images/f/f4/The_Power_of_Three.jpg)](/File:The_Power_of_Three.jpg "The Power of Three icon")

The Power of Three

Own a Crown Colony, a Self-Governing Colony and a Private Enterprise.

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World")

*   [![Colonists.png](/images/thumb/3/34/Colonists.png/28px-Colonists.png)](/Colonist "Colonist") Has a Crown Colony
*   [![Colonists.png](/images/thumb/3/34/Colonists.png/28px-Colonists.png)](/Colonist "Colonist") Has a Self-Governing Colony
*   [![Colonists.png](/images/thumb/3/34/Colonists.png/28px-Colonists.png)](/Colonist "Colonist") Has a Private Enterprise

[![Leviathan.png](/images/thumb/0/0a/Leviathan.png/28px-Leviathan.png)](/Leviathan "Leviathan")

[1.31](/1.31 "1.31")

E

[![The Princess is in this Castle icon](/images/0/01/The_Princess_is_in_this_Castle.jpg)](/File:The_Princess_is_in_this_Castle.jpg "The Princess is in this Castle icon")

The Princess is in this Castle

As a country that does not start with a female heir, have a female heir while having a Castle in your capital (more advanced fort buildings do not count).

[![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") Does not have a female [heir](/Heir "Heir")

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Latin fort01.png](/images/thumb/2/28/Latin_fort01.png/28px-Latin_fort01.png)](/Castle "Castle") Capital has Castle
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Have a female heir

Easily done as [![Flag of Castile](/images/thumb/e/ee/Castile.png/20px-Castile.png)](/Castile "Castile") [Castile](/Castile "Castile") by waiting for the Iberian wedding event while not upgrading or deleting the capital fort. Note that most Muslim countries cannot get female heirs, and those that can have a very low probability of getting one.

The Spice Must Flow

Form the nation of Malaya.

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Malaya](/images/thumb/1/11/Malaya.png/20px-Malaya.png)](/Malaya "Malaya") [Malaya](/Malaya "Malaya")

Easiest as [![Flag of Malacca](/images/thumb/f/fd/Malacca.png/20px-Malacca.png)](/Malacca "Malacca") [Malacca](/Malacca "Malacca") or [![Flag of Pasai](/images/thumb/a/a2/Pasai.png/20px-Pasai.png)](/Pasai "Pasai") [Pasai](/Pasai "Pasai").

[1.9](/1.9 "1.9")

E

[![The White Company icon](/images/3/34/The_White_Company.jpg)](/File:The_White_Company.jpg "The White Company icon")

[The White Company](/The_White_Company "The White Company")

Join a war on the other side of someone to whom you have rented condottieri.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Join a war against a nation that you hire out condottieri to. Have the country flag _white\_company_

As you don't have to accept a call to arms for a few months the easiest way to do this is when one of your allies asks you to join a war, first rent out condottieri to one of their enemies in the war then accept the call to arms.

*   [![Mare Nostrum.png](/images/thumb/f/ff/Mare_Nostrum.png/28px-Mare_Nostrum.png)](/Mare_Nostrum "Mare Nostrum")
*   [![Nation designer.png](/images/a/ab/Nation_designer.png)](/Nation_designer "Nation designer")

To the Bone

As Bone, use pillage capital at least 7 times.

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Bone](/images/thumb/2/2c/Bone.png/20px-Bone.png)](/Bone "Bone") [Bone](/Bone "Bone")
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Bone](/images/thumb/2/2c/Bone.png/20px-Bone.png)](/Bone "Bone") [Bone](/Bone "Bone")
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Has used the pillage capital [peace term](/Peace_term "Peace term") at least 7 times

[![Trade Hegemon icon](/images/3/32/Trade_Hegemon.jpg)](/File:Trade_Hegemon.jpg "Trade Hegemon icon")

[Trade Hegemon](/Trade_Hegemon "Trade Hegemon")

Starting as any European country, conquer and have cores on Aden, Hormoz and Malacca.

[![Capital.png](/images/thumb/6/6e/Capital.png/28px-Capital.png)](/Capital "Capital") Capital is in Europe

[![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own and core the provinces of Aden, Hormuz and Malacca

Expand

[![Trade Hegemon map.png](/images/thumb/a/a3/Trade_Hegemon_map.png/140px-Trade_Hegemon_map.png)](/File:Trade_Hegemon_map.png)

[](/File:Trade_Hegemon_map.png "Enlarge")

Note that nations such as [![Flag of Ottomans](/images/thumb/8/89/Ottomans.png/20px-Ottomans.png)](/Ottomans "Ottomans") [Ottomans](/Ottomans "Ottomans"), [![Flag of Kazan](/images/thumb/3/33/Kazan.png/20px-Kazan.png)](/Kazan "Kazan") [Kazan](/Kazan "Kazan") and [![Flag of Great Horde](/images/thumb/b/b7/Great_Horde.png/20px-Great_Horde.png)](/Great_Horde "Great Horde") [Great Horde](/Great_Horde "Great Horde") are considered as European countries.

[1.2](/1.2 "1.2")

E

[![Turn the Table icon](/images/3/33/Turn_the_Table.jpg)](/File:Turn_the_Table.jpg "Turn the Table icon")

Turn the Table

As a colony, break free and vassalize your former overlord without forming any other nation.

*   [![Subject colony icon.png](/images/thumb/d/de/Subject_colony_icon.png/28px-Subject_colony_icon.png)](/Colonial_nation "Colonial nation") Playing as a former colonial nation
*   [![Vassalage.png](/images/thumb/7/71/Vassalage.png/28px-Vassalage.png)](/Vassalage "Vassalage") Vassalize the former owner of the colonial nation

*   Forming another country as the colonial nation _will_ prevent this achievement even if that country is a colonial formable like [![Flag of USA](/images/thumb/3/32/United_States.png/20px-United_States.png)](/USA "USA") [USA](/USA "USA") or [![Flag of Australia](/images/thumb/4/43/Australia.png/20px-Australia.png)](/Australia "Australia") [Australia](/Australia "Australia").
*   Easily done as [![Flag of Ternate](/images/thumb/4/41/Ternate.png/20px-Ternate.png)](/Ternate "Ternate") [Ternate](/Ternate "Ternate"). Colonize Australia to the point where a colonial nation forms. Release them and select 'Play As', then vassalize your former overlord.

[![Conquest of Paradise.png](/images/thumb/3/31/Conquest_of_Paradise.png/28px-Conquest_of_Paradise.png)](/Conquest_of_Paradise "Conquest of Paradise")

[1.4](/1.4 "1.4")

E

[![Turning the Tide icon](/images/f/fd/Turning_the_Tide.jpg)](/File:Turning_the_Tide.jpg "Turning the Tide icon")

Turning the Tide

Start as a Steppe Horde in 1444 and embrace all institutions.

[![Tab domestic government.png](/images/thumb/f/ff/Tab_domestic_government.png/28px-Tab_domestic_government.png)](/Government "Government") Government type is [![Government native.png](/images/thumb/a/a8/Government_native.png/28px-Government_native.png)](/Steppe_nomads "Steppe nomads") _Steppe Nomads_

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Institutions.png](/images/thumb/4/43/Institutions.png/28px-Institutions.png)](/Institutions "Institutions") Have embraced all [institutions](/Institutions "Institutions")

Much faster in pre-1.17 patches, where the requirement is westernizing, which can be done by around 1520 instead of waiting until 1750 for the institutions to appear.

[1.3](/1.3 "1.3")

E

[![Vasa or Wettin? icon](/images/5/56/Vasa_or_Wettin%3F.jpg)](/File:Vasa_or_Wettin%3F.jpg "Vasa or Wettin? icon")

Vasa or Wettin?

Get a ruler of your dynasty on the throne of Poland or the Commonwealth while they are an elective monarchy.

[![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") Not playing as [![Flag of Poland](/images/thumb/9/99/Poland.png/20px-Poland.png)](/Poland "Poland") [Poland](/Poland "Poland")

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") [![Flag of Poland](/images/thumb/9/99/Poland.png/20px-Poland.png)](/Poland "Poland") [Poland](/Poland "Poland") or the [![Flag of Commonwealth](/images/thumb/d/df/Commonwealth.png/20px-Commonwealth.png)](/Commonwealth "Commonwealth") [Commonwealth](/Commonwealth "Commonwealth") has a ruler that is of your dynasty and was acquired via the elective monarchy.

Once Poland enables [elective monarchy](/Elective_monarchy "Elective monarchy") countries of the same religion can support candidates to their throne via diplomatic action. High diplomatic reputation and good relations with Poland increase the likelihood gaining support.

[![Res Publica.png](/images/thumb/b/b5/Res_Publica.png/28px-Res_Publica.png)](/Res_Publica "Res Publica")

[1.7](/1.7 "1.7")

E

[![Viva la Revolución! icon](/images/5/58/Viva_la_Revoluci%C3%B3n%21.jpg)](/File:Viva_la_Revoluci%C3%B3n!.jpg "Viva la Revolución! icon")

Viva la Revolución!

Have rebels you support in another country enforce their demands.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Have [supported rebels](/Support_rebels "Support rebels") in another country that enforced their demands.

Possible to do as [![Flag of Tondo](/images/thumb/2/21/Tondo.png/20px-Tondo.png)](/Tondo "Tondo") [Tondo](/Tondo "Tondo"), as neighbouring [![Flag of Pangasinan](/images/thumb/0/07/Pangasinan.png/20px-Pangasinan.png)](/Pangasinan "Pangasinan") [Pangasinan](/Pangasinan "Pangasinan") starts with a single province of a heathen religion. Immediately rival them and declare an offensive war using the Humiliate Rival CB. Sit on their capital to increase their war exhaustion until you can support the Animist rebels. When an uprising is about to take place, white peace. The rebels will enforce their demands as soon as they take the province.

[1.1](/Patch_1.1.X "Patch 1.1.X")

E

[![Voting Streak icon](/images/c/c8/Voting_Streak.jpg)](/File:Voting_Streak.jpg "Voting Streak icon")

[Voting Streak](/Voting_Streak "Voting Streak")

Successfully pass 11 issues in a row in Parliament.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Pass 11 [parliament](/Parliament "Parliament") issues in a row

England is the only nation with a parliament in 1444.

[![Where Am I? icon](/images/b/b8/Where_Am_I%3F.png)](/File:Where_Am_I%3F.png "Where Am I? icon")

Where Am I?

As a New World native with Random New World active, explore the entire New World.

*   [![Tab domestic government.png](/images/thumb/f/ff/Tab_domestic_government.png/28px-Tab_domestic_government.png)](/Government "Government") Government type is [![Government native.png](/images/thumb/a/a8/Government_native.png/28px-Government_native.png)](/Steppe_nomads "Steppe nomads") _Native_
*   [![Capital.png](/images/thumb/6/6e/Capital.png/28px-Capital.png)](/Capital "Capital") Capital is in the New World
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World")
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") No more than 1 custom nation exists in the world
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") Used no more than 201 nation designer points if playing as a custom nation

[![Explorer](/images/thumb/c/ca/Explorer.png/28px-Explorer.png)](/Military_leaders "Explorer") Has discovered all provinces in the New World.

Eligible countries show “Tribe” as the government in the nation selection screen or are custom nations with one of the government reforms in the “Native” category

Sometimes a random world is generated where all of the land is already discovered by most native nations, one only needs to unpause in order to get the achievement

*   [![Conquest of Paradise.png](/images/thumb/3/31/Conquest_of_Paradise.png/28px-Conquest_of_Paradise.png)](/Conquest_of_Paradise "Conquest of Paradise")
*   [![Nation designer.png](/images/a/ab/Nation_designer.png)](/Nation_designer "Nation designer")

[1.28](/1.28 "1.28")

E

[![Winged Hussars icon](/images/0/0a/Winged_Hussars.jpg)](/File:Winged_Hussars.jpg "Winged Hussars icon")

Winged Hussars

Have Winged Hussars as your active unit with more than +50% cavalry combat ability.

*   [![Cavalry.png](/images/thumb/1/15/Cavalry.png/28px-Cavalry.png)](/Cavalry "Cavalry") Have Winged Hussars as your primary cavalry unit
*   [![Cavalry combat ability.png](/images/thumb/d/dc/Cavalry_combat_ability.png/28px-Cavalry_combat_ability.png)](/Cavalry_combat_ability "Cavalry combat ability") Have a [cavalry combat ability](/Cavalry_combat_ability "Cavalry combat ability") of at least 50%

*   Winged Hussars cavalry unit is part of the [![Eastern technology group](/images/thumb/6/6d/Eastern.png/28px-Eastern.png)](/Technology_group "Eastern technology group") Eastern technology group (military tech level 22). For details on [![Cavalry combat ability.png](/images/thumb/d/dc/Cavalry_combat_ability.png/28px-Cavalry_combat_ability.png)](/Cavalry_combat_ability "Cavalry combat ability") cavalry combat ability see the article on [Land units](/Land_units#Combat_ability_2 "Land units").
*   Poland is the easiest nation to play for this achievement due to the cavalry combat ability in their national ideas. Taking Aristocratic and Quality ideas will give Poland enough combat ability to satisfy this achievement.

[1.2](/1.2 "1.2")

E

[![World Discoverer icon](/images/d/d6/World_Discoverer.jpg)](/File:World_Discoverer.jpg "World Discoverer icon")

World Discoverer

Discover all non-wasteland land provinces.

[![Explorer](/images/thumb/c/ca/Explorer.png/28px-Explorer.png)](/Military_leaders "Explorer") Discover all [terra incognita](/Terra_incognita "Terra incognita").

You do not have to discover all Terra Incognita yourself, as TI can be automatically uncovered via spread of discovery. The condition is simply that no TI exists in the world for you, not including sea zones. Wastelands are not needed. Easiest in Europe. With Mare Nostrum DLC, a good way to find the last few is to check the [Request to share maps](/Diplomacy#Request_to_share_maps "Diplomacy") diplomatic action on colonizers or anybody else.

[1.1](/Patch_1.1.X "Patch 1.1.X")

[![You Get A New Home, And You Get A New Home icon](/images/3/3e/You_Get_a_New_Home%2C_and_You_Get_a_New_Home.png)](/File:You_Get_a_New_Home,_and_You_Get_a_New_Home.png "You Get A New Home, And You Get A New Home icon")

You Get A New Home, And You Get A New Home

Expel 5 different minorities to your colonies.

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") No more than 1 custom nation exists in the world
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") Used no more than 201 nation designer points if playing as a custom nation

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Has expelled 5 different minorities to colonial provinces.

*   [![Golden Century.png](/images/thumb/b/bb/Golden_Century.png/28px-Golden_Century.png)](/Golden_Century "Golden Century")
*   [![Nation designer.png](/images/a/ab/Nation_designer.png)](/Nation_designer "Nation designer")

[1.28](/1.28 "1.28")

E

[![A Fine Goosestep icon](/images/3/35/A_Fine_Goosestep.jpg)](/File:A_Fine_Goosestep.jpg "A Fine Goosestep icon")

A Fine Goosestep

Form Prussia and have at least 125% Discipline.

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Prussia](/images/thumb/2/28/Prussia.png/20px-Prussia.png)](/Prussia "Prussia") [Prussia](/Prussia "Prussia")
*   [![Discipline.png](/images/thumb/5/59/Discipline.png/28px-Discipline.png)](/Discipline "Discipline") Have 125% discipline

The following actions can increase Prussian discipline:

Expand

*   Increasing [![Militarization of state.png](/images/thumb/d/de/Militarization_of_state.png/28px-Militarization_of_state.png)](/Militarization "Militarization") Militarization of Country (maximum **+10%**)
*   Increasing [![Absolutism.png](/images/thumb/c/c2/Absolutism.png/28px-Absolutism.png)](/Absolutism "Absolutism") Absolutism (maximum **+5%**)
*   Completing [![Quality idea group.png](/images/thumb/7/72/Quality_idea_group.png/28px-Quality_idea_group.png)](/Quality_ideas "Quality ideas") Quality Ideas (**+5%**)
*   Unlocking “Esprit de Corps” in [![Offensive idea group.png](/images/thumb/4/40/Offensive_idea_group.png/28px-Offensive_idea_group.png)](/Offensive_ideas "Offensive ideas") Offensive ideas (**+5%**)
*   Economic-Quality policy “Weapon Quality Standards” (**+5%**)
*   Unlocking the [![Idea bonus.png](/images/thumb/d/db/Idea_bonus.png/28px-Idea_bonus.png)](/Idea "Idea") Prussian ambition (**+5%**)
*   Having a Commandant [![Advisor.png](/images/thumb/6/6a/Advisor.png/28px-Advisor.png)](/Advisor "Advisor") advisor (**+5%**)
*   Having a ruler with the [![Discipline.png](/images/thumb/5/59/Discipline.png/28px-Discipline.png)](/Discipline "Discipline") “Strict” personality (**+5%**)
*   Converting to [![Protestantism](/images/thumb/0/0d/Protestant.png/28px-Protestant.png)](/Protestant "Protestant") Protestantism and obtaining the [![Church power.png](/images/thumb/f/fd/Church_power.png/28px-Church_power.png)](/Church_power "Church power") Aspect of Faith “Holy Sacraments” (**+2.5%**)

[1.12](/1.12 "1.12")

M

[![A tale of two Families icon](/images/f/fd/A_tale_of_two_Families.jpg)](/File:A_tale_of_two_Families.jpg "A tale of two Families icon")

A tale of two Families

Starting as Vijayanagar or Bahmanis conquer the other’s capital and have them not exist.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as _either_:

*    [![Flag of Bahmanis](/images/thumb/d/de/Bahmanis.png/20px-Bahmanis.png)](/Bahmanis "Bahmanis") [Bahmanis](/Bahmanis "Bahmanis")
*    [![Flag of Vijayanagar](/images/thumb/3/31/Vijayanagar.png/20px-Vijayanagar.png)](/Vijayanagar "Vijayanagar") [Vijayanagar](/Vijayanagar "Vijayanagar")

*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own and core the provinces Bidar (1948) and Vijayanagar (541)
*   Is _either_:
    *    [![Flag of Bahmanis](/images/thumb/d/de/Bahmanis.png/20px-Bahmanis.png)](/Bahmanis "Bahmanis") [Bahmanis](/Bahmanis "Bahmanis") and [![Flag of Vijayanagar](/images/thumb/3/31/Vijayanagar.png/20px-Vijayanagar.png)](/Vijayanagar "Vijayanagar") [Vijayanagar](/Vijayanagar "Vijayanagar") doesn't exist
    *    [![Flag of Vijayanagar](/images/thumb/3/31/Vijayanagar.png/20px-Vijayanagar.png)](/Vijayanagar "Vijayanagar") [Vijayanagar](/Vijayanagar "Vijayanagar") and [![Flag of Bahmanis](/images/thumb/d/de/Bahmanis.png/20px-Bahmanis.png)](/Bahmanis "Bahmanis") [Bahmanis](/Bahmanis "Bahmanis") doesn't exist

Forming [![Flag of Bharat](/images/thumb/b/b0/Bharat.png/20px-Bharat.png)](/Bharat "Bharat") [Bharat](/Bharat "Bharat") or [![Flag of Hindustan](/images/thumb/3/3e/Hindustan.png/20px-Hindustan.png)](/Hindustan "Hindustan") [Hindustan](/Hindustan "Hindustan") _will_ prevent the achievement.

[1.18](/1.18 "1.18")

M

[![AEIOU icon](/images/7/70/AEIOU.png)](/File:AEIOU.png "AEIOU icon")

AEIOU

Complete the Austrian mission tree.

[![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World")

[![Mission.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Mission.png/24px-Mission.png)](/Missions "Missions") Complete all [Austrian missions](/Austrian_missions "Austrian missions")

You can trigger the religious peace by enacting "Proclaim Erbkaisertum" reform, since it will not block the mission [A Holy Empire](/Austrian_missions#A_Holy_Empire "Austrian missions"). Forming another country which gives new missions (e.g. [![Flag of Germany](/images/thumb/9/9b/Germany.png/20px-Germany.png)](/Germany "Germany") [Germany](/Germany "Germany") or unifying the [![Flag of Holy Roman Empire](/images/thumb/e/ee/Holy_Roman_Empire.png/20px-Holy_Roman_Empire.png)](/Holy_Roman_Empire "Holy Roman Empire") [Holy Roman Empire](/Holy_Roman_Empire "Holy Roman Empire")) will prevent you from getting the achievement.

[![Emperor](/images/thumb/c/c5/Emperor.png/28px-Emperor.png)](/Emperor_(DLC) "Emperor")

[1.30](/1.30 "1.30")

[![All Your Trade Are Belong to Us icon](/images/d/d0/All_Your_Trade_Are_Belong_to_Us.jpg)](/File:All_Your_Trade_Are_Belong_to_Us.jpg "All Your Trade Are Belong to Us icon")

All Your Trade Are Belong to Us

Have the highest trade power in Genoa, Venice and English Channel while having an income of at least 300 ducats per month.

*   [![Trade power.png](/images/thumb/1/10/Trade_power.png/28px-Trade_power.png)](/Trade_power "Trade power") Highest Trade power in Genoa, Venice, and English Channel
*   [![Income.png](/images/a/aa/Income.png)](/Income "Income") Have 300 income

Easily done as [![Flag of England](/images/thumb/2/21/England.png/20px-England.png)](/England "England") [England](/England "England") or [![Flag of Netherlands](/images/thumb/3/32/Netherlands.png/20px-Netherlands.png)](/Netherlands "Netherlands") [Netherlands](/Netherlands "Netherlands") by controlling the English Channel via provincial trade power and sending light ships to the Venice and Genoa trade nodes.

M

[![Arabian Coffee icon](/images/e/e2/Arabian_Coffee.jpg)](/File:Arabian_Coffee.jpg "Arabian Coffee icon")

Arabian Coffee

Form Arabia and be the nation producing the most coffee in the world.

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Arabia](/images/thumb/e/ed/Arabia.png/20px-Arabia.png)](/Arabia "Arabia") [Arabia](/Arabia "Arabia")
*   [![Coffee.png](/images/thumb/e/e9/Coffee.png/28px-Coffee.png)](/Coffee "Coffee") Be production leader of coffee

Coffee is common in the area around [![Flag of Ethiopia](/images/thumb/0/06/Ethiopia.png/20px-Ethiopia.png)](/Ethiopia "Ethiopia") [Ethiopia](/Ethiopia "Ethiopia") and [![Flag of Mali](/images/thumb/f/f0/Mali.png/20px-Mali.png)](/Mali "Mali") [Mali](/Mali "Mali"). If you are not the leading producer after conquering these areas, build manufactories or conquer Mesoamerica. Forming [![Flag of Arabia](/images/thumb/e/ed/Arabia.png/20px-Arabia.png)](/Arabia "Arabia") [Arabia](/Arabia "Arabia") is easiest as The [![Flag of Mamluks](/images/thumb/c/ca/The_Mamluks.png/20px-The_Mamluks.png)](/Mamluks "Mamluks") [Mamluks](/Mamluks "Mamluks").

[1.10](/1.10 "1.10")

M

[![Atwix Legacy icon](/images/9/9d/Atwix_Legacy.png)](/File:Atwix_Legacy.png "Atwix Legacy icon")

Atwix Legacy

Have 10 personal unions at the same time.

[![Personal union.png](/images/thumb/3/39/Personal_union.png/28px-Personal_union.png)](/Personal_union "Personal union") Have 10 or more personal unions

Named as a tribute to the forum user Atwix who wrote the [guide to royal marriages, personal unions and claim throne.](https://forum.paradoxplaza.com/forum/index.php?threads/788829 "forum:788829") and who passed away during the development of the 1.32 patch.

A good way is to choose a country with many PUs in its mission tree such as Hungary, Bohemia or Austria. Follow Atwix guide and make use of the new favor feature to spread your dynasty. Ensure that your PU subjects are fairly large to avoid inheriting their throne.

[1.22](/1.22 "1.22")

M

[![Carthago Delenda Est icon](/images/b/bb/Carthago_Delenda_Est.png)](/File:Carthago_Delenda_Est.png "Carthago Delenda Est icon")

Carthago Delenda Est

As an Italian culture nation, make sure entire Tunis Area is at 100 devastation.

[![Culture icon.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Culture_icon.png/28px-Culture_icon.png)](/Culture "Culture") Culture group is _Latin_

*   [![Culture icon.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Culture_icon.png/28px-Culture_icon.png)](/Culture "Culture") Culture group is _Latin_
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") All provinces in the Tunisia area have [![Devastation.png](/images/thumb/8/8c/Devastation.png/28px-Devastation.png)](/Devastation "Devastation") 100 devastation

Culture must be Latin at game start _and_ when Tunisia is devastated. [![Flag of Naples](/images/thumb/b/b8/Naples.png/20px-Naples.png)](/Naples "Naples") [Naples](/Naples "Naples") is by far the strongest and closest Latin nation in 1444. Regardless of the nation selected, declare a war in which land may be taken from Tunis. Take the Tunisia area in the war. Then go bankrupt repeatedly until you have 100 devastation (going bankrupt adds 10 devastation to all provinces). The first bankruptcy can be declared manually, but this button can't be used while being bankrupt. So the subsequent bankruptcies must be achieved by taking the maximum amount of loans and spending all the money while running a deficit. A high deficit can be achieved by using the loans to hire and upgrade advisors. This is far faster than trying to raise devastation using other methods such as occupying the land while at war and using scorch earth.

[1.20](/1.20 "1.20")

M

[![Cherrypicking icon](/images/1/10/Cherrypicking.png)](/File:Cherrypicking.png "Cherrypicking icon")

Cherrypicking

Conscript a 3 star general from a Daimyo Subject.

[![Culture icon.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Culture_icon.png/28px-Culture_icon.png)](/Culture "Culture") Culture group is _Japanese_

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Conscript a 3-star general from a Daimyo subject

The most reliable way is to vassalize a Jurchen tribe and make them fulfill their mission [Unite the Jurchen Tribes](/Manchurian_missions#Unite_the_Jurchen_Tribes "Manchurian missions") which gives a 3-star general as a reward.

This can be done in under a month by creating a custom nation shogun, releasing a jurchen subject and feeding them the required provinces.

*   [![Mandate of Heaven.png](/images/thumb/7/7c/Mandate_of_Heaven.png/28px-Mandate_of_Heaven.png)](/Mandate_of_Heaven "Mandate of Heaven")
*   [![Nation designer.png](/images/a/ab/Nation_designer.png)](/Nation_designer "Nation designer")

Fugger Banking

As Augsburg, subsidize 3 Great Powers 20% of their income while having less than 20 provinces.

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Augsburg](/images/thumb/2/25/Augsburg.png/20px-Augsburg.png)](/Augsburg "Augsburg") [Augsburg](/Augsburg "Augsburg")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Augsburg](/images/thumb/2/25/Augsburg.png/20px-Augsburg.png)](/Augsburg "Augsburg") [Augsburg](/Augsburg "Augsburg")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") less than 20 provinces
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") [Subsidize](/Subsidies "Subsidies") 3 [![Great power.png](/images/thumb/f/fc/Great_power.png/24px-Great_power.png)](/Great_power "Great power") Great Powers at least 20% of their income.

The subsidies also count as income, so the subsidies have to be 25% of the income before subsidies. The total income can be seen in the Income Comparison page in the ledger. The Country page doesn't show all income sources. You can subsidize up to 50% of your income to each country, which means you need to reach at least half the income of the 3 poorest great powers.

A good way to get it quickly is to get a hold of the Inntal or Eger goldmine and to develop it.

*   [![Rights of Man.png](/images/thumb/5/50/Rights_of_Man.png/28px-Rights_of_Man.png)](/Rights_of_Man "Rights of Man") _or_ [![Emperor](/images/thumb/c/c5/Emperor.png/28px-Emperor.png)](/Emperor_(DLC) "Emperor")

[1.26](/1.26 "1.26")

M

[![Georgia on my Mind icon](/images/6/6b/Georgia_on_my_Mind.png)](/File:Georgia_on_my_Mind.png "Georgia on my Mind icon")

Georgia on my Mind

Fully own all three Georgias.

[![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World").

[![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own or have a non-tributary subject own all provinces in the areas: [Kartli-Kakheti](/Kartli-Kakheti "Kartli-Kakheti"), [Samtskhe](/European_regions#Samtskhe "European regions") and [Imereti](/European_regions#Imereti "European regions").

*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own or have a non-tributary subject own all provinces in the areas: [Georgia](/North_American_regions#Georgia "North American regions") and [Upper Georgia](/Upper_Georgia "Upper Georgia")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own or have a non-tributary subject own the province of South Georgia (2025)

Expand

[![Georgia on my Mind map.png](/images/thumb/2/2b/Georgia_on_my_Mind_map.png/140px-Georgia_on_my_Mind_map.png)](/File:Georgia_on_my_Mind_map.png)

[](/File:Georgia_on_my_Mind_map.png "Enlarge")

Easiest to do as a coloniser such as [![Flag of France](/images/thumb/d/de/France.png/20px-France.png)](/France "France") [France](/France "France"), [![Flag of Spain](/images/thumb/5/58/Spain.png/20px-Spain.png)](/Spain "Spain") [Spain](/Spain "Spain") or [![Flag of Great Britain](/images/thumb/2/2b/Great_Britain.png/20px-Great_Britain.png)](/Great_Britain "Great Britain") [Great Britain](/Great_Britain "Great Britain") since you can easily acquire the required provinces in North America and the South Atlantic. Remaining provinces can be obtained by declaring no-CB wars on nations in Caucasia to vassalize them early before they're conquered by [![Flag of Russia](/images/thumb/e/ee/Russia.png/20px-Russia.png)](/Russia "Russia") [Russia](/Russia "Russia") or the [![Flag of Ottomans](/images/thumb/8/89/Ottomans.png/20px-Ottomans.png)](/Ottomans "Ottomans") [Ottomans](/Ottomans "Ottomans").

Gold Rush

[1.20](/1.20 "1.20")

M

[![Golden Horn icon](/images/2/25/Golden_Horn.jpg)](/File:Golden_Horn.jpg "Golden Horn icon")

Golden Horn

As a Somali nation, fully own the Horn of Africa region and have a monthly gold income of at least 10 ducats.

[![Culture icon.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Culture_icon.png/28px-Culture_icon.png)](/Culture "Culture") Culture is _Somali_

*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") All provinces of the [Horn of Africa](/African_regions#Horn_of_Africa "African regions") region are owned by the player's country _or_ its non-tributary [subjects](/Subjects "Subjects").
*   [![Income.png](/images/a/aa/Income.png)](/Income "Income") Have 10 income from [![Gold](/images/thumb/1/10/Gold.png/28px-Gold.png)](/Trade_goods#Gold "Gold") gold

Expand

[![Golden Horn map.png](/images/thumb/1/17/Golden_Horn_map.png/140px-Golden_Horn_map.png)](/File:Golden_Horn_map.png)

[](/File:Golden_Horn_map.png "Enlarge")

*   Note that the provinces of Fazughli, Afder and Ogaden have to be colonized for the achievement, but the colonies do not need to be complete. You can just send your colonist to all 3 provinces at once as soon as you have the other land.
*   Start as [![Flag of Adal](/images/thumb/8/81/Adal.png/20px-Adal.png)](/Adal "Adal") [Adal](/Adal "Adal") or [![Flag of Ajuuraan](/images/thumb/5/52/Ajuuraan.png/20px-Ajuuraan.png)](/Ajuuraan "Ajuuraan") [Ajuuraan](/Ajuuraan "Ajuuraan"), and set the National Focus to administrative, then swiftly conquer all adjacent nations in the region that are smaller than you. [Aggressive Expansion](/Aggressive_Expansion "Aggressive Expansion") will not be an issue due to the nations belonging to different religious groups. To attain the gold income, improve production development in the gold provinces Kaffa (2757) and Damot (2762).
*   Convert the religion in the gold provinces to your state religion, which will increase your gold income, requiring less development.

[1.16](/1.16 "1.16")

M

[![Golden Wind icon](/images/8/88/Golden_Wind.png)](/File:Golden_Wind.png "Golden Wind icon")

Golden Wind

As Air, make 50 ducats profit per month and have 50% of your income made through gold provinces.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Air](/images/thumb/5/5f/Air.png/20px-Air.png)](/Air "Air") [Air](/Air "Air")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Air](/images/thumb/5/5f/Air.png/20px-Air.png)](/Air "Air") [Air](/Air "Air")
*   [![Income.png](/images/a/aa/Income.png)](/Income "Income") monthly balance is at least **50**
*   [![Gold](/images/thumb/1/10/Gold.png/28px-Gold.png)](/Trade_goods#Gold "Gold") 50% of the monthly income is from gold

This achievement is only visible if the [![Origins.png](/images/thumb/8/8e/Origins.png/28px-Origins.png)](/Origins "Origins") Origins DLC is active, but no DLC is needed to complete it.

As [![Flag of Air](/images/thumb/5/5f/Air.png/20px-Air.png)](/Air "Air") [Air](/Air "Air") consider royal marrying [![Flag of Songhai](/images/thumb/2/24/Songhai.png/20px-Songhai.png)](/Songhai "Songhai") [Songhai](/Songhai "Songhai") and [![Flag of Mali](/images/thumb/f/f0/Mali.png/20px-Mali.png)](/Mali "Mali") [Mali](/Mali "Mali") and improving relations after to get an alliance. Both should start neutral most of the time and are strong allies. After, look for choice targets and build over force limit by hiring a free company. Air starts with a level 2 fort on their capital so rushing smaller enemy capital forts is a viable strategy, no need to take unnecessary battles.

You need 50 positive balance, not income. Consider disbanding armies, firing advisors and deleting forts when your income is over 60 ducats, with at least 50% gold income. Almost all expenses can be reduced to near 0 except for state maintenance. To get enough gold income controlling and developing the three gold mines in West Africa should be enough. In 1444 two are owned by [![Flag of Mali](/images/thumb/f/f0/Mali.png/20px-Mali.png)](/Mali "Mali") [Mali](/Mali "Mali") and one by [![Flag of Kong](/images/thumb/2/26/Kong.png/20px-Kong.png)](/Kong "Kong") [Kong](/Kong "Kong").

[1.32](/1.32 "1.32")

M

[![Great Moravia icon](/images/0/0f/Great_Moravia.png)](/File:Great_Moravia.png "Great Moravia icon")

Great Moravia

Restore the Great Moravian borders as Nitra or Moravia.

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Nitra](/images/thumb/4/47/Nitra.png/20px-Nitra.png)](/Nitra "Nitra") [Nitra](/Nitra "Nitra") or [![Flag of Moravia](/images/thumb/9/9b/Moravia.png/20px-Moravia.png)](/Moravia "Moravia") [Moravia](/Moravia "Moravia")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own and core the following provinces:

Expand

[![Great Moravia map.png](/images/thumb/b/ba/Great_Moravia_map.png/140px-Great_Moravia_map.png)](/File:Great_Moravia_map.png)

[](/File:Great_Moravia_map.png "Enlarge")

Nitra's cores don't expire except by culture conversion. Requires all the territory of [![Flag of Bohemia](/images/thumb/4/41/Bohemia.png/20px-Bohemia.png)](/Bohemia "Bohemia") [Bohemia](/Bohemia "Bohemia"), [![Flag of Glogow](/images/thumb/5/59/Glogow.png/20px-Glogow.png)](/Glogow "Glogow") [Glogow](/Glogow "Glogow") and [![Flag of Opole](/images/thumb/7/78/Opole.png/20px-Opole.png)](/Opole "Opole") [Opole](/Opole "Opole"), Wien (134), Manhartsberg (1770), Traungau (4761) and Wienerwald (4762) from [![Flag of Austria](/images/thumb/7/7f/Austria.png/20px-Austria.png)](/Austria "Austria") [Austria](/Austria "Austria"), Kraków (262) and Nowy Sącz (2960) from [![Flag of Poland](/images/thumb/9/99/Poland.png/20px-Poland.png)](/Poland "Poland") [Poland](/Poland "Poland"), and the Slovakia and Transdanubia areas from [![Flag of Hungary](/images/thumb/6/6a/Hungary.png/20px-Hungary.png)](/Hungary "Hungary") [Hungary](/Hungary "Hungary").

If choosing to play as [![Flag of Moravia](/images/thumb/9/9b/Moravia.png/20px-Moravia.png)](/Moravia "Moravia") [Moravia](/Moravia "Moravia"), you will incur much more agresssive expansion and find it harder to make alliances due to being a heretic nation (Hussite) if you release them on day 1. There are advantages to starting in the empire though, so you may find it useful to convert some of Moravia's cores to Catholic before switching to them.

M

[![Hanukkah Mutapa icon](/images/0/06/Hanukkah_Mutapa.png)](/File:Hanukkah_Mutapa.png "Hanukkah Mutapa icon")

Hanukkah Mutapa

Starting as Mutapa, convert to Judaism and celebrate a festival.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Mutapa](/images/thumb/2/23/Mutapa.png/20px-Mutapa.png)](/Mutapa "Mutapa") [Mutapa](/Mutapa "Mutapa")

*   [![Jewish.png](/images/thumb/c/cd/Jewish.png/28px-Jewish.png)](/Jewish "Jewish") Religion is Jewish
*   Has used the Jewish religion action _“Celebrate Festival”_

This achievement is misspelled as _“Hannukah Mutapa”_ in the steam version of the game.

At the start of the game the 2 only Jewish provinces are in [![Flag of Ethiopia](/images/thumb/0/06/Ethiopia.png/20px-Ethiopia.png)](/Ethiopia "Ethiopia") [Ethiopia](/Ethiopia "Ethiopia"), due to [![Flag of Ethiopia](/images/thumb/0/06/Ethiopia.png/20px-Ethiopia.png)](/Ethiopia "Ethiopia") [Ethiopia](/Ethiopia "Ethiopia")'s missions the AI will always pick the option to temporarily accept Jewish religion, giving you 25 years to take them.

 [![Flag of Mutapa](/images/thumb/2/23/Mutapa.png/20px-Mutapa.png)](/Mutapa "Mutapa") [Mutapa](/Mutapa "Mutapa")'s gold mines should allow you to go over force limit and quickly declare a war of conquest against [![Flag of Kilwa](/images/thumb/c/cb/Kilwa.png/20px-Kilwa.png)](/Kilwa "Kilwa") [Kilwa](/Kilwa "Kilwa") despite the technology disadvantage. Focus on military mana to not fall further behind [![Flag of Ethiopia](/images/thumb/0/06/Ethiopia.png/20px-Ethiopia.png)](/Ethiopia "Ethiopia") [Ethiopia](/Ethiopia "Ethiopia").

[![Origins.png](/images/thumb/8/8e/Origins.png/28px-Origins.png)](/Origins "Origins")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") is [![Flag of Hesse](/images/thumb/2/2a/Hesse.png/20px-Hesse.png)](/Hesse "Hesse") [Hesse](/Hesse "Hesse")
*   [![Mercenary manpower.png](/images/thumb/b/b2/Mercenary_manpower.png/28px-Mercenary_manpower.png)](/Available_mercenaries "Available mercenaries") Have 50 regiments of [mercenaries](/Mercenaries "Mercenaries")

Hoarder

As a Fetishist nation, have 13 available Cults.

With the [Cradle of Civilization](/Cradle_of_Civilization "Cradle of Civilization") DLC activated, [Kilwa](/Kilwa "Kilwa") may convert all of Madagascar to Islam once they gain more than 50% trade power in Zanzibar, making the achievement impossible if the three Malagasy cults have not been gained already.

Home and Away

*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own Glamorgan (241), Pale (373), Lothian (248), Roma (118), Paris (183) and London (236)

*   It is not needed to core the required provinces.
*   The welsh names of the provinces in eu4 are Morgannwg(241), Dulyn(373), Lleuddiniawn(248), Rhufain(118), Paris(183) and Llundain(236)

[1.25](/1.25 "1.25")

M

[![Ideas Guy icon](/images/3/3b/Ideas_Guy.jpg)](/File:Ideas_Guy.jpg "Ideas Guy icon")

Ideas Guy

Starting as a custom nation with the full 800 points but no more than 3 total development, have a monthly income of at least 500 ducats.

*   [![Nation designer.png](/images/a/ab/Nation_designer.png)](/Nation_designer "Nation designer") Playing as a custom nation
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Only 1 custom nation exists in the world
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") Used no more than 801 nation designer points
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") No more than [![Development.png](/images/thumb/a/a4/Development.png/28px-Development.png)](/Development "Development") 3 total development

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Income.png](/images/a/aa/Income.png)](/Income "Income") Has at least 500 ducats in income

Despite the description, can be done with fewer than 800 points. Spoils of war do not count towards the income; you must make 500 ducats, not including Spoils.  
It became very easy after Third Rome, due to Siberian frontier ability: Start a nation in Americas with Siberian Frontier as a tradition, it will allow you to expand in uncolonized regions rapidly.

Can also be paired with [![For Odin!.jpg](/images/thumb/4/4a/For_Odin%21.jpg/28px-For_Odin%21.jpg)](/File:For_Odin!.jpg) [For Odin!](#For_Odin.21) and [![From Humble Origins.jpg](/images/thumb/5/59/From_Humble_Origins.jpg/28px-From_Humble_Origins.jpg)](/File:From_Humble_Origins.jpg) [From Humble Origins](#From_Humble_Origins)

[![El Dorado.png](/images/thumb/1/16/El_Dorado.png/28px-El_Dorado.png)](/El_Dorado "El Dorado")

*   [![Nation designer.png](/images/a/ab/Nation_designer.png)](/Nation_designer "Nation designer")

[1.14](/1.14 "1.14")

[![Italian Ambition icon](/images/d/d2/Italian_Ambition.jpg)](/File:Italian_Ambition.jpg "Italian Ambition icon")

[Italian Ambition](/Italian_Ambition "Italian Ambition")

Form Italy.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Italy](/images/thumb/2/2a/Italy.png/20px-Italy.png)](/Italy "Italy") [Italy](/Italy "Italy")

Become [Italy](/Italy "Italy"). The primary culture of the country you start with should be in the Latin culture group (the achievement won't be visible in game unless you are Latin) but you can also get the achievement via culture shift. The [Papal State](/Papal_State "Papal State") and The [Holy Roman Empire](/Holy_Roman_Empire "Holy Roman Empire") can't form Italy.

[1.1](/Patch_1.1.X "Patch 1.1.X")
