[![Je maintiendrai icon](/images/c/c5/Je_maintiendrai.jpg)](/File:Je_maintiendrai.jpg "Je maintiendrai icon")

Je maintiendrai

Form the Netherlands as a minor nation starting with Dutch culture.

[![Culture icon.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Culture_icon.png/28px-Culture_icon.png)](/Culture "Culture") Culture is _Dutch_

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is the [![Flag of Netherlands](/images/thumb/3/32/Netherlands.png/20px-Netherlands.png)](/Netherlands "Netherlands") [Netherlands](/Netherlands "Netherlands")

Possible starts are [![Flag of Holland](/images/thumb/6/60/Holland.png/20px-Holland.png)](/Holland "Holland") [Holland](/Holland "Holland"), [![Flag of Utrecht](/images/thumb/d/d4/Utrecht.png/20px-Utrecht.png)](/Utrecht "Utrecht") [Utrecht](/Utrecht "Utrecht"), [![Flag of Gelre](/images/thumb/4/41/Gelre.png/20px-Gelre.png)](/Gelre "Gelre") [Gelre](/Gelre "Gelre"). Easily done as Holland by seeking independence support from [![Flag of Burgundy](/images/thumb/b/b0/Burgundy.png/20px-Burgundy.png)](/Burgundy "Burgundy") [Burgundy](/Burgundy "Burgundy")'s enemies and then carefully eating the other Dutch minors.

One could also try grabbing the Burgundian inheritance as Gelre, which grants most of the land required for free. Remember that you must send the royal marriage offer, not them.

Kingdom of God

[1.30](/1.30 "1.30")

M

[![Kirishitan Japan icon](/images/c/c9/Kirishitan_Japan.jpg)](/File:Kirishitan_Japan.jpg "Kirishitan Japan icon")

Kirishitan Japan

Start as a Japanese Daimyo, convert yourself and all of Japan to Christianity.

[![Tab domestic government.png](/images/thumb/f/ff/Tab_domestic_government.png/28px-Tab_domestic_government.png)](/Government "Government") Government type is [![Government monarchy.png](/images/thumb/4/4d/Government_monarchy.png/28px-Government_monarchy.png)](/Monarchy "Monarchy") _Daimyo_

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Japan](/images/thumb/f/fc/Japan.png/20px-Japan.png)](/Japan "Japan") [Japan](/Japan "Japan")
*   [![Reform desire.png](/images/thumb/e/e2/Reform_desire.png/28px-Reform_desire.png)](/Reform_desire "Reform desire") In Christian religious group
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") All provinces in [Japanese](/Asian_regions#Japan "Asian regions") region are in Christian religious group.

*   You must start as a Daimyo subject of [![Flag of Ashikaga](/images/thumb/a/a1/Ashikaga.png/20px-Ashikaga.png)](/Ashikaga "Ashikaga") [Ashikaga](/Ashikaga "Ashikaga"). The Japan region includes Okinawa, Hokkaido, and the Kuril Islands. Uncolonized provinces are required as well. Best done with [![Flag of Otomo](/images/thumb/a/ad/Otomo.png/20px-Otomo.png)](/Otomo "Otomo") [Otomo](/Otomo "Otomo"), who receive an extra missionary in addition to increased papal influence.
*   [![Mandate of Heaven.png](/images/thumb/7/7c/Mandate_of_Heaven.png/28px-Mandate_of_Heaven.png)](/Mandate_of_Heaven "Mandate of Heaven") Wait for the Spread of Christianity incident, which usually pops up around 1600 or so. Always take the most "Open" or pro-Christian options in events. A few years after the incident ends, an event to convert to Catholic will pop up.
*   If Mandate of Heaven is disabled: don't take the decision to enforce Sakoku, wait for events to convert your provinces and spawn Catholic rebels, and let them convert at least half your provinces. Harder if you have too many disconnected provinces outside the Japan region.

*   [![Tobacco.png](/images/thumb/1/19/Tobacco.png/28px-Tobacco.png)](/Tobacco "Tobacco") The leading producer of Tobacco is _either_ this country or a subject of this country

*   Not possible with Random New World.
*   Making the leading tobacco producer a tributary would count.

M

[![My armies are invincible! icon](/images/3/3d/My_armies_are_invincible%21.jpg)](/File:My_armies_are_invincible!.jpg "My armies are invincible! icon")

My armies are invincible!

Gain at least 7.0 land morale.

[![Morale of armies.png](/images/thumb/f/fa/Morale_of_armies.png/28px-Morale_of_armies.png)](/Morale_of_armies "Morale of armies") Have **7** Morale of armies

Research military techs, invest in ideas that improve morale, maintain high [prestige](/Prestige "Prestige") and [army tradition](/Army_tradition "Army tradition"). Finally hire an [Army Reformer](/Army_Reformer "Army Reformer"). Easiest as [France](/France "France"), with their national idea "Élan!" that gives +20% morale.

[1.1](/Patch_1.1.X "Patch 1.1.X")

M

[![Napoleon’s Ambition icon](/images/3/35/Napoleon%E2%80%99s_Ambition.png)](/File:Napoleon%E2%80%99s_Ambition.png "Napoleon’s Ambition icon")

Napoleon’s Ambition

As Revolutionary France, spread the Revolution to 10 countries.

[![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of France](/images/thumb/d/de/France.png/20px-France.png)](/France "France") [France](/France "France")
*   has used the _“Spread the Revolution”_ peace term 10 times

"Spread the Revolution" peace term can only be used by the [revolution target](/Revolution_target "Revolution target") against nations that have at least one province the Center of Revolution hasn't spread to. They can also only be used against the country directly attacked with the CB (not any allies). Best done quickly as revolutionary ideas can spread across the entire world, preventing the achievement. Small nations in the Americas, Africa and Asia can be targeted to get to 10 if necessary.

[![Emperor](/images/thumb/c/c5/Emperor.png/28px-Emperor.png)](/Emperor_(DLC) "Emperor")

[1.30](/1.30 "1.30")

M

[![Neither Holy, Nor German icon](/images/f/f0/Neither_Holy%2C_Nor_German.jpg)](/File:Neither_Holy,_Nor_German.jpg "Neither Holy, Nor German icon")

[Neither Holy, Nor German](/Neither_Holy,_Nor_German "Neither Holy, Nor German")

Have 7 Free Cities in the Empire, none of which is of a Germanic culture.

*   [![Imperial authority.png](/images/thumb/4/46/Imperial_authority.png/28px-Imperial_authority.png)](/Imperial_authority "Imperial authority") Is emperor of the [Holy Roman Empire](/Holy_Roman_Empire "Holy Roman Empire")
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes")There are least **7** countries which:
    *   *   [![Free City](/images/thumb/b/b1/Gov_free_city.png/24px-Gov_free_city.png)](/Republic#Free_City "Free City") have the government reform [Free City](/Republic#Free_City "Republic")
        *   [![Primary culture.png](/images/thumb/e/e1/Primary_culture.png/24px-Primary_culture.png)](/Primary_culture "Primary culture") have a primary culture which is _not_ in the _Germanic_ culture group

*   There can be germanic free cities, but there have to be at least 7 non-germanic ones
*   You can release OPM client states that are republics. Make sure they dislike you before granting them independence, which actually raises their opinion of you. They will then accept free city status.

[![Common Sense.png](/images/thumb/e/e4/Common_Sense.png/28px-Common_Sense.png)](/Common_Sense "Common Sense")

[1.12](/1.12 "1.12")

M

[![No Pirates in my Caribbean icon](/images/7/78/No_Pirates_in_my_Caribbean.jpg)](/File:No_Pirates_in_my_Caribbean.jpg "No Pirates in my Caribbean icon")

No Pirates in my Caribbean

Own or have a subject own the entire Caribbean.

[![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World").

*   [![Colonists.png](/images/thumb/3/34/Colonists.png/28px-Colonists.png)](/Colonist "Colonist") Owns or has a non-tributary subject own all provinces of the [Caribbean](/Caribbean "Caribbean") region.
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ a [pirate republic](/Pirate_republic "Pirate republic")

*   The required provinces are the geographical region of the Caribbean, not the colonial region. Don't forget Bermuda.
*   [Portugal](/Portugal "Portugal") is a good nation to try for this achievement. Simply make sure to block [Spain](/Spain "Spain") from colonizing any provinces in Africa or in any of the islands in the Atlantic Ocean. This strategy should give enough time to colonize all of the Caribbean. With [![Mandate of Heaven.png](/images/thumb/7/7c/Mandate_of_Heaven.png/28px-Mandate_of_Heaven.png)](/Mandate_of_Heaven "Mandate of Heaven") Mandate of Heaven, the "Portuguese Colonial Growth" splendor ability can give Portugal a huge head start. Annexing Portugal with [Castile](/Castile "Castile") in the early game is also a working method for being the first in the Caribbean. It is enough to start colonizing the province, for it to count towards the achievement.

Not just Pizza

[![Great power.png](/images/thumb/f/fc/Great_power.png/28px-Great_power.png)](/Great_power "Great power") Is a Great power

Parisian Pasha

Assign Pasha to Paris.

Can be done as either [![Flag of Ottomans](/images/thumb/8/89/Ottomans.png/20px-Ottomans.png)](/Ottomans "Ottomans") [Ottomans](/Ottomans "Ottomans") or [![Flag of Rûm](/images/thumb/8/85/R%C3%BBm.png/20px-R%C3%BBm.png)](/R%C3%BBm "Rûm") [Rûm](/R%C3%BBm "Rûm")

Possible reforms are [Ottoman Government](/Ottoman_Government "Ottoman Government"), [Modernized Ottoman Government](/Modernized_Ottoman_Government "Modernized Ottoman Government"), [Reorganized Ottoman Government](/Reorganized_Ottoman_Government "Reorganized Ottoman Government") and [Sultanate of Rûm](/Sultanate_of_R%C3%BBm "Sultanate of Rûm")

Poland can into space

On the flip side, forming Poland will not make you eligible for the achievement.

*   [![Zoroastrianism.png](/images/thumb/2/25/Zoroastrianism.png/28px-Zoroastrianism.png)](/Zoroastrian "Zoroastrian") Is Zoroastrian

Rise of the White Sheep

As Aq Qoyunlu, own Tabriz and have Qara Qoyunlu not exist by 1478.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Aq Qoyunlu](/images/thumb/6/67/Aq_Qoyunlu.png/20px-Aq_Qoyunlu.png)](/Aq_Qoyunlu "Aq Qoyunlu") [Aq Qoyunlu](/Aq_Qoyunlu "Aq Qoyunlu")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") The year is before 1478
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") [![Flag of Qara Qoyunlu](/images/thumb/9/99/Qara_Qoyunlu.png/20px-Qara_Qoyunlu.png)](/Qara_Qoyunlu "Qara Qoyunlu") [Qara Qoyunlu](/Qara_Qoyunlu "Qara Qoyunlu") does _not_ exist
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Owns Tabriz

As long as you own Tabriz, any other provinces owned by [![Flag of Qara Qoyunlu](/images/thumb/9/99/Qara_Qoyunlu.png/20px-Qara_Qoyunlu.png)](/Qara_Qoyunlu "Qara Qoyunlu") [Qara Qoyunlu](/Qara_Qoyunlu "Qara Qoyunlu") at game start can be owned by other nations. Vassal/ally feeding can be useful. [![Flag of Iraq](/images/thumb/c/c4/Iraq.png/20px-Iraq.png)](/Iraq "Iraq") [Iraq](/Iraq "Iraq") has many cores on the required area, and there are several nations that can be released from Qara Qoyunlu's provinces.

[![Ruina Imperii icon](/images/b/b9/Ruina_Imperii.jpg)](/File:Ruina_Imperii.jpg "Ruina Imperii icon")

Ruina Imperii

Dismantle the Holy Roman Empire.

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") There are no countries in the Holy Roman Empire
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") [![Flag of Holy Roman Empire](/images/thumb/e/ee/Holy_Roman_Empire.png/20px-Holy_Roman_Empire.png)](/Holy_Roman_Empire "Holy Roman Empire") [Holy Roman Empire](/Holy_Roman_Empire "Holy Roman Empire") does _not_ exist

Dismantling the Holy Roman Empire requires allying electors or controlling their capital as well as controlling the emperor's capital. Note that the HRE disbanding itself due to lack of an eligible emperor and another nation disbanding HRE both counts for the achievement.

[1.1](/Patch_1.1.X "Patch 1.1.X")

M

[![Sakoku Law icon](/images/c/ce/Sakoku_Law.png)](/File:Sakoku_Law.png "Sakoku Law icon")

Sakoku Law

Go full isolationist in 6 Incidents.

[![Tolerance of the true faith.png](/images/thumb/d/d9/Tolerance_of_the_true_faith.png/28px-Tolerance_of_the_true_faith.png)](/Tolerance_of_the_true_faith "Tolerance of the true faith") Religion is [![Shintoism](/images/thumb/8/85/Shinto.png/28px-Shinto.png)](/Shinto "Shinto") Shinto

Isolationism achievement counter is 6

By "going full isolationist" the game is _not_ referring to the level of isolationism in your country. Rather, it's referring to the fact that each incident has an outcome of either open, neutral, or isolationist. To get the achievement you must get the isolationist outcome of 6 incidents.

*   [![Mandate of Heaven.png](/images/thumb/7/7c/Mandate_of_Heaven.png/28px-Mandate_of_Heaven.png)](/Mandate_of_Heaven "Mandate of Heaven")
*   [![Nation designer.png](/images/a/ab/Nation_designer.png)](/Nation_designer "Nation designer")

[![Sinaasappel! icon](/images/a/a0/Sinaasappel%21.jpg)](/File:Sinaasappel!.jpg "Sinaasappel! icon")

Sinaasappel!

Get Orangists in power with 100% Republican Tradition, and owning a province in China.

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Orangists/Monarchists are in power
*   [![Republican tradition.png](/images/e/ee/Republican_tradition.png)](/Republic_tradition "Republic tradition") **99%** Republican tradition
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own and core at least one province in the [China sub-continent](/China_(sub-continent) "China (sub-continent)").

*   Orangist-Statist mechanics require the [Dutch Republic](/Dutch_Republic "Dutch Republic") (only available for the [![Flag of Netherlands](/images/thumb/3/32/Netherlands.png/20px-Netherlands.png)](/Netherlands "Netherlands") [Netherlands](/Netherlands "Netherlands")) or [The Feuillant System](/The_Feuillant_System "The Feuillant System") (only available to Revolutionary republics) or [States General](/States_General "States General") (only available to Monarchies) government reform. It is _not_ possible to get the achievement with the States General reform, because a monarchy doesn't have republican tradition. The achievement will not be visible unless the country's primary culture is Dutch or Flemish, but it can still be obtained.
*   Colonizing Taiwan counts for the achievement; no need to wait for a Mingplosion.

[![Res Publica.png](/images/thumb/b/b5/Res_Publica.png/28px-Res_Publica.png)](/Res_Publica "Res Publica")

[![Sleepless in Seattle icon](/images/7/7a/Sleepless_in_Seattle.png)](/File:Sleepless_in_Seattle.png "Sleepless in Seattle icon")

Sleepless in Seattle

Own 10 Coffee producing provinces, and have your capital in Salish.

*   [![Capital.png](/images/thumb/6/6e/Capital.png/28px-Capital.png)](/Capital "Capital") Capital is Salish (874)
*   [![Coffee.png](/images/thumb/e/e9/Coffee.png/28px-Coffee.png)](/Coffee "Coffee") Own 10 Coffee producing provinces

Easiest to complete as a New World nation, as this will simplify moving your capital and help with attacking colonial nations. Coffee has an increased chance to be produced in the Brazil, Caribbean and Colombia colonial regions.

Super Trooper

Starting as Sweden, enact the Allotment System government reform, have 80 regiments of Carolean raised at the same time with at least +40% infantry combat ability.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Sweden](/images/thumb/9/98/Sweden.png/20px-Sweden.png)](/Sweden "Sweden") [Sweden](/Sweden "Sweden")

*   [![Government monarchy.png](/images/thumb/4/4d/Government_monarchy.png/28px-Government_monarchy.png)](/Monarchy "Monarchy")/[![Government republic.png](/images/thumb/5/5d/Government_republic.png/28px-Government_republic.png)](/Republic "Republic") Has enacted the [Allotment System](/Allotment_System "Allotment System") government reform
*   Has at least 80 [carolean](/Army#Caroleans "Army") regiments
*   [![Infantry combat ability.png](/images/thumb/2/21/Infantry_combat_ability.png/28px-Infantry_combat_ability.png)](/Infantry_combat_ability "Infantry combat ability") Infantry combat ability is at least **40%**

Take quality and innovative ideas for **45%** [![Infantry combat ability.png](/images/thumb/2/21/Infantry_combat_ability.png/28px-Infantry_combat_ability.png)](/Infantry_combat_ability "Infantry combat ability") infantry combat ability with swedish ideas. Since only development from swedish and finnish cultured provinces counts towards increasing how many [carolean](/Army#Caroleans "Army") regiments are available you need to culture convert other provinces to reach 800 development.

[![Lions of the North.png](/images/thumb/c/cd/Lions_of_the_North.png/28px-Lions_of_the_North.png)](/Lions_of_the_North "Lions of the North")

Swahili Persuasion

As Kilwa, convert all of the Moluccas and Indonesia.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Kilwa](/images/thumb/c/cb/Kilwa.png/20px-Kilwa.png)](/Kilwa "Kilwa") [Kilwa](/Kilwa "Kilwa")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Kilwa](/images/thumb/c/cb/Kilwa.png/20px-Kilwa.png)](/Kilwa "Kilwa") [Kilwa](/Kilwa "Kilwa")
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") all provinces in the regions [Moluccas](/Moluccas "Moluccas") and [Indonesia](/Indonesia "Indonesia") follow the state religion of [![Flag of Kilwa](/images/thumb/c/cb/Kilwa.png/20px-Kilwa.png)](/Kilwa "Kilwa") [Kilwa](/Kilwa "Kilwa")

Uncolonized provinces must also follow your state religion. [Propagate Religion](/Trade#Trade_policies "Trade") is helpful however try to keep the Europeans out of the area as it won't convert Christian provinces.

This achievement is only visible if the [![Origins.png](/images/thumb/8/8e/Origins.png/28px-Origins.png)](/Origins "Origins") Origins DLC is active, but it can be achieved even without the DLC

Sweden is not overpowered!

Own and have cores on the entire Baltic coastline as Sweden.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Sweden](/images/thumb/9/98/Sweden.png/20px-Sweden.png)](/Sweden "Sweden") [Sweden](/Sweden "Sweden")

Expand

[![Achievement sweden conditions map.png](/images/thumb/9/90/Achievement_sweden_conditions_map.png/140px-Achievement_sweden_conditions_map.png)](/File:Achievement_sweden_conditions_map.png)

It is only required that you start as Sweden. Forming Scandinavia or releasing and playing as a vassal won't prevent getting the achievement.

[1.1](/Patch_1.1.X "Patch 1.1.X")

M

[![Sweet Harmony icon](/images/6/6d/Sweet_Harmony.png)](/File:Sweet_Harmony.png "Sweet Harmony icon")

Sweet Harmony

Harmonize 7 religions as Confucian.

*   [![Confucianism](/images/thumb/a/a2/Confucianism.png/28px-Confucianism.png)](/Confucian "Confucian") Is Confucian
*   [![Yearly harmony increase.png](/images/thumb/c/c3/Yearly_harmony_increase.png/28px-Yearly_harmony_increase.png)](/Harmony "Harmony") Have 7 harmonized religions

Harmonization takes 33.3 years, but events can speed it up marginally. [![Flag of Ming](/images/thumb/a/a5/Ming.png/20px-Ming.png)](/Ming "Ming") [Ming](/Ming "Ming") and [![Flag of Korea](/images/thumb/4/45/Korea.png/20px-Korea.png)](/Korea "Korea") [Korea](/Korea "Korea") start with Mahayana already harmonized. Easiest as Ming, conquering some Hindu, Sunni, and Shinto land.

It is also a good option to start as Korea, form [![Flag of Japan](/images/thumb/f/fc/Japan.png/20px-Japan.png)](/Japan "Japan") [Japan](/Japan "Japan"), then conquer Philippines, Indonesia to achieve this achievement. Harmonization requires owning 20 development of the target religion or religious group. Might be quicker and more fun to create a custom nation with harmonizing ideas.

*   [![Mandate of Heaven.png](/images/thumb/7/7c/Mandate_of_Heaven.png/28px-Mandate_of_Heaven.png)](/Mandate_of_Heaven "Mandate of Heaven")
*   [![Nation designer.png](/images/a/ab/Nation_designer.png)](/Nation_designer "Nation designer")

[1.20](/1.20 "1.20")

M

[![Switzerlake icon](/images/7/7b/Switzerlake.png)](/File:Switzerlake.png "Switzerlake icon")

Switzerlake

Own 99 provinces as Switzerland while owning no ports.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Switzerland](/images/thumb/0/01/Switzerland.png/20px-Switzerland.png)](/Switzerland "Switzerland") [Switzerland](/Switzerland "Switzerland")

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Own 99 provinces
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") Own no ports

It is required to start as [![Flag of Switzerland](/images/thumb/0/01/Switzerland.png/20px-Switzerland.png)](/Switzerland "Switzerland") [Switzerland](/Switzerland "Switzerland"). Forming it later doesn't give the achievement. Can be achieved as part of a normal game and then giving away all the coastal provinces. Avoid expanding into the Holy Roman Empire to prevent high aggressive expansion.

[1.9](/1.9 "1.9")

[![Take that, von Habsburgs! icon](/images/6/6f/Take_that%2C_von_Habsburgs%21.jpg)](/File:Take_that,_von_Habsburgs!.jpg "Take that, von Habsburgs! icon")

Take that, von Habsburgs!

As Hungary, own all of Austria as core provinces.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Hungary](/images/thumb/6/6a/Hungary.png/20px-Hungary.png)](/Hungary "Hungary") [Hungary](/Hungary "Hungary")

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Hungary](/images/thumb/6/6a/Hungary.png/20px-Hungary.png)](/Hungary "Hungary") [Hungary](/Hungary "Hungary")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own and core all of the [Inner Austria](/Inner_Austria "Inner Austria"), [Austria Proper](/Austria_Proper "Austria Proper"), [Carniola](/Carniola "Carniola") and [Tirol](/European_regions#Tirol "European regions") areas.

Expand

[![Take that, von Habsburgs! map.png](/images/e/e2/Take_that%2C_von_Habsburgs%21_map.png)](/File:Take_that,_von_Habsburgs!_map.png)

[](/File:Take_that,_von_Habsburgs!_map.png "Enlarge")

Besides provinces from [![Flag of Austria](/images/thumb/7/7f/Austria.png/20px-Austria.png)](/Austria "Austria") [Austria](/Austria "Austria"), also requires taking Istria (130) from [![Flag of Venice](/images/thumb/e/e1/Venice.png/20px-Venice.png)](/Venice "Venice") [Venice](/Venice "Venice"), Cilli (4751) from [![Flag of Cilli](/images/thumb/7/71/Cilli.png/20px-Cilli.png)](/Cilli "Cilli") [Cilli](/Cilli "Cilli"), Trentino (110) from [![Flag of Trent](/images/thumb/9/94/Trent.png/20px-Trent.png)](/Trent "Trent") [Trent](/Trent "Trent") and Bregenz (4710) from [![Flag of Bregenz](/images/thumb/4/4d/Bregenz.png/20px-Bregenz.png)](/Bregenz "Bregenz") [Bregenz](/Bregenz "Bregenz"). Does not require Sundgau (1880), Breisgau (72) or anything else Austria may have expanded into.

M

[![That's No Mon icon](/images/c/c8/That%27s_No_Mon.jpg)](/File:That%27s_No_Mon.jpg "That's No Mon icon")

That's No Mon

As Pegu, own at least 50 provinces that are not of the Mon culture.

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Pegu](/images/thumb/3/3b/Pegu.png/20px-Pegu.png)](/Pegu "Pegu") [Pegu](/Pegu "Pegu")
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Pegu](/images/thumb/3/3b/Pegu.png/20px-Pegu.png)](/Pegu "Pegu") [Pegu](/Pegu "Pegu")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") At least 50 owned provinces do not have Mon culture

This achievement is only visible if the [![Leviathan.png](/images/thumb/0/0a/Leviathan.png/28px-Leviathan.png)](/Leviathan "Leviathan") Leviathan DLC is active, but it can be achieved even without the DLC. This can be done at the same time as the [Sailor Mon](/Sailor_Mon "Sailor Mon") achievement, and will often occur without any additional effort. With Leviathan, the [![Flag of Pegu](/images/thumb/3/3b/Pegu.png/20px-Pegu.png)](/Pegu "Pegu") [Pegu](/Pegu "Pegu") mission tree grants a subjugation cb on [![Flag of Ayutthaya](/images/thumb/9/9d/Ayutthaya.png/20px-Ayutthaya.png)](/Ayutthaya "Ayutthaya") [Ayutthaya](/Ayutthaya "Ayutthaya"), which can lead to quite a large acquisition of provinces. The player can also flip cultures to Burmese to ensure colonies are not of Mon culture and can culture convert their original provinces to a new culture.

The Levant Turnabout

As the Mamluks, have 100 Army Professionalism and annex the Ottomans.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Mamluks](/images/thumb/c/ca/The_Mamluks.png/20px-The_Mamluks.png)](/Mamluks "Mamluks") [Mamluks](/Mamluks "Mamluks")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Have **100** Army Professionalism
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") [![Flag of Ottomans](/images/thumb/8/89/Ottomans.png/20px-Ottomans.png)](/Ottomans "Ottomans") [Ottomans](/Ottomans "Ottomans") does _not_ exist
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own and core Edirne (149), Constantinople (151), Hüdavendigar (317), and Ankara (326)

Expand

[![The Levant Turnabout map.png](/images/7/7f/The_Levant_Turnabout_map.png)](/File:The_Levant_Turnabout_map.png)

[](/File:The_Levant_Turnabout_map.png "Enlarge")

Forming [![Flag of Arabia](/images/thumb/e/ed/Arabia.png/20px-Arabia.png)](/Arabia "Arabia") [Arabia](/Arabia "Arabia") will not prevent the achievement. Be sure to attack the Ottomans early or at least cut them off from further expansion into Arabia and the Caucasus. You also don't need to have 100% professionalism at the time of annexing the Ottomans. You can just build up to that number later.

[![Cradle of Civilization.png](/images/thumb/2/23/Cradle_of_Civilization.png/28px-Cradle_of_Civilization.png)](/Cradle_of_Civilization "Cradle of Civilization")

[1.23](/1.23 "1.23")

M

[![The Navigator icon](/images/8/88/The_Navigator.png)](/File:The_Navigator.png "The Navigator icon")

The Navigator

As Portugal, get owned provinces in Africa, India and Indonesia before 1500.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Portugal](/images/thumb/1/12/Portugal.png/20px-Portugal.png)](/Portugal "Portugal") [Portugal](/Portugal "Portugal")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") The year is before 1500
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Owns a province in the continent of Africa and the super-regions of India and East Indies.

It's enough to just start a colony. It doesn't need to be finished. Portugal gets [an event](/Portuguese_events#Vasco_da_Gama_in_India "Portuguese events") to instantly annex Goa if the [appropriate mission](/Portuguese_missions#Push_to_India "Portuguese missions") is completed. The islands of Hollhavai and the Maldives are considered part of the East Indies despite being closer to India.

[1.20](/1.20 "1.20")

M

[![The Ostenders icon](/images/4/4c/The_Ostenders.png)](/File:The_Ostenders.png "The Ostenders icon")

The Ostenders

As Austria have the District and Military Administration investments in the West Bengal area.

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Austria](/images/thumb/7/7f/Austria.png/20px-Austria.png)](/Austria "Austria") [Austria](/Austria "Austria")
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") No more than 1 custom nation exists in the world
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") Used no more than 201 nation designer points

*   [![Subject tradecompany icon.png](/images/thumb/8/8d/Subject_tradecompany_icon.png/28px-Subject_tradecompany_icon.png)](/Trade_company "Trade company") Owns a province in West Bengal area with the District trade company investment
*   [![Subject tradecompany icon.png](/images/thumb/8/8d/Subject_tradecompany_icon.png/28px-Subject_tradecompany_icon.png)](/Trade_company "Trade company") Owns a province in West Bengal area with the Military Administration trade company investment

Either conquer or charter Bengal Delta from its owner. Add it to a trade company and save up [![Gold Icon.png](/images/2/26/Gold_Icon.png)](/Ducats "Ducats") 1,200 ducats. Switch to the territory tab. Buy the second building of both the Foreign Influence and Governance Trade Company Investments.

This is one of only two achievements which allows a [![Nation designer.png](/images/a/ab/Nation_designer.png)](/Nation_designer "Nation designer") custom nation on the map which can't be earned by playing that custom nation.

[![Dharma.png](/images/thumb/f/fc/Dharma.png/28px-Dharma.png)](/Dharma "Dharma")

[1.26](/1.26 "1.26")

M

[![The pen is mightier than the sword icon](/images/9/90/The_pen_is_mightier_than_the_sword.jpg)](/File:The_pen_is_mightier_than_the_sword.jpg "The pen is mightier than the sword icon")

The pen is mightier than the sword

Have three unions at the same time as Austria.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Austria](/images/thumb/7/7f/Austria.png/20px-Austria.png)](/Austria "Austria") [Austria](/Austria "Austria")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Austria](/images/thumb/7/7f/Austria.png/20px-Austria.png)](/Austria "Austria") [Austria](/Austria "Austria")
*   [![Personal union.png](/images/thumb/3/39/Personal_union.png/28px-Personal_union.png)](/Personal_union "Personal union") Have 3 [personal unions](/Personal_Union "Personal Union")

[Austrian missions](/Austrian_missions "Austrian missions") can give Restore Union CBs on Bohemia and Hungary and several others with the Emperor DLC. Check the page for the exact requirements. Acquiring PUs on these two are will be sufficient for the achievement, as Croatia is a PU subject under Hungary that will be transferred onto you. Events can also lead to a Habsburg ruling in Spain, allowing Austria the opportunity to claim the throne of Castile, and possibly Aragon and Naples as well.

[1.1](/Patch_1.1.X "Patch 1.1.X")

M

  

[![The Prince of Egypt icon](/images/8/87/The_Prince_of_Egypt.png)](/File:The_Prince_of_Egypt.png "The Prince of Egypt icon")

The Prince of Egypt

Starting as Florence, form Egypt.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Florence](/images/thumb/d/d9/Florence.png/20px-Florence.png)](/Florence "Florence") [Florence](/Florence "Florence")

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Egypt](/images/thumb/3/37/Egypt.png/20px-Egypt.png)](/Egypt "Egypt") [Egypt](/Egypt "Egypt")

Forming [![Flag of Tuscany](/images/thumb/b/b2/Tuscany.png/20px-Tuscany.png)](/Tuscany "Tuscany") [Tuscany](/Tuscany "Tuscany") or another country before Egypt will not prevent this achievement. As of 1.26 [![Flag of Italy](/images/thumb/2/2a/Italy.png/20px-Italy.png)](/Italy "Italy") [Italy](/Italy "Italy") is an end game tag, and if you form it you won't be able to form [![Flag of Egypt](/images/thumb/3/37/Egypt.png/20px-Egypt.png)](/Egypt "Egypt") [Egypt](/Egypt "Egypt").

One intermediate tag that may be useful is [![Flag of Jerusalem](/images/thumb/e/ef/Jerusalem.png/20px-Jerusalem.png)](/Jerusalem "Jerusalem") [Jerusalem](/Jerusalem "Jerusalem"), since it gives claims on most of the Egyptian culture lands.

You can play a normal campaign (even form Italy) then release and play as the mamluks, achieve independence and form Egypt at the end. You can go as far to make a backup save so you can continue as Italy normally, if you please.

[1.23](/1.23 "1.23")

M

[![The Rising Sun icon](/images/2/20/The_Rising_Sun.jpg)](/File:The_Rising_Sun.jpg "The Rising Sun icon")

The Rising Sun

Own and have cores on all of Japan as a European nation.

[![Capital.png](/images/thumb/6/6e/Capital.png/28px-Capital.png)](/Capital "Capital") Capital is in Europe

[![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own and core all provinces in the [Japan region](/Asian_regions#Japan "Asian regions")

*   The Japan region includes Okinawa, Tsushima, Hokkaido, and the Kuril Islands.
*   One possible and relatively easy way to do this is with [![Flag of Spain](/images/thumb/5/58/Spain.png/20px-Spain.png)](/Spain "Spain") [Spain](/Spain "Spain"). After you can reach the East Siberian Coastline after getting some colonies in [North](/North_America "North America") or [South America](/South_America "South America"), get a colony there and start wars with [![Flag of Japan](/images/thumb/f/fc/Japan.png/20px-Japan.png)](/Japan "Japan") [Japan](/Japan "Japan") afterwards. Due to their lacking of good military forces and technology those wars are pretty easy to win.

[![The Sudanese Expedition icon](/images/f/f8/The_Sudanese_Expedition.jpg)](/File:The_Sudanese_Expedition.jpg "The Sudanese Expedition icon")

The Sudanese Expedition

Starting as Morocco, conquer the Niger and Sahel Regions.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Morocco](/images/thumb/e/e4/Morocco.png/20px-Morocco.png)](/Morocco "Morocco") [Morocco](/Morocco "Morocco")

[![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own all of the [Niger](/Niger "Niger") and [Sahel](/Sahel "Sahel") regions

_For the event see: [The Sudanese Expedition](/Moroccan_events#The_Sudanese_Expedition "Moroccan events")._  

Forming [![Flag of Andalusia](/images/thumb/0/09/Andalusia.png/20px-Andalusia.png)](/Andalusia "Andalusia") [Andalusia](/Andalusia "Andalusia") will not prevent the achievement.

The provinces of Yola, Wukari, Bauchi, and Djado do NOT need to be fully colonized, building a colony will suffice.

[The Uncommonwealth](/The_Uncommonwealth "The Uncommonwealth")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Commonwealth](/images/thumb/d/df/Commonwealth.png/20px-Commonwealth.png)](/Commonwealth "Commonwealth") [Commonwealth](/Commonwealth "Commonwealth")

Lithuanias missions will give a restoration of Union casus belli against Poland, if Lithuania are independent after 1450, rival Poland and have annexed all of [![Flag of Livonian Order](/images/thumb/8/81/Livonian_Order.png/20px-Livonian_Order.png)](/Livonian_Order "Livonian Order") [Livonian Order](/Livonian_Order "Livonian Order") and [![Flag of Riga](/images/thumb/4/4c/Riga.png/20px-Riga.png)](/Riga "Riga") [Riga](/Riga "Riga")

The White Elephant

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Ayutthaya](/images/thumb/9/9d/Ayutthaya.png/20px-Ayutthaya.png)](/Ayutthaya "Ayutthaya") [Ayutthaya](/Ayutthaya "Ayutthaya")

*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own and core all of the [Indochina](/Indochina "Indochina") and [Burma](/Burma "Burma") regions

[1.12](/1.12 "1.12")

M

[![This is fine icon](/images/7/7b/This_is_fine.png)](/File:This_is_fine.png "This is fine icon")

This is fine

Have at least +10 Global Unrest and be in a winning coalition war, which was targeted against you.

*   [![National unrest.png](/images/thumb/8/8d/National_unrest.png/28px-National_unrest.png)](/National_unrest "National unrest") National unrest is at least **+10**
*   [![Coalition.png](/images/thumb/c/cc/Coalition.png/28px-Coalition.png)](/Coalition "Coalition") Is the defending war leader in a punitive war and has at least [![War score.png](/images/thumb/b/b3/War_score.png/28px-War_score.png)](/War_score "War score") **+30%** war score in that war

The national unrest can be seen in the stability tab.

Start as [![Flag of England](/images/thumb/2/21/England.png/20px-England.png)](/England "England") [England](/England "England"), declare no-CB wars on two Irish nations. White peace them ASAP. Other Irish nations and [![Flag of Scotland](/images/thumb/2/27/Scotland.png/20px-Scotland.png)](/Scotland "Scotland") [Scotland](/Scotland "Scotland") should create a coalition against you. Delete your armies. When they declare the coalition war on you, block the strait at Ayshire, then occupy [![Flag of Scotland](/images/thumb/2/27/Scotland.png/20px-Scotland.png)](/Scotland "Scotland") [Scotland](/Scotland "Scotland"). This should give you enough warscore; if not, beat some of their armies. Wait for the War of the Roses disaster to fire, which should give enough unrest (altogether with war exhaustion and −3 stability). Can be done in 4 years, depending on how quick the coalition war fires. Can also be done in combination with [To the Bone](#To_the_Bone). Start as [![Flag of Bone](/images/thumb/2/2c/Bone.png/20px-Bone.png)](/Bone "Bone") [Bone](/Bone "Bone") and declare no-CB wars on your two immediate neighbours, pillage their capitals, truce break and repeat. When you reach -3 stability stab up once and continue. This will give a high war exhaustion and a coalition should form against you.

[1.32](/1.32 "1.32")

M

[![This navy can take it all icon](/images/9/9f/This_navy_can_take_it_all.jpg)](/File:This_navy_can_take_it_all.jpg "This navy can take it all icon")

This navy can take it all

Gain at least 7.0 naval morale.

[![Morale of navies.png](/images/thumb/8/80/Morale_of_navies.png/28px-Morale_of_navies.png)](/Morale_of_navies "Morale of navies") Have **7** Morale of navies

Research diplomatic techs, invest in ideas that improve [naval morale](/Naval_warfare#Max_naval_morale "Naval warfare"), maintain high [prestige](/Prestige "Prestige") and [navy tradition](/Navy_tradition "Navy tradition"). Finally hire a [Naval Reformer](/Naval_Reformer "Naval Reformer").

[1.1](/Patch_1.1.X "Patch 1.1.X")

M

[![This Revolution Was Crushed icon](/images/a/a5/This_Revolution_Was_Crushed.jpg)](/File:This_Revolution_Was_Crushed.jpg "This Revolution Was Crushed icon")

This Revolution Was Crushed

In a war against the target of the Revolution, control their capital and have at least 99% war score.

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is at war with a revolution target
*   [![Capital.png](/images/thumb/6/6e/Capital.png/28px-Capital.png)](/Capital "Capital") Control the capital of the revolution target
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Have greater than **98%** warscore against the revolution target

The [Revolution](/Revolution "Revolution") disaster (and the [French Revolution](/French_Revolution "French Revolution") variant) is announced in a major event: '[Revolution in $COUNTRY$](/Revolution#Revolution_in_.24COUNTRY.24 "Revolution")' (or '[The General Estates](/French_Revolution#The_General_Estates "French Revolution")').

With the [![Emperor](/images/thumb/c/c5/Emperor.png/28px-Emperor.png)](/Emperor_(DLC) "Emperor") Emperor DLC, there can be multiple revolutionary countries, but there can only be one revolutionary target. And it is possible that there is no revolutionary target even though there are revolutionary countries. The "Birthplace of the revolution" icon in the lower right part of the screen shows which country is the revolutionary target.

Without the [![Emperor](/images/thumb/c/c5/Emperor.png/28px-Emperor.png)](/Emperor_(DLC) "Emperor") Emperor DLC, A country will become the revolution target, with "Revolutionary" in its name, if its capital is occupied by rebels while the disaster is active. The disaster spawns a stack of rebels, adds +10 national unrest and removes 3 stability. The player can check if the disaster is still active for a country by looking for the +10 unrest modifier on its provinces.

It is feasible both to wait for (or encourage) an AI revolution target, or to become the revolutionary target oneself before releasing (and playing as) a powerful vassal or colonial nation.

[![Art of War.png](/images/thumb/0/0f/Art_of_War.png/28px-Art_of_War.png)](/Art_of_War "Art of War")

Total Control

[![Trustworthy icon](/images/4/49/Trustworthy.jpg)](/File:Trustworthy.jpg "Trustworthy icon")

Trustworthy

Have five allies with 100 trust towards you each.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Have 5 allies with 100 trust

Can be done as [![Flag of Ming](/images/thumb/a/a5/Ming.png/20px-Ming.png)](/Ming "Ming") [Ming](/Ming "Ming") by releasing 5 OPMs (not bordering each other), allying them and waiting for the trust to tick up.

Can be sped up with [![Rights of Man.png](/images/thumb/5/50/Rights_of_Man.png/28px-Rights_of_Man.png)](/Rights_of_Man "Rights of Man") Rights of Man by using the _Influence nation_ interaction as a [great power](/Great_power "Great power"), or with [![The Cossacks.png](/images/thumb/b/b6/The_Cossacks.png/28px-The_Cossacks.png)](/The_Cossacks "The Cossacks") The Cossacks by trading favors for trust.

[1.14](/1.14 "1.14")

M

[![Turtles all the way down icon](/images/f/f5/Turtles_all_the_way_down.png)](/File:Turtles_all_the_way_down.png "Turtles all the way down icon")

Turtles all the way down

As Korea get 135% Ship Durability.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Korea](/images/thumb/4/45/Korea.png/20px-Korea.png)](/Korea "Korea") [Korea](/Korea "Korea")

[![Ship durability](/images/thumb/5/58/Ship_durability.png/28px-Ship_durability.png)](/Ship_durability "Ship durability") Ship durability is at least 135%.

Can be easily achieved during a standard Korea Emperor of China run by waiting until you have a ruler with the "navigator" personality (which gives +10% ship durability) and enacting the "Promote Naval Officers" celestial empire decree for an additional +20% durability. This, along with Korea's 4th national idea will give 140% total ship durability. To avoid waiting for a ruler with the correct personality, naval ideas can be selected for its 10% ship durability bonus.

[1.20](/1.20 "1.20")

[![Victorian Three icon](/images/a/a5/Victorian_Three.jpg)](/File:Victorian_Three.jpg "Victorian Three icon")

[Victorian Three](/Victorian_Three "Victorian Three")

As Busoga, Buganda or Karagwe, reach administrative, diplomatic and military technology level 32.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as _either_:

*    [![Flag of Buganda](/images/thumb/4/43/Buganda.png/20px-Buganda.png)](/Buganda "Buganda") [Buganda](/Buganda "Buganda")
*    [![Flag of Busoga](/images/thumb/7/7f/Busoga.png/20px-Busoga.png)](/Busoga "Busoga") [Busoga](/Busoga "Busoga")
*    [![Flag of Karagwe](/images/thumb/d/d6/Karagwe.png/20px-Karagwe.png)](/Karagwe "Karagwe") [Karagwe](/Karagwe "Karagwe")

*   [![Administrative technology.png](/images/8/8e/Administrative_technology.png)](/Administrative_technology "Administrative technology") Administration technology is **32**
*   [![Diplomatic technology.png](/images/2/22/Diplomatic_technology.png)](/Diplomatic_technology "Diplomatic technology") Diplomatic technology is **32**
*   [![Military technology.png](/images/1/1a/Military_technology.png)](/Military_technology "Military technology") Military technology is **32**

Most easily accomplished by manually spawning Renaissance, Colonialism and Printing Press, and not expanding too much. To get the other institutions, build manufactories and universities. Researching level 32 loses the ahead-of-time penalty in 1820.

Forming [![Flag of Kitara](/images/thumb/7/79/Kitara.png/20px-Kitara.png)](/Kitara "Kitara") [Kitara](/Kitara "Kitara") will not prevent this achievement.

[1.16](/1.16 "1.16")

M

[![We bled for this icon](/images/6/6b/We_bled_for_this.jpg)](/File:We_bled_for_this.jpg "We bled for this icon")

We bled for this

Win a war with at least one million dead on both sides.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Won a war with over 1 million casualties on both sides.

*   Both sides each need to have at least 1 million casualties (attrition _does_ count) in the war details screen when the war leader is peaced out. Allies and enemies that are peaced out before the war leader do not contribute their casualties.
*   League Wars (requires [![Art of War.png](/images/thumb/0/0f/Art_of_War.png/28px-Art_of_War.png)](/Art_of_War "Art of War") Art of War) can be a good time to get this achievement if you are the war leader. Protect your allies and don't separate peace countries. Alternatively, you can trigger a big war in the late 1700s after you get strong. Regardless, be prepared to buy down war exhaustion as the war will almost certainly last way longer than it should.

*   [![Rights of Man.png](/images/thumb/5/50/Rights_of_Man.png/28px-Rights_of_Man.png)](/Rights_of_Man "Rights of Man")
*   [![Nation designer.png](/images/a/ab/Nation_designer.png)](/Nation_designer "Nation designer")

Where are the penguins?

*    [![Flag of Betsimisaraka](/images/thumb/1/16/Betsimisaraka.png/20px-Betsimisaraka.png)](/Betsimisaraka "Betsimisaraka") [Betsimisaraka](/Betsimisaraka "Betsimisaraka")

*    [![Flag of Imerina](/images/thumb/0/07/Imerina.png/20px-Imerina.png)](/Imerina "Imerina") [Imerina](/Imerina "Imerina")
*    [![Flag of Mahafaly](/images/thumb/f/fc/Mahafaly.png/20px-Mahafaly.png)](/Mahafaly "Mahafaly") [Mahafaly](/Mahafaly "Mahafaly")
*    [![Flag of Antemoro](/images/thumb/b/bc/Antemoro.png/20px-Antemoro.png)](/Antemoro "Antemoro") [Antemoro](/Antemoro "Antemoro")

[![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own and core all provinces in the following areas:

*   Madagascar Highlands
*   Betsimasaraka
*   Sakalava
*   Southern Madagascar

Expand[![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own or have a non-tributary subject own all the following provinces:

*   Cape (1177)
*   Swellendam (1179)
*   Algoa Bay (833)

ExpandMap of the provinces:

[![Where are the penguins map.png](/images/thumb/3/37/Where_are_the_penguins_map.png/300px-Where_are_the_penguins_map.png)](/File:Where_are_the_penguins_map.png)

[](/File:Where_are_the_penguins_map.png "Enlarge")

After taking over Madagascar befriend [![Flag of Kilwa](/images/thumb/c/cb/Kilwa.png/20px-Kilwa.png)](/Kilwa "Kilwa") [Kilwa](/Kilwa "Kilwa") to get Feudalism spreading. Take Exploration, then Expansion and colonize the provinces on the Cape of Good Hope. Afterwards focus your attention mostly on the Atlantic islands and South America to get the required provinces before [![Flag of Portugal](/images/thumb/1/12/Portugal.png/20px-Portugal.png)](/Portugal "Portugal") [Portugal](/Portugal "Portugal") does, only spreading east when waiting for colonies to finish for reach. Station troops in Australia after the colonial nation forms, otherwise the natives will attack.

This achievement is only visible if the [![Origins.png](/images/thumb/8/8e/Origins.png/28px-Origins.png)](/Origins "Origins") Origins DLC is active, but no DLC is needed to complete it.

[1.32](/1.32 "1.32")

M

[![Wonderful icon](/images/a/a6/Wonderful.jpg)](/File:Wonderful.jpg "Wonderful icon")

Wonderful

Own 8 different monuments on tier 3.

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Has 8 Tier 3 monuments

Easiest done with [![Flag of France](/images/thumb/d/de/France.png/20px-France.png)](/France "France") [France](/France "France") as they starts with 2 and can expand into [![Flag of England](/images/thumb/2/21/England.png/20px-England.png)](/England "England") [England](/England "England"), Iberia, [![Flag of Morocco](/images/thumb/e/e4/Morocco.png/20px-Morocco.png)](/Morocco "Morocco") [Morocco](/Morocco "Morocco") and [![Flag of Norway](/images/thumb/0/0f/Norway.png/20px-Norway.png)](/Norway "Norway") [Norway](/Norway "Norway") while starting with a decent economy. Alternatively a Buddhist nation in Indochina can do it easily as they have 6 eligible monuments in Tibet and Indochina alone and limited aggressive expansion penalties.

India is also a good option as it has more than 8 monuments. If the monument has religious requirements preventing from building it, don't forget that you can improve your subject's monument and then integrate them.

[![Leviathan.png](/images/thumb/0/0a/Leviathan.png/28px-Leviathan.png)](/Leviathan "Leviathan")

[1.31](/1.31 "1.31")

M

[![Brentry! icon](/images/b/bc/Brentry%21.png)](/File:Brentry!.png "Brentry! icon")

Brentry!

Starting as England, form the Angevin Kingdom and enact all the 'Acts of Crown' parliamentary issues.

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Angevin Kingdom](/images/thumb/b/be/Angevin_Kingdom.png/20px-Angevin_Kingdom.png)](/Angevin_Kingdom "Angevin Kingdom") [Angevin Kingdom](/Angevin_Kingdom "Angevin Kingdom")
*   [![Parliament.png](/images/thumb/f/f9/Parliament.png/28px-Parliament.png)](/Parliament "Parliament") Has enacted all of the following parliament issues:
    *   Crown of Ireland Act
    *   Act of the Spanish Crown
    *   Act of the Italian Crown
    *   Crown of the Empire

Do _not_ dismantle the HRE, because that prevents the issue _“Crown of the Empire”_.

Copium Wars

[![](/images/thumb/3/3e/Stiff_Upper_Lippe_map.png/140px-Stiff_Upper_Lippe_map.png)](/File:Stiff_Upper_Lippe_map.png)

Britain region

This is one of only two achievements which allows a [![Nation designer.png](/images/a/ab/Nation_designer.png)](/Nation_designer "Nation designer") custom nation on the map which can't be earned by playing that custom nation.

[1.35](/1.35 "1.35")

M

[![No Country for Old Tercios icon](/images/c/c6/No_Country_for_Old_Tercios.png)](/File:No_Country_for_Old_Tercios.png "No Country for Old Tercios icon")

No Country for Old Tercios

As Spain, have Reformed Tercios, 33 Tercio Units, and control 3 Great Power capitals at the same time

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Spain](/images/thumb/5/58/Spain.png/20px-Spain.png)](/Spain "Spain") [Spain](/Spain "Spain")
*   Has the modifier _“Reformed Tercio Regiments”_ (from the mission [Refine the Tercios](/Castilian_missions#Refine_the_Tercios "Castilian missions"))
*   Has at least 33 [tercio](/Army#Tercio "Army") regiments
*   [![Capital.png](/images/thumb/6/6e/Capital.png/28px-Capital.png)](/Capital "Capital") Control the capitals of three [![Great power.png](/images/thumb/f/fc/Great_power.png/28px-Great_power.png)](/Great_power "Great power") great powers

To get the mission, [![Flag of Spain](/images/thumb/5/58/Spain.png/20px-Spain.png)](/Spain "Spain") [Spain](/Spain "Spain") must be formed by a country which _never_ was [![Flag of Aragon](/images/thumb/6/61/Aragon.png/20px-Aragon.png)](/Aragon "Aragon") [Aragon](/Aragon "Aragon").

[![Domination.png](/images/thumb/3/3d/Domination.png/28px-Domination.png)](/Domination "Domination") _and_ [![Rights of Man.png](/images/thumb/5/50/Rights_of_Man.png/28px-Rights_of_Man.png)](/Rights_of_Man "Rights of Man") _or_ [![Emperor](/images/thumb/c/c5/Emperor.png/28px-Emperor.png)](/Emperor_(DLC) "Emperor")

[1.35](/1.35 "1.35")

M

[![The Reapers icon](/images/8/87/The_Reapers.png)](/File:The_Reapers.png "The Reapers icon")

The Reapers

Starting as Aragon, be a Peasant Republic and have Madrid and Paris owned by any Peasant Republic.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Aragon](/images/thumb/6/61/Aragon.png/20px-Aragon.png)](/Aragon "Aragon") [Aragon](/Aragon "Aragon")

*   [![Government republic.png](/images/thumb/5/5d/Government_republic.png/28px-Government_republic.png)](/Republic "Republic") Has enacted the [Peasants Republic](/Peasants_Republic "Peasants Republic") government reform
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") The owner of the province Madrid (217) has enacted the [Peasants Republic](/Peasants_Republic "Peasants Republic") government reform
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") The owner of the province Paris (183) has enacted the [Peasants Republic](/Peasants_Republic "Peasants Republic") government reform

The only feasible way to become a peasant republic as Aragon is with the third option in the event [Sindicat Remença](/Aragonese_events#flavor_ara.6 "Aragonese events"). That option is only available if the country has negative stability or less than 50 legitimacy when the event happens. Breaking a royal marriage or declaring a no-cb war are easy ways to get negative stability at the start of the game. You'll still be eligible for the Iberian Wedding as a republic.

[1.35](/1.35 "1.35")

M

[![A Blessed Nation icon](/images/e/e5/A_Blessed_Nation.jpg)](/File:A_Blessed_Nation.jpg "A Blessed Nation icon")

A Blessed Nation

As a Coptic Nation, gain all 5 Blessings.

*   [![Coptic.png](/images/thumb/7/74/Coptic.png/28px-Coptic.png)](/Coptic "Coptic") Is Coptic
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Have 5 active blessings

Player can start as Muslim nation (such as The Ottomans) and switch religion by rebels.

[1.18](/1.18 "1.18")

H

[![A Decent Reserve icon](/images/2/25/A_Decent_Reserve.jpg)](/File:A_Decent_Reserve.jpg "A Decent Reserve icon")

A Decent Reserve

Have a maximum manpower of at least 1 million.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Have [![Manpower.png](/images/thumb/0/0c/Manpower.png/28px-Manpower.png)](/Manpower "Manpower") at least 1 million manpower

Although the achievement specifically says "maximum manpower" you actually need to have a million saved up and the maximum doesn't matter. Easiest done as [![Flag of Ottomans](/images/thumb/8/89/Ottomans.png/20px-Ottomans.png)](/Ottomans "Ottomans") [Ottomans](/Ottomans "Ottomans") or [![Flag of Muscovy](/images/thumb/4/41/Muscovy.png/20px-Muscovy.png)](/Muscovy "Muscovy") [Muscovy](/Muscovy "Muscovy") or [![Flag of Ming](/images/thumb/a/a5/Ming.png/20px-Ming.png)](/Ming "Ming") [Ming](/Ming "Ming"); the latter can demand manpower from its tributaries.

Becoming Revolutionary Empire grants extra +25% national manpower modifier.

Another way to get this achievement is to slacken recruiting standards, until the point you reach 1 million manpower.

[1.12](/1.12 "1.12")

H

[![A Hero’s Welcome icon](/images/3/35/A_Hero%E2%80%99s_Welcome.png)](/File:A_Hero%E2%80%99s_Welcome.png "A Hero’s Welcome icon")

A Hero’s Welcome

Starting as Karaman, form the Sultanate of Rum.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Karaman](/images/thumb/4/44/Karaman.png/20px-Karaman.png)](/Karaman "Karaman") [Karaman](/Karaman "Karaman")

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Rûm](/images/thumb/8/85/R%C3%BBm.png/20px-R%C3%BBm.png)](/R%C3%BBm "Rûm") [Rûm](/R%C3%BBm "Rûm")

Initial moves for a success are for the player to ally [![Flag of Mamluks](/images/thumb/c/ca/The_Mamluks.png/20px-The_Mamluks.png)](/Mamluks "Mamluks") [Mamluks](/Mamluks "Mamluks") and later when possible [![Flag of Timurids](/images/thumb/6/6a/Timurids.png/20px-Timurids.png)](/Timurids "Timurids") [Timurids](/Timurids "Timurids"). Expanding East and land locking the [![Flag of Ottomans](/images/thumb/8/89/Ottomans.png/20px-Ottomans.png)](/Ottomans "Ottomans") [Ottomans](/Ottomans "Ottomans") in the Anatolia region by quick expansion east and north will in conjunction with your powerful allies forces the Ottomans to expand into Europe, once this occurs your best chance is to wait for a good opportunity strike with your allies when the ottomans are weak. Your main objective should be to get the provinces of Kocaeli and Biga, so that in next war you can build up your galley navy and block the straits.

[![A Kaiser not just in name icon](/images/1/1a/A_Kaiser_not_just_in_name.jpg)](/File:A_Kaiser_not_just_in_name.jpg "A Kaiser not just in name icon")

A Kaiser not just in name

Form the Holy Roman Empire.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Holy Roman Empire](/images/thumb/e/ee/Holy_Roman_Empire.png/20px-Holy_Roman_Empire.png)](/Holy_Roman_Empire "Holy Roman Empire") [Holy Roman Empire](/Holy_Roman_Empire "Holy Roman Empire")

Easiest as [![Flag of Austria](/images/thumb/7/7f/Austria.png/20px-Austria.png)](/Austria "Austria") [Austria](/Austria "Austria"), playing a normal emperor game, revoking the privilegia and then either forming the holy roman empire and continuing to play; or saving before forming, and then doing Alt+F4 once the achievement has been fulfilled, thereby continuing the campaign with revoke. Can easily be combined with most of the HRE- and Austria- centric achievements.

H

[![Anglophile icon](/images/1/19/Anglophile.png)](/File:Anglophile.png "Anglophile icon")

[Anglophile](/Anglophile "Anglophile")

Complete all English and British missions.

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World")
*   [![Culture icon.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Culture_icon.png/28px-Culture_icon.png)](/Culture "Culture") Has a culture out of the British group.

*   [![Mission.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Mission.png/24px-Mission.png)](/Missions "Missions") Complete one of the following mission trees:
    *   [![Rule Britannia.png](/images/thumb/5/5a/Rule_Britannia.png/28px-Rule_Britannia.png)](/Rule_Britannia "Rule Britannia") [British missions from the Rule Britannia DLC](/British_missions_without_domination "British missions without domination").
    *   [![Domination.png](/images/thumb/3/3d/Domination.png/28px-Domination.png)](/Domination "Domination") [English/British missions from the Domination DLC](/English_missions "English missions").
    *    [![Flag of Angevin Kingdom](/images/thumb/b/be/Angevin_Kingdom.png/20px-Angevin_Kingdom.png)](/Angevin_Kingdom "Angevin Kingdom")[Angevin missions from the Domination DLC](/Angevin_missions "Angevin missions").

*   Strategies for Rule Britannia missions:
    *   Provided you are able to force France into a PU, the missions are fairly easy to complete apart from being elected Emperor of the HRE - you will either need to convert to Protestant and win the league wars, or convert to Anglican or Reformed and hope the Peace of Westphalia occurs - which can be very difficult. You may want to stay out of the league wars and rent out your troops to the losing side so you can keep the war going.
    *   Alternatively, you can just disband the HRE while remaining any religion.

*   [![Rule Britannia.png](/images/thumb/5/5a/Rule_Britannia.png/28px-Rule_Britannia.png)](/Rule_Britannia "Rule Britannia") _or_ [![Domination.png](/images/thumb/3/3d/Domination.png/28px-Domination.png)](/Domination "Domination")

[![Assembly Instructions Needed icon](/images/a/a2/Assembly_Instructions_Needed.png)](/File:Assembly_Instructions_Needed.png "Assembly Instructions Needed icon")

Assembly Instructions Needed

Form Scandinavia and revoke the privilegia of the Holy Roman Empire while being the Emperor.

One of the following:

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Scandinavia](/images/thumb/d/db/Scandinavia.png/20px-Scandinavia.png)](/Scandinavia "Scandinavia") [Scandinavia](/Scandinavia "Scandinavia") and the [![Imperial authority.png](/images/thumb/4/46/Imperial_authority.png/28px-Imperial_authority.png)](/Imperial_authority "Imperial authority") emperor of the [HRE](/HRE "HRE") and has passed the imperial reform _“Revoke The Privilegia”_
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is the [![Flag of Holy Roman Empire](/images/thumb/e/ee/Holy_Roman_Empire.png/20px-Holy_Roman_Empire.png)](/Holy_Roman_Empire "Holy Roman Empire") [Holy Roman Empire](/Holy_Roman_Empire "Holy Roman Empire") and was [![Flag of Scandinavia](/images/thumb/d/db/Scandinavia.png/20px-Scandinavia.png)](/Scandinavia "Scandinavia") [Scandinavia](/Scandinavia "Scandinavia") before

Easy to do as [![Flag of Denmark](/images/thumb/6/69/Denmark.png/20px-Denmark.png)](/Denmark "Denmark") [Denmark](/Denmark "Denmark"). Restart until [![Flag of Burgundy](/images/thumb/b/b0/Burgundy.png/20px-Burgundy.png)](/Burgundy "Burgundy") [Burgundy](/Burgundy "Burgundy") is friendly, hire diplomatic reputation advisor, take religious diplomats estate privilege, and insult their rival. This should guarantee alliance and marriage for potential BI. Then ally and max relations with 3-4 electors, and you should become the emperor. Then the standard HRE approach of killing the Reformation. Join the HRE for a one-time IA boost. Ideas: Diplomatic, Religious, Influence. Diplomatic reputation for passing reforms and inheriting thrones and Religious to convert centers of reformation. Emperor [![Flag of Denmark](/images/thumb/6/69/Denmark.png/20px-Denmark.png)](/Denmark "Denmark") [Denmark](/Denmark "Denmark") also has an easy time killing Swedish pretender rebels.

*    [![Flag of Yolngu](/images/thumb/c/c0/Yolngu.png/20px-Yolngu.png)](/Yolngu "Yolngu") [Yolngu](/Yolngu "Yolngu")
*    [![Flag of Yanuwa](/images/thumb/f/f8/Yanuwa.png/20px-Yanuwa.png)](/Yanuwa "Yanuwa") [Yanuwa](/Yanuwa "Yanuwa")
*    [![Flag of Awngthim](/images/thumb/8/8a/Awngthim.png/20px-Awngthim.png)](/Awngthim "Awngthim") [Awngthim](/Awngthim "Awngthim")
*    [![Flag of Kamilaroi](/images/thumb/3/38/Kamilaroi.png/20px-Kamilaroi.png)](/Kamilaroi "Kamilaroi") [Kamilaroi](/Kamilaroi "Kamilaroi")
*    [![Flag of Mianjin](/images/thumb/a/a9/Mianjin.png/20px-Mianjin.png)](/Mianjin "Mianjin") [Mianjin](/Mianjin "Mianjin")
*    [![Flag of Eora](/images/thumb/a/a7/Eora.png/20px-Eora.png)](/Eora "Eora") [Eora](/Eora "Eora")
*    [![Flag of Kulin](/images/thumb/b/be/Kulin.png/20px-Kulin.png)](/Kulin "Kulin") [Kulin](/Kulin "Kulin")
*    [![Flag of Kaurna](/images/thumb/e/e3/Kaurna.png/20px-Kaurna.png)](/Kaurna "Kaurna") [Kaurna](/Kaurna "Kaurna")
*    [![Flag of Palawa](/images/thumb/2/2e/Palawa.png/20px-Palawa.png)](/Palawa "Palawa") [Palawa](/Palawa "Palawa")
*    [![Flag of Wurundjeri](/images/thumb/0/06/Wurundjeri.png/20px-Wurundjeri.png)](/Wurundjeri "Wurundjeri") [Wurundjeri](/Wurundjeri "Wurundjeri")
*    [![Flag of Nyoongah](/images/thumb/d/d4/Nyoongah.png/20px-Nyoongah.png)](/Nyoongah "Nyoongah") [Nyoongah](/Nyoongah "Nyoongah")
*    [![Flag of Malgana](/images/thumb/2/28/Malgana.png/20px-Malgana.png)](/Malgana "Malgana") [Malgana](/Malgana "Malgana")

Forming a federation will make the achievement harder as your nation tag will change in the process. One possible way to circumvent this is becoming a steppe horde through goverment reforms, which changes the technology group to [![Nomadic technology group](/images/thumb/b/b8/Nomadic.png/28px-Nomadic.png)](/Technology_group "Nomadic technology group") nomadic and allows you to form [![Flag of Australia](/images/thumb/4/43/Australia.png/20px-Australia.png)](/Australia "Australia") [Australia](/Australia "Australia").

Back in Control

Form Yuan and be the only nation holding land in China.

*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") All colonized provinces in the [China super-region](/China_(super-region) "China (super-region)") owned by Yuan.

Taiwan is only required if it is colonized. Forming [![Flag of Mongol Empire](/images/thumb/e/e4/Mongol_Empire.png/20px-Mongol_Empire.png)](/Mongol_Empire "Mongol Empire") [Mongol Empire](/Mongol_Empire "Mongol Empire") will prevent the achievement.

If you choose to play as either Silesian minor, forming [![Flag of Silesia](/images/thumb/f/f7/Silesia.png/20px-Silesia.png)](/Silesia "Silesia") [Silesia](/Silesia "Silesia"), which does not exist at game start, will _not_ prevent you from getting the achievement.

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Livonian Order](/images/thumb/8/81/Livonian_Order.png/20px-Livonian_Order.png)](/Livonian_Order "Livonian Order") [Livonian Order](/Livonian_Order "Livonian Order") or [![Flag of Teutonic Order](/images/thumb/2/2f/Teutonic_Order.png/20px-Teutonic_Order.png)](/Teutonic_Order "Teutonic Order") [Teutonic Order](/Teutonic_Order "Teutonic Order")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own and core all fully colonized provinces in the [Pontic Steppe](/Pontic_Steppe "Pontic Steppe"), [Russia](/Russia_(region) "Russia (region)"), and [Ural](/Ural "Ural") regions.
*   [![Catholicism](/images/thumb/3/39/Catholic.png/28px-Catholic.png)](/Catholic "Catholic") All these provinces are Catholic

Expand

[![Baltic Crusader map.png](/images/thumb/8/81/Baltic_Crusader_map.png/140px-Baltic_Crusader_map.png)](/File:Baltic_Crusader_map.png)

[](/File:Baltic_Crusader_map.png "Enlarge")

Easiest as Teutonic Order; ally Muscovy, Austria and Bohemia and DOW Poland ASAP, or else Poland will form a PU with Lithuania. Restarting until Poland declines the PU is also a viable strategy.

Dracula's Revenge

Start as Wallachia or Moldavia, form Romania and own or have a subject own all of the Balkans.

Primary culture is _Romanian_

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Romania](/images/thumb/8/8f/Romania.png/20px-Romania.png)](/Romania "Romania") [Romania](/Romania "Romania")
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") All provinces in the [Balkans](/Balkans "Balkans") region are owned by [![Flag of Romania](/images/thumb/8/8f/Romania.png/20px-Romania.png)](/Romania "Romania") [Romania](/Romania "Romania") _or_ its non-tributary [subjects](/Subjects "Subjects").

Possible starts are [![Flag of Moldavia](/images/thumb/5/59/Moldavia.png/20px-Moldavia.png)](/Moldavia "Moldavia") [Moldavia](/Moldavia "Moldavia") and [![Flag of Wallachia](/images/thumb/1/1a/Wallachia.png/20px-Wallachia.png)](/Wallachia "Wallachia") [Wallachia](/Wallachia "Wallachia")

[1.9](/1.9 "1.9")

H

[![Emperor of Hindustan icon](/images/e/ea/Emperor_of_Hindustan.png)](/File:Emperor_of_Hindustan.png "Emperor of Hindustan icon")

Emperor of Hindustan

Starting as Delhi, Restore their Empire's borders.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Delhi](/images/thumb/d/d5/Delhi.png/20px-Delhi.png)](/Delhi "Delhi") [Delhi](/Delhi "Delhi")

[![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") The following provinces are owned by the country _or_ its non-tributary [subjects](/Subjects "Subjects"):

Expand

[![Emperor of Hindustan map.png](/images/thumb/d/d1/Emperor_of_Hindustan_map.png/140px-Emperor_of_Hindustan_map.png)](/File:Emperor_of_Hindustan_map.png)

[](/File:Emperor_of_Hindustan_map.png "Enlarge")

Avoid the event at the start of the game that attempts to free Sirhind by using the 'place relative on throne' subject interaction right away. To make them loyal you can do development in their land, remember that it costs 0 dip to integrate them as you already start with cores. Focus on expanding south and northwest to begin the game.

Alternatively, get lots of allies and let the event fire. Sirhind will attack you without any allies such as Jaunpur.

Provinces owned by vassals and other non-tributary subjects of the player's country will count for the achievement.

Forming another nation, such as [![Flag of Hindustan](/images/thumb/3/3e/Hindustan.png/20px-Hindustan.png)](/Hindustan "Hindustan") [Hindustan](/Hindustan "Hindustan") will not lock the achievement. On the flip side, forming Delhi will not make you eligible for the achievement.

[![Everything's Coming Up Mulhouse icon](/images/0/0a/Everything%27s_Coming_Up_Mulhouse.png)](/File:Everything%27s_Coming_Up_Mulhouse.png "Everything's Coming Up Mulhouse icon")

Everything's Coming Up Mulhouse

Starting as Mulhouse, become Emperor of the HRE and completely decentralize the Empire.

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Mulhouse](/images/thumb/3/30/Mulhouse.png/20px-Mulhouse.png)](/Mulhouse "Mulhouse") [Mulhouse](/Mulhouse "Mulhouse")
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World")

*   [![Imperial authority.png](/images/thumb/4/46/Imperial_authority.png/28px-Imperial_authority.png)](/Imperial_authority "Imperial authority") Is the emperor of the [Holy Roman Empire](/Holy_Roman_Empire "Holy Roman Empire")
*   Has enacted the reform Reichskrieg

Mulhouse starts as a republic, and needs to become a monarchy to be able to become the Holy Roman Emperor. Forming another nation (like [![Flag of Swabia](/images/thumb/a/a1/Swabia.png/20px-Swabia.png)](/Swabia "Swabia") [Swabia](/Swabia "Swabia")) does not prevent the player from getting the achievement.

Forever Golden

Complete the Spanish Mission Tree.

[![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World")

*   [![Mission.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Mission.png/24px-Mission.png)](/Missions "Missions") Complete one of the following mission trees:
    *   [![Golden Century.png](/images/thumb/b/bb/Golden_Century.png/28px-Golden_Century.png)](/Golden_Century "Golden Century") [Spanish missions from the Golden Century DLC](/Spanish_missions_without_domination "Spanish missions without domination").
    *   [![Domination.png](/images/thumb/3/3d/Domination.png/28px-Domination.png)](/Domination "Domination") [Castilian/Spanish missions from the Domination DLC](/Castilian_missions "Castilian missions").
    *   [![Domination.png](/images/thumb/3/3d/Domination.png/28px-Domination.png)](/Domination "Domination") [Aragonese missions from the Domination DLC](/Aragonese_missions "Aragonese missions") _and_ the lower half of the [Castilian missions](/Castilian_missions "Castilian missions") which [![Flag of Aragon](/images/thumb/6/61/Aragon.png/20px-Aragon.png)](/Aragon "Aragon") [Aragon](/Aragon "Aragon") gets upon forming [![Flag of Spain](/images/thumb/5/58/Spain.png/20px-Spain.png)](/Spain "Spain") [Spain](/Spain "Spain").

The achievement _cannot_ be completed with the Aragonese missions from the Golden Century DLC. If the Golden Century, but not the Domination DLC is active, Spain must be formed by a country which does _not_ have Aragonese _nor_ Catalan as primary culture, because these cultures give Aragonese missions instead of Spanish missions(culture converting after formation does not change your missions).

*   [![Golden Century.png](/images/thumb/b/bb/Golden_Century.png/28px-Golden_Century.png)](/Golden_Century "Golden Century") _or_ [![Domination.png](/images/thumb/3/3d/Domination.png/28px-Domination.png)](/Domination "Domination")
