[![Good King René icon](/images/7/7b/Good_King_Ren%C3%A9.png)](/File:Good_King_Ren%C3%A9.png "Good King René icon")

Good King René

Start as Provence, form the Kingdom of Jerusalem.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Provence](/images/thumb/b/bd/Provence.png/20px-Provence.png)](/Provence "Provence") [Provence](/Provence "Provence")

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Jerusalem](/images/thumb/e/ef/Jerusalem.png/20px-Jerusalem.png)](/Jerusalem "Jerusalem") [Jerusalem](/Jerusalem "Jerusalem")

Note that the Kingdom of Jerusalem cannot be formed after Age of Reformation ends.

[1.23](/1.23 "1.23")

H

[![Guarantor of Peace icon](/images/7/71/Guarantor_of_Peace.png)](/File:Guarantor_of_Peace.png "Guarantor of Peace icon")

Guarantor of Peace

Guarantee the Independence of France, The Ottoman Empire and Russia.

*   [![Diplomatic relations.png](/images/thumb/5/58/Diplomatic_relations.png/28px-Diplomatic_relations.png)](/Diplomatic_relations "Diplomatic relations") [Guarantee the independence](/Diplomacy#Proclaim_guarantee "Diplomacy") of:
    *    [![Flag of France](/images/thumb/d/de/France.png/20px-France.png)](/France "France") [France](/France "France")
    *    [![Flag of Ottomans](/images/thumb/8/89/Ottomans.png/20px-Ottomans.png)](/Ottomans "Ottomans") [Ottomans](/Ottomans "Ottomans")
    *    [![Flag of Russia](/images/thumb/e/ee/Russia.png/20px-Russia.png)](/Russia "Russia") [Russia](/Russia "Russia")

You can only guarantee a country if you are larger than it. Can be achieved easily after unifying the HRE.

[1.9](/1.9 "1.9")

H

[![Holy Horder icon](/images/7/7d/Holy_Horder.png)](/File:Holy_Horder.png "Holy Horder icon")

Holy Horder

Starting as the Teutonic Order, form the Mongol Empire while have the Holy Horde government reform enacted.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Teutonic Order](/images/thumb/2/2f/Teutonic_Order.png/20px-Teutonic_Order.png)](/Teutonic_Order "Teutonic Order") [Teutonic Order](/Teutonic_Order "Teutonic Order")

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is the [![Flag of Mongol Empire](/images/thumb/e/e4/Mongol_Empire.png/20px-Mongol_Empire.png)](/Mongol_Empire "Mongol Empire") [Mongol Empire](/Mongol_Empire "Mongol Empire")
*   [![Government theocracy.png](/images/thumb/8/81/Government_theocracy.png/28px-Government_theocracy.png)](/Theocracy "Theocracy") Has enacted the [Holy Horde](/Holy_Horde "Holy Horde") government reform

To form the [![Flag of Mongol Empire](/images/thumb/e/e4/Mongol_Empire.png/20px-Mongol_Empire.png)](/Mongol_Empire "Mongol Empire") [Mongol Empire](/Mongol_Empire "Mongol Empire") as the [![Flag of Teutonic Order](/images/thumb/2/2f/Teutonic_Order.png/20px-Teutonic_Order.png)](/Teutonic_Order "Teutonic Order") [Teutonic Order](/Teutonic_Order "Teutonic Order") you need to choose the crusader path of missions after completing [Defeat Poland](/Teutonic_missions#Defeat_Poland "Teutonic missions"), this will unlock the mission [Crusaders of the Steppes](/Teutonic_missions#Crusaders_of_the_Steppes "Teutonic missions") which allows forming the [![Flag of Mongol Empire](/images/thumb/e/e4/Mongol_Empire.png/20px-Mongol_Empire.png)](/Mongol_Empire "Mongol Empire") [Mongol Empire](/Mongol_Empire "Mongol Empire") due to the unique government reform.

[![Lions of the North.png](/images/thumb/c/cd/Lions_of_the_North.png/28px-Lions_of_the_North.png)](/Lions_of_the_North "Lions of the North")

[1.34](/1.34 "1.34")

H

[![Holy Trinity icon](/images/f/fa/Holy_Trinity.png)](/File:Holy_Trinity.png "Holy Trinity icon")

[Holy Trinity](/Holy_Trinity "Holy Trinity")

As the Papacy, own Jerusalem and have Livonian Order, Teutonic Order and The Knights as Marches.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of The Papal State](/images/thumb/7/71/The_Papal_State.png/20px-The_Papal_State.png)](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State") [The Papal State](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") is [![Flag of The Papal State](/images/thumb/7/71/The_Papal_State.png/20px-The_Papal_State.png)](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State") [The Papal State](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own and core Jerusalem.
*   [![March icon.png](/images/thumb/1/1d/March_icon.png/28px-March_icon.png)](/March "March") Have [![Flag of Livonian Order](/images/thumb/8/81/Livonian_Order.png/20px-Livonian_Order.png)](/Livonian_Order "Livonian Order") [Livonian Order](/Livonian_Order "Livonian Order"), [![Flag of Teutonic Order](/images/thumb/2/2f/Teutonic_Order.png/20px-Teutonic_Order.png)](/Teutonic_Order "Teutonic Order") [Teutonic Order](/Teutonic_Order "Teutonic Order") and [![Flag of The Knights](/images/thumb/8/84/The_Knights.png/20px-The_Knights.png)](/The_Knights "The Knights") [The Knights](/The_Knights "The Knights") as marches.

This achievement has several common pitfalls which would make it all but impossible to complete it if they happen. The strategy page for this achievement has [a section which explains them](/Holy_Trinity#Common_pitfalls_which_must_be_avoided "Holy Trinity") and some ways to get out of these situations. The player is advised to read that before attempting the achievement.

[![Art of War.png](/images/thumb/0/0f/Art_of_War.png/28px-Art_of_War.png)](/Art_of_War "Art of War")

[1.9](/1.9 "1.9")

H

[![I don't like sand icon](/images/a/a7/I_don%27t_like_sand.png)](/File:I_don%27t_like_sand.png "I don't like sand icon")

I don't like sand

Have the most development while owning no province with terrain other than desert or coastal desert.

[![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World")

*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") All provinces are either [![Combat terrain desert.png](/images/thumb/3/33/Combat_terrain_desert.png/72px-Combat_terrain_desert.png)](/File:Combat_terrain_desert.png) desert or [![Combat terrain coastal desert.png](/images/thumb/a/a4/Combat_terrain_coastal_desert.png/72px-Combat_terrain_coastal_desert.png)](/File:Combat_terrain_coastal_desert.png) coastal desert
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") No other country has a higher [![Development.png](/images/thumb/a/a4/Development.png/28px-Development.png)](/Development "Development") development than this country

Expand

[![](/images/thumb/f/fa/I_dont_like_sand_map.png/300px-I_dont_like_sand_map.png)](/File:I_dont_like_sand_map.png)

[](/File:I_dont_like_sand_map.png "Enlarge")

All desert and coastal desert provinces

Easiest as [![Flag of Ajuuraan](/images/thumb/5/52/Ajuuraan.png/20px-Ajuuraan.png)](/Ajuuraan "Ajuuraan") [Ajuuraan](/Ajuuraan "Ajuuraan"), because of their national ideas and the "Hydraulic Rights" estate privilege (which reduces the additional cost from developing deserts and coastal desert by half), that is unlocked through a mission in [![Origins.png](/images/thumb/8/8e/Origins.png/28px-Origins.png)](/Origins "Origins") Origins DLC.

[1.32](/1.32 "1.32")

H

[![It's All Greek To Me icon](/images/7/73/It%27s_All_Greek_To_Me.png)](/File:It%27s_All_Greek_To_Me.png "It's All Greek To Me icon")

It's All Greek To Me

Form Greece and own and have cores on Zeta, Thatta, Lamba, and Roh.

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Greece](/images/thumb/d/d8/Greece.png/20px-Greece.png)](/Greece "Greece") [Greece](/Greece "Greece")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own the core provinces of Zeta (138), Thatta (504), Roh (578), and Lamba (4104)

Expand

[![It's All Greek To Me map.png](/images/thumb/5/5a/It%27s_All_Greek_To_Me_map.png/140px-It%27s_All_Greek_To_Me_map.png)](/File:It%27s_All_Greek_To_Me_map.png)

[](/File:It%27s_All_Greek_To_Me_map.png "Enlarge")

*   Forming Greece requires Greek primary culture. Zeta begins held by [![Flag of Serbia](/images/thumb/7/76/Serbia.png/20px-Serbia.png)](/Serbia "Serbia") [Serbia](/Serbia "Serbia"), Thatta held by [![Flag of Sindh](/images/thumb/3/39/Sindh.png/20px-Sindh.png)](/Sindh "Sindh") [Sindh](/Sindh "Sindh"), Roh held by [![Flag of Afghanistan](/images/thumb/7/7d/Afghanistan.png/20px-Afghanistan.png)](/Afghanistan "Afghanistan") [Afghanistan](/Afghanistan "Afghanistan"), and Lamba uncolonized in Central Africa.
*   Alternatively, you can conquer Byzantium and wait for Greek cores to form after the Greek Separatism event fires (requires Admin Tech 20). Release Greece as a vassal and feed him the required provinces. Once they are cored, diplomatically annex Greece and release them again, but chose to play as Greece this time. Note that since Thatta is in a [Trade Company](/Trade_Company "Trade Company") region you must own the province yourself to state and fully core it before giving it to Greece, otherwise they will lose their territorial core upon annexing.

[1.22](/1.22 "1.22")

H

[![Keep the Flame Burning icon](/images/9/9c/Keep_the_Flame_Burning.jpg)](/File:Keep_the_Flame_Burning.jpg "Keep the Flame Burning icon")

Keep the Flame Burning

As a Zoroastrian nation, own all Religious Centers and Monument Baku Ateshgah on tier 3.

*   [![Zoroastrianism.png](/images/thumb/2/25/Zoroastrianism.png/28px-Zoroastrianism.png)](/Zoroastrian "Zoroastrian") Religion is Zoroastrian
*   [![Great project fire temple of ateshgah.png](/images/thumb/6/64/Great_project_fire_temple_of_ateshgah.png/28px-Great_project_fire_temple_of_ateshgah.png)](/File:Great_project_fire_temple_of_ateshgah.png) [Baku Ateshgah](/Great_project#Baku_Ateshgah "Great project") is tier 3
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") The following provinces are owned and follow the [![Zoroastrianism.png](/images/thumb/2/25/Zoroastrianism.png/28px-Zoroastrianism.png)](/Zoroastrian "Zoroastrian") Zoroastrian faith:
    *   Larestan (2223)
    *   Daman (4430)
    *   Khiva (441)
    *   Sabzevar (2235)
    *   Shirvan (421)

Easiest as [![Flag of Timurids](/images/thumb/6/6a/Timurids.png/20px-Timurids.png)](/Timurids "Timurids") [Timurids](/Timurids "Timurids"): play a standard game while you integrate your vassals, then convert via rebels.

Note that this achievement cannot be combined with Rekindling the Flames because it cannot be earned as a Custom Nation, which is required for Rekindling the Flames.

[![Leviathan.png](/images/thumb/0/0a/Leviathan.png/28px-Leviathan.png)](/Leviathan "Leviathan")

*    [![Flag of The Knights](/images/thumb/8/84/The_Knights.png/20px-The_Knights.png)](/The_Knights "The Knights") [The Knights](/The_Knights "The Knights")

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Jerusalem](/images/thumb/e/ef/Jerusalem.png/20px-Jerusalem.png)](/Jerusalem "Jerusalem") [Jerusalem](/Jerusalem "Jerusalem")

Completing the mission [Jerusalem!](/Crusader_missions#Jerusalem.21 "Crusader missions") allows forming Jerusalem after the age of reformation.

[Kinslayer](/Kinslayer "Kinslayer")

As Tver, Yaroslavl, Ryazan, Beloozero, Rostov or Odoyev, eliminate all other Rurikovich nations without changing your ruling dynasty.

*    [![Flag of Ryazan](/images/thumb/7/7b/Ryazan.png/20px-Ryazan.png)](/Ryazan "Ryazan") [Ryazan](/Ryazan "Ryazan")

*    [![Flag of Yaroslavl](/images/thumb/b/b9/Yaroslavl.png/20px-Yaroslavl.png)](/Yaroslavl "Yaroslavl") [Yaroslavl](/Yaroslavl "Yaroslavl")
*    [![Flag of Beloozero](/images/thumb/a/a9/Beloozero.png/20px-Beloozero.png)](/Beloozero "Beloozero") [Beloozero](/Beloozero "Beloozero")
*    [![Flag of Rostov](/images/thumb/3/38/Rostov.png/20px-Rostov.png)](/Rostov "Rostov") [Rostov](/Rostov "Rostov")

This country and its junior partners are the only countries with the Rurikovich dynasty

Knights of the Caribbean

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of The Knights](/images/thumb/8/84/The_Knights.png/20px-The_Knights.png)](/The_Knights "The Knights") [The Knights](/The_Knights "The Knights")

Expand[![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Owns the following core provinces:

*   Rhodes (320)
*   Cyprus (321)
*   Crete (163)
*   Naxos (164)
*   Chios (2348)
*   Euboea (3003)
*   Lesbos (4700)
*   Cephalonia (4698)
*   Corfu (142)
*   Syracuse (2982)
*   Messina (124)
*   Palermo (125)
*   Girgenti (4737)
*   Trapani (4736)
*   Djerba (2954)
*   Malta (126)
*   Sassari (127)
*   Corsica (1247)
*   Menorca (4559)
*   Ibiza (4560)
*   Mallorca (333)
*   Venezia (112)
*   Arborea (4735)
*   Cagliari (2986)

ExpandMap of the Mediterranean provinces:

Luck of the Irish

Own and have cores on the British Isles as an Irish nation.

[![Primary culture.png](/images/thumb/e/e1/Primary_culture.png/28px-Primary_culture.png)](/Primary_culture "Primary culture") Primary culture is _Irish_

[![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own and core all provinces of the [Britain](/European_regions#British_Isles "European regions") region.

Possible starts are [![Flag of Clanricarde](/images/thumb/5/55/Clanricarde.png/20px-Clanricarde.png)](/Clanricarde "Clanricarde") [Clanricarde](/Clanricarde "Clanricarde"), [![Flag of Desmond](/images/thumb/5/5e/Desmond.png/20px-Desmond.png)](/Desmond "Desmond") [Desmond](/Desmond "Desmond"), [![Flag of Kildare](/images/thumb/7/7a/Kildare.png/20px-Kildare.png)](/Kildare "Kildare") [Kildare](/Kildare "Kildare"), [![Flag of Leinster](/images/thumb/4/49/Leinster.png/20px-Leinster.png)](/Leinster "Leinster") [Leinster](/Leinster "Leinster"), [![Flag of Munster](/images/thumb/e/e5/Munster.png/20px-Munster.png)](/Munster "Munster") [Munster](/Munster "Munster"), [![Flag of Offaly](/images/thumb/3/3a/Offaly.png/20px-Offaly.png)](/Offaly "Offaly") [Offaly](/Offaly "Offaly"), [![Flag of Ormond](/images/thumb/f/fd/Ormond.png/20px-Ormond.png)](/Ormond "Ormond") [Ormond](/Ormond "Ormond"), [![Flag of Sligo](/images/thumb/2/28/Sligo.png/20px-Sligo.png)](/Sligo "Sligo") [Sligo](/Sligo "Sligo"), [![Flag of Thomond](/images/thumb/d/db/Thomond.png/20px-Thomond.png)](/Thomond "Thomond") [Thomond](/Thomond "Thomond"), [![Flag of Tyrconnell](/images/thumb/e/e9/Tyrconnell.png/20px-Tyrconnell.png)](/Tyrconnell "Tyrconnell") [Tyrconnell](/Tyrconnell "Tyrconnell"), [![Flag of Tyrone](/images/thumb/c/c7/Tyrone.png/20px-Tyrone.png)](/Tyrone "Tyrone") [Tyrone](/Tyrone "Tyrone") and [![Flag of Ulster](/images/thumb/b/b9/Ulster.png/20px-Ulster.png)](/Ulster "Ulster") [Ulster](/Ulster "Ulster").

 [![Flag of Desmond](/images/thumb/5/5e/Desmond.png/20px-Desmond.png)](/Desmond "Desmond") [Desmond](/Desmond "Desmond") is a good choice due to early military ideas. Rushing to conquer the rest of the Irish OPMs and securing an alliance with [![Flag of Scotland](/images/thumb/2/27/Scotland.png/20px-Scotland.png)](/Scotland "Scotland") [Scotland](/Scotland "Scotland") can deter [![Flag of England](/images/thumb/2/21/England.png/20px-England.png)](/England "England") [England](/England "England") until the time is right.

[![Mare Nostrum icon](/images/e/e8/Mare_Nostrum.jpg)](/File:Mare_Nostrum.jpg "Mare Nostrum icon")

Mare Nostrum

Restore the Roman Empire and own the entire Mediterranean and Black Sea coast lines.

[![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") Not playing as [![Flag of The Papal State](/images/thumb/7/71/The_Papal_State.png/20px-The_Papal_State.png)](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State") [The Papal State](/The_Papal_State "The Papal State")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Roman Empire](/images/thumb/4/4e/Roman_Empire.png/20px-Roman_Empire.png)](/Roman_Empire "Roman Empire") [Roman Empire](/Roman_Empire "Roman Empire")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own the following provinces:

Expand

[![Requirements Mare Nostrum.png](/images/thumb/3/3d/Requirements_Mare_Nostrum.png/140px-Requirements_Mare_Nostrum.png)](/File:Requirements_Mare_Nostrum.png)

[](/File:Requirements_Mare_Nostrum.png "Enlarge")

Easiest to do as the [![Flag of Ottomans](/images/thumb/8/89/Ottomans.png/20px-Ottomans.png)](/Ottomans "Ottomans") [Ottomans](/Ottomans "Ottomans") after converting to Christianity. Alternatively, with [![Golden Century.png](/images/thumb/b/bb/Golden_Century.png/28px-Golden_Century.png)](/Golden_Century "Golden Century") Golden Century, this is relatively easy as [![Flag of Aragon](/images/thumb/6/61/Aragon.png/20px-Aragon.png)](/Aragon "Aragon") [Aragon](/Aragon "Aragon") as their mission tree gives you claims on most of the required territory.

[![Mass Production icon](/images/8/88/Mass_Production.png)](/File:Mass_Production.png "Mass Production icon")

Mass Production

Starting as Odoyev, own one of every manufactory.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Odoyev](/images/thumb/f/f4/Odoyev.png/20px-Odoyev.png)](/Odoyev "Odoyev") [Odoyev](/Odoyev "Odoyev")

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Own at least one [manufactory](/Buildings#Manufactories "Buildings") of each type

*   The new manufactories (Ramparts, Soldier's Households, Impressment Offices, State House) are also necessary
*   With the [![Rule Britannia.png](/images/thumb/5/5a/Rule_Britannia.png/28px-Rule_Britannia.png)](/Rule_Britannia "Rule Britannia") Rule Britannia DLC a furnace is also necessary.
*   Building the manufactories isn't very hard. The hard part is surviving long enough to get to the required technology (admin tech 16 without [![Rule Britannia.png](/images/thumb/5/5a/Rule_Britannia.png/28px-Rule_Britannia.png)](/Rule_Britannia "Rule Britannia") Rule Britannia and till the Enlightenment with the DLC) as well as getting provinces with the correct trade goods.
*   Forming [![Flag of Ruthenia](/images/thumb/e/e2/Ruthenia.png/20px-Ruthenia.png)](/Ruthenia "Ruthenia") [Ruthenia](/Ruthenia "Ruthenia") through your missions does not prevent the player from getting the achievement.

[1.22](/1.22 "1.22")

H

[![Master of India icon](/images/e/e0/Master_of_India.jpg)](/File:Master_of_India.jpg "Master of India icon")

Master of India

Own and have cores on all of India as a European nation.

[![Capital.png](/images/thumb/6/6e/Capital.png/28px-Capital.png)](/Capital "Capital") Capital is in Europe

[![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own or have a non-tributary subject own all provinces in the [Indian sub-continent](/India_(sub-continent) "India (sub-continent)") (regions Deccan, Coromandel, Bengal, Hindustan and Western India).

It's _not_ required anymore for the player to directly own all provinces inside the Indian sub-continent. Vassals and other direct subjects count as long as they are not tributaries. Coring the provinces is also not longer required.

The capital does not need to remain in Europe. Edirne is European, so the [Ottomans](/Ottomans "Ottomans") are eligible and have the best shot at a quick land rush into India.

Mewar Never Changes

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World")

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Has completed all [![Mission.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Mission.png/24px-Mission.png)](/Missions "Missions") [Mewari missions](/Mewari_missions "Mewari missions")

This achievement is only visible if the country has [![Mission.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Mission.png/24px-Mission.png)](/Missions "Missions") [Mewari missions](/Mewari_missions "Mewari missions"), but it is not required to start as [![Flag of Mewar](/images/thumb/7/7d/Mewar.png/20px-Mewar.png)](/Mewar "Mewar") [Mewar](/Mewar "Mewar"). It is also possible to start as any non [end-game tag](/End-game_tag "End-game tag") and then form [![Flag of Rajputana](/images/thumb/e/e8/Rajputana.png/20px-Rajputana.png)](/Rajputana "Rajputana") [Rajputana](/Rajputana "Rajputana") to get these missions.

[1.30](/1.30 "1.30")

H

[![One nation to rule them all icon](/images/7/7f/One_nation_to_rule_them_all.png)](/File:One_nation_to_rule_them_all.png "One nation to rule them all icon")

One nation to rule them all

As Saruhan, have at least 9 loyal vassals with at least 100 development each.

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Saruhan](/images/thumb/6/69/Saruhan.png/20px-Saruhan.png)](/Saruhan "Saruhan") [Saruhan](/Saruhan "Saruhan")
*   9 countries fulfill the following conditions:
    *   is a [![Vassal.png](/images/thumb/4/47/Vassal.png/28px-Vassal.png)](/Vassal "Vassal") vassal of [![Flag of Saruhan](/images/thumb/6/69/Saruhan.png/20px-Saruhan.png)](/Saruhan "Saruhan") [Saruhan](/Saruhan "Saruhan")
    *   has less than [![Liberty desire.png](/images/thumb/f/fd/Liberty_desire.png/28px-Liberty_desire.png)](/Liberty_desire "Liberty desire") **50%** liberty desire
    *   has at least [![Development.png](/images/thumb/a/a4/Development.png/28px-Development.png)](/Development "Development") **100** development

 [![Flag of Saruhan](/images/thumb/6/69/Saruhan.png/20px-Saruhan.png)](/Saruhan "Saruhan") [Saruhan](/Saruhan "Saruhan")'s core starts under the control of the [![Flag of Ottomans](/images/thumb/8/89/Ottomans.png/20px-Ottomans.png)](/Ottomans "Ottomans") [Ottomans](/Ottomans "Ottomans"). Suggested strategy: expand rapidly as you normally would with the Ottomans until you have ~1200 development. Then, plan to release-and-play as Saruhan, taking most of Otto's lands. To do this, you will need to release Saruhan as vassal, wait 10 years, start to annex (to designate cores), feed it land, finalize annexation, and then release-and-play. You can cheese the release-and-play by feeding past the point of loyalty and then applying all available [annexation cost](/Vassal#Cost "Vassal") reductions (Acquire Subjects mission, Influence idea, Amirs privilege, as well as any possible Policies). Make sure you wait until the last day of the month to do this, or else annexation progress will drop and you will be unable to proceed. As long as your annexation progress is above 100 on the month tick, it won't matter if liberty desire is over 50%.

Once you have reannexed, you will be able to release-and-play. Ideally you will then own almost all Ottoman lands, making independence relatively easy to pursue. From there, you need to obtain 9 loyal vassals (NOT marches, NOT client states) with 100+ development. Rather than directly subjugating enemies to meet the vassal count, it is suggested that the player conquer and then [release vassals](/Vassal#Releasing_a_nation "Vassal"); this avoids the forced vassalization malus. To help reduce liberty desire and thus total development needed, choose the relevant policies, and be sure to get the [Splendor abilities in the Age of Revolutions](/Ages#Abilities_4 "Ages") (Anti-Revolutionary Zeal + Loyal Subjects). Upon release, you will no longer have the Ottoman government form, and should choose [Iqta](/Monarchy#Iqta "Monarchy"). Then on your goverment tab choose Lenient Taxation, which provides another Liberty Desire reduction.

Note that during the feeding of Saruhan and following your transition to playing as them, the Ottomans will likely be severely weakened and thus open to attack. Keep this in mind, perhaps securing treaties in advance or locking in allies (though too many allies for Otto will make subsequent independence harder). Ideally you will be able to secure independence support from a rival.

Østindisk Kompagni Te

As Denmark establish Trade company and have at least 10% Tea market share.

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Denmark](/images/thumb/6/69/Denmark.png/20px-Denmark.png)](/Denmark "Denmark") [Denmark](/Denmark "Denmark")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Denmark](/images/thumb/6/69/Denmark.png/20px-Denmark.png)](/Denmark "Denmark") [Denmark](/Denmark "Denmark") _or_ [![Flag of Scandinavia](/images/thumb/d/db/Scandinavia.png/20px-Scandinavia.png)](/Scandinavia "Scandinavia") [Scandinavia](/Scandinavia "Scandinavia")
*   [![Subject tradecompany icon.png](/images/thumb/8/8d/Subject_tradecompany_icon.png/28px-Subject_tradecompany_icon.png)](/Trade_company "Trade company") Has at least one province in Asia assigned to a trade company
*   [![Tea.png](/images/thumb/5/59/Tea.png/28px-Tea.png)](/Tea "Tea") Has 10% market share in Tea

Easiest when Denmark chooses exploration ideas early to reach Southeast Asia. Then form a claim in [![Flag of Ayutthaya](/images/thumb/9/9d/Ayutthaya.png/20px-Ayutthaya.png)](/Ayutthaya "Ayutthaya") [Ayutthaya](/Ayutthaya "Ayutthaya") or wait for Mingsplosion.

[![Wealth of Nations.png](/images/thumb/7/7d/Wealth_of_Nations.png/28px-Wealth_of_Nations.png)](/Wealth_of_Nations "Wealth of Nations") _or_ [![Dharma.png](/images/thumb/f/fc/Dharma.png/28px-Dharma.png)](/Dharma "Dharma")

Protect the Secret

[![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World")

Conditions may be fulfilled any time after 1699, and do not need to be fulfilled before that time. Yemen is reformable via culture shift, so this is very attainable playing as any country. Can be combined with the [Arabian Coffee](#Arabian_Coffee) achievement. Do not form [![Flag of Arabia](/images/thumb/e/ed/Arabia.png/20px-Arabia.png)](/Arabia "Arabia") [Arabia](/Arabia "Arabia")

Sailor Mon

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Pegu](/images/thumb/3/3b/Pegu.png/20px-Pegu.png)](/Pegu "Pegu") [Pegu](/Pegu "Pegu")

The achievement needs 100k sailors in the sailor pool. The maximum sailors don't matter. Exploiting production development in coastal provinces generates sailors even if the maximum has already been reached, but this reduces the maximum, so it is only useful if 100k can actually be reached in this way.

Then no DLC is necessary.

H

[![Spain is the Emperor icon](/images/4/4f/Spain_is_the_Emperor.jpg)](/File:Spain_is_the_Emperor.jpg "Spain is the Emperor icon")

Spain is the Emperor

Become the Emperor of the Holy Roman Empire as Spain.

[![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") Not the emperor of the [Holy Roman Empire](/Holy_Roman_Empire "Holy Roman Empire")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Spain](/images/thumb/5/58/Spain.png/20px-Spain.png)](/Spain "Spain") [Spain](/Spain "Spain")
*   [![Imperial authority.png](/images/thumb/4/46/Imperial_authority.png/28px-Imperial_authority.png)](/Imperial_authority "Imperial authority") Is the emperor of the [Holy Roman Empire](/Holy_Roman_Empire "Holy Roman Empire")

Easiest to do as [![Flag of Aragon](/images/thumb/6/61/Aragon.png/20px-Aragon.png)](/Aragon "Aragon") [Aragon](/Aragon "Aragon") by allying [![Flag of Austria](/images/thumb/7/7f/Austria.png/20px-Austria.png)](/Austria "Austria") [Austria](/Austria "Austria") in 1444, abandoning your Personal Union with [![Flag of Naples](/images/thumb/b/b8/Naples.png/20px-Naples.png)](/Naples "Naples") [Naples](/Naples "Naples"), and returning 1-2 provinces in Sicily to get just below 200 development. This way, you can add your provinces to the HRE so becoming the Emperor is much easier. Once you get to Administrative Technology 10, and the Iberian Wedding event has happened, form Spain diplomatically. Wait until you're already Emperor or you'll have to leave the HRE and it will become much harder to do again.

[1.1](/Patch_1.1.X "Patch 1.1.X")

H

[![Spice Girls icon](/images/e/ed/Spice_Girls.jpg)](/File:Spice_Girls.jpg "Spice Girls icon")

Spice Girls

Having a female ruler, have active trading bonuses for Cloves, Spices, Salt and Sugar.

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Have a female ruler
*   [![Cloves.png](/images/thumb/5/5d/Cloves.png/28px-Cloves.png)](/Cloves "Cloves") Has country modifier _Trading in Cloves_
*   [![Spices.png](/images/thumb/9/94/Spices.png/28px-Spices.png)](/Spices "Spices") Has country modifier _Trading in Spices_
*   [![Salt.png](/images/thumb/7/77/Salt.png/28px-Salt.png)](/Salt "Salt") Has country modifier _Trading in Salt_
*   [![Sugar.png](/images/thumb/a/a9/Sugar.png/28px-Sugar.png)](/Sugar "Sugar") Has country modifier _Trading in Sugar_

*   This achievement is only visible if the [![Leviathan.png](/images/thumb/0/0a/Leviathan.png/28px-Leviathan.png)](/Leviathan "Leviathan") Leviathan DLC is active, but it can be achieved even without the DLC.
*   Having a Queen Regency with a male heir is sufficient.

[1.31](/1.31 "1.31")

H

[![Stern des Südens icon](/images/e/ed/Stern_des_S%C3%BCdens.png)](/File:Stern_des_S%C3%BCdens.png "Stern des Südens icon")

Stern des Südens

Form Bavaria starting as München and have your Subject Bremen own Werder.

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Munich](/images/thumb/4/4a/Munich.png/20px-Munich.png)](/Munich "Munich") [Munich](/Munich "Munich")
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Bavaria](/images/thumb/b/b3/Bavaria.png/20px-Bavaria.png)](/Bavaria "Bavaria") [Bavaria](/Bavaria "Bavaria")
*    [![Flag of Bremen](/images/thumb/c/c4/Bremen.png/20px-Bremen.png)](/Bremen "Bremen") [Bremen](/Bremen "Bremen") is a subject of [![Flag of Bavaria](/images/thumb/b/b3/Bavaria.png/20px-Bavaria.png)](/Bavaria "Bavaria") [Bavaria](/Bavaria "Bavaria")
*    [![Flag of Bremen](/images/thumb/c/c4/Bremen.png/20px-Bremen.png)](/Bremen "Bremen") [Bremen](/Bremen "Bremen") owns Werder (2778)

Expand

[![Stern des Südens map.png](/images/thumb/0/05/Stern_des_S%C3%BCdens_map.png/140px-Stern_des_S%C3%BCdens_map.png)](/File:Stern_des_S%C3%BCdens_map.png)

[](/File:Stern_des_S%C3%BCdens_map.png "Enlarge")

Werder (2778) is in the Horn of Africa region and owned by [![Flag of Marehan](/images/thumb/a/a6/Marehan.png/20px-Marehan.png)](/Marehan "Marehan") [Marehan](/Marehan "Marehan") at the start of the game. As Munich, take your time consolidating into [![Flag of Bavaria](/images/thumb/b/b3/Bavaria.png/20px-Bavaria.png)](/Bavaria "Bavaria") [Bavaria](/Bavaria "Bavaria"). If you can, befriend the emperor and/or electors to make your life within the HRE easier. Once you have a border with [![Flag of Bremen](/images/thumb/c/c4/Bremen.png/20px-Bremen.png)](/Bremen "Bremen") [Bremen](/Bremen "Bremen"), or coastal provinces in coring range of Bremen, look for war opportunities which Bremen will be called ito as an ally. As they are a free city, it will be much harder if you declare directly on them (as the Emperor will defend free cities). Annex Bremen in a separate peace and release them as your vassal (you can't vassalize a free city in a peace deal). Afterwards, expand in power so that you can combat your most powerful neighbours - Ottomans, Spain, France, etc. Make sure to give Bremen land, either in the direction of the Ottomans or in the direction of Spain. You will have to fight your way through at least one, feeding Bremen provinces to "snake" their land down to Werder (this is because vassals need adjacent land or sea tiles to be given provinces and do not care about coring distance/colonial range). The least time-consuming method would be to give them a province per sea tile starting from the Mediterranean, down through the [![Flag of Mamluks](/images/thumb/c/ca/The_Mamluks.png/20px-The_Mamluks.png)](/Mamluks "Mamluks") [Mamluks](/Mamluks "Mamluks") to the Red Sea coast, and finally down to Werder.

[![Stiff Upper Lippe icon](/images/7/7a/Stiff_Upper_Lippe.png)](/File:Stiff_Upper_Lippe.png "Stiff Upper Lippe icon")

Stiff Upper Lippe

As Lippe, own all of the British Isles.

[![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Lippe](/images/thumb/7/71/Lippe.png/20px-Lippe.png)](/Lippe "Lippe") [Lippe](/Lippe "Lippe")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own all provinces in [Britain](/European_regions#Britain "European regions")

Expand

[![](/images/thumb/3/3e/Stiff_Upper_Lippe_map.png/140px-Stiff_Upper_Lippe_map.png)](/File:Stiff_Upper_Lippe_map.png)

[](/File:Stiff_Upper_Lippe_map.png "Enlarge")

Britain region

Lippe doesn't exist in 1444, but it can be released from its core province Ravensberg (4775) which is owned by [![Flag of Berg](/images/thumb/d/dd/Berg.png/20px-Berg.png)](/Berg "Berg") [Berg](/Berg "Berg"). By first releasing Lippe as a regular vassal, giving them provinces to core and annexing them gives more land when releasing them again.

Can be done as part of a HRE campaign. Ensure Lippe exists before you pass "Revoke the Privilegia". Feed all of Britain's cores to your Lippe vassal and then either annex Lippe or pass the final reform "Renovatio Imperii", then release and play as Lippe, earning you the achievement.

[1.30](/1.30 "1.30")

H

[![Sun Invasion icon](/images/a/a3/Sun_Invasion.png)](/File:Sun_Invasion.png "Sun Invasion icon")

Sun Invasion

As the Madyas, own and have cores on Tepeacac, Mexico, Tullucan and Huastec.

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Madyas](/images/thumb/e/e9/Madyas.png/20px-Madyas.png)](/Madyas "Madyas") [Madyas](/Madyas "Madyas")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own and core the provinces of Tepeacac (2628), Mexico (852), Tullucan (2626) and Tlapacoyan(853, formerly called Huastec).

Expand

[![Sun Invasion map.png](/images/a/a0/Sun_Invasion_map.png)](/File:Sun_Invasion_map.png)

You need to directly own and core the target provinces, and not through your colonial nation. There are several ways to achieve this:

Move your capital city to North America before a colonial nation forms.

Get a colonial nation in one of the colonial regions adjacent to Mexico and grant them a chain of colonized or conquered provinces in Mexico up to the achievement provinces with the help of the grant province subject interaction(or by transferring occupations in a war if they are on the same continent as the capital of the CN). The achievement provinces can be cored as soon as the colonial nation has cored a province next to them.

Vassalize a native, take land from some other native including the needed ones and a chain of provinces leading to the coast. Core one coastal province to be able to start coring the 4 achievement provinces. To avoid forming a colonial nation, the cored coastal province then has to be given to the vassal.

Use the [![Ab no distance for core.png](/images/thumb/0/08/Ab_no_distance_for_core.png/24px-Ab_no_distance_for_core.png)](/File:Ab_no_distance_for_core.png) Unrestricted Conquest age ability from the [![Age of Revolutions.png](/images/thumb/5/59/Age_of_Revolutions.png/24px-Age_of_Revolutions.png)](/Age_of_Revolutions "Age of Revolutions") Age of Revolutions.

Simply annexing a vassal in the region won't fire the achievement.

Stardust Crusaders

*   [![Missionaries.png](/images/thumb/a/ad/Missionaries.png/28px-Missionaries.png)](/Missionary "Missionary") The palastine area and the province Cairo (361) have a [christian](/Christian "Christian") religion and are owned by this country

Sworn Fealty

Starting as an Arabian Tribal Federation, unite Arabia and have Maximum tribal Allegiance.

*   [![Culture icon.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Culture_icon.png/28px-Culture_icon.png)](/Culture "Culture") Culture group is _Levantine_
*   [![Primary culture.png](/images/thumb/e/e1/Primary_culture.png/28px-Primary_culture.png)](/Primary_culture "Primary culture") Culture is not _Turkish_
*   [![Government tribal.png](/images/thumb/a/a5/Government_tribal.png/28px-Government_tribal.png)](/Tribal_government "Tribal government") Has the [Tribal Federation](/Tribal_Federation "Tribal Federation") government reform

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Arabia](/images/thumb/e/ed/Arabia.png/20px-Arabia.png)](/Arabia "Arabia") [Arabia](/Arabia "Arabia")
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Have **100** Tribal Allegiance

Possible starts are [![Flag of Anizah](/images/thumb/9/90/Anizah.png/20px-Anizah.png)](/Anizah "Anizah") [Anizah](/Anizah "Anizah"), [![Flag of Dawasir](/images/thumb/f/ff/Dawasir.png/20px-Dawasir.png)](/Dawasir "Dawasir") [Dawasir](/Dawasir "Dawasir"), [![Flag of Fadl](/images/thumb/3/34/Fadl.png/20px-Fadl.png)](/Fadl "Fadl") [Fadl](/Fadl "Fadl"), [![Flag of Najd](/images/thumb/c/c9/Najd.png/20px-Najd.png)](/Najd "Najd") [Najd](/Najd "Najd"), [![Flag of Najran](/images/thumb/5/50/Najran.png/20px-Najran.png)](/Najran "Najran") [Najran](/Najran "Najran"), [![Flag of Shammar](/images/thumb/3/34/Shammar.png/20px-Shammar.png)](/Shammar "Shammar") [Shammar](/Shammar "Shammar") and [![Flag of Yas](/images/thumb/d/d3/Yas.png/20px-Yas.png)](/Yas "Yas") [Yas](/Yas "Yas")

[Terra Mariana](/Terra_Mariana "Terra Mariana")

[1.14](/1.14 "1.14")

H

[![That's a Silk Road icon](/images/2/29/That%27s_a_Silk_Road.jpg)](/File:That%27s_a_Silk_Road.jpg "That's a Silk Road icon")

That's a Silk Road

Own or have a subject own all provinces in the world producing silk.

[![Silk.png](/images/thumb/8/83/Silk.png/28px-Silk.png)](/Silk "Silk") All provinces with silk are owned by the player's country or its non-tributary [subjects](/Subjects "Subjects").

Silk provinces stretch from Hüdavendigar to Kyoto, with concentrations in the Persia, India and South China regions. With [![Golden Century.png](/images/thumb/b/bb/Golden_Century.png/28px-Golden_Century.png)](/Golden_Century "Golden Century") Golden Century, [![Flag of Aragon](/images/thumb/6/61/Aragon.png/20px-Aragon.png)](/Aragon "Aragon") [Aragon](/Aragon "Aragon") has a mission that makes Valencia produce silk. With [![Emperor](/images/thumb/c/c5/Emperor.png/28px-Emperor.png)](/Emperor_(DLC) "Emperor") Emperor, [![Flag of Milan](/images/thumb/d/d6/Milan.png/20px-Milan.png)](/Milan "Milan") [Milan](/Milan "Milan") has a mission that makes Como produce silk.

[![The 52 Garhs icon](/images/5/55/The_52_Garhs.png)](/File:The_52_Garhs.png "The 52 Garhs icon")

The 52 Garhs

As Garhwal own and maintain 52 forts without going into debt.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Garhwal](/images/thumb/d/dd/Garhwal.png/20px-Garhwal.png)](/Garhwal "Garhwal") [Garhwal](/Garhwal "Garhwal")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Has no loans
*   [![Fort level.png](/images/thumb/a/a0/Fort_level.png/28px-Fort_level.png)](/Fort_level "Fort level") Own at least 52 forts (level 2)

Forming [![Flag of Nepal](/images/thumb/3/3a/Nepal.png/20px-Nepal.png)](/Nepal "Nepal") [Nepal](/Nepal "Nepal") does not prevent getting this achievement.

[1.22](/1.22 "1.22")

H

[![The Animal Kingdom icon](/images/3/35/The_Animal_Kingdom.jpg)](/File:The_Animal_Kingdom.jpg "The Animal Kingdom icon")

The Animal Kingdom

As Manipur, unite the Bengal region and convert it to Animism.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Manipur](/images/thumb/7/71/Manipur.png/20px-Manipur.png)](/Manipur "Manipur") [Manipur](/Manipur "Manipur")

*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") All provinces in the [Bengal](/Indian_regions "Indian regions") region are owned by the player's country _or_ its non-tributary [subjects](/Subjects "Subjects").
*   [![Animism](/images/thumb/1/18/Animist.png/28px-Animist.png)](/Animist "Animist") All provinces in the Bengal region are Animist

As soon as you can, take on your western neighbours, [![Flag of Kachar](/images/thumb/3/3e/Kachar.png/20px-Kachar.png)](/Kachar "Kachar") [Kachar](/Kachar "Kachar") and/or [![Flag of Tripura](/images/thumb/9/94/Tripura.png/20px-Tripura.png)](/Tripura "Tripura") [Tripura](/Tripura "Tripura"). You will not have much luck east from game start, as Ava will guard it's tributaries. Best option is to not conquer both provinces, but to take one as a vassal - and a second OPM vassal in india as soon as possible as well. You can force them to be animist and feed them Indian culture provinces that you conquer. Allies are hard to come by, and vassals will be obliged to help you, pay you, give you extra force limit, etc.. Look for an opportunity to eat nations up north such as Assam, Sadiya, Mong Kawng, and Koch before [![Flag of Bengal](/images/thumb/c/c6/Bengal.png/20px-Bengal.png)](/Bengal "Bengal") [Bengal](/Bengal "Bengal") annexes them or [![Flag of Ming](/images/thumb/a/a5/Ming.png/20px-Ming.png)](/Ming "Ming") [Ming](/Ming "Ming") makes them a tributary. Delay becoming a tributary of Ming as long as possible (or never if you can), but do not be afraid to use it as an inroad for expansion east as Ming will have a lot of tributary states in that direction. Once you are set up, it's the same as any other OPM-to-#1-Great-Power game. Get religious ideas to make conversions faster, especially against Islamic provinces.

[1.16](/1.16 "1.16")

H

[![The Chrysanthemum Throne icon](/images/2/2e/The_Chrysanthemum_Throne.jpg)](/File:The_Chrysanthemum_Throne.jpg "The Chrysanthemum Throne icon")

The Chrysanthemum Throne

Unite Japan as a Daimyo.

[![Government monarchy.png](/images/thumb/4/4d/Government_monarchy.png/28px-Government_monarchy.png)](/Monarchy "Monarchy") Has the [Daimyo](/Daimyo "Daimyo") government reform

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Japan](/images/thumb/f/fc/Japan.png/20px-Japan.png)](/Japan "Japan") [Japan](/Japan "Japan")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") All provinces in [Japan region](/Asian_regions#Japan "Asian regions") must be either owned and cored by Japan or unowned.

You must start as a Daimyo subject of the [![Flag of Ashikaga](/images/thumb/a/a1/Ashikaga.png/20px-Ashikaga.png)](/Ashikaga "Ashikaga") [Ashikaga](/Ashikaga "Ashikaga") Shogunate. The Japan region includes Okinawa, Hokkaido, and the Kuril Islands.

[1.1](/Patch_1.1.X "Patch 1.1.X")

H

[![The Freest Man in the World icon](/images/d/d6/The_Freest_Man_in_the_World.png)](/File:The_Freest_Man_in_the_World.png "The Freest Man in the World icon")

The Freest Man in the World

Ensure that no colonized province in the world produces slaves while having the War Against the World Doctrine government reform enacted.

*   [![Government republic.png](/images/thumb/5/5d/Government_republic.png/28px-Government_republic.png)](/Republic "Republic") Has enacted the [Pirate Republic](/Pirate_Republic "Pirate Republic") government reform
*   [![Government republic.png](/images/thumb/5/5d/Government_republic.png/28px-Government_republic.png)](/Republic "Republic") Has enacted the [War Against the World Doctrine](/War_Against_the_World_Doctrine "War Against the World Doctrine") government reform
*   [![Slaves.png](/images/thumb/2/25/Slaves.png/28px-Slaves.png)](/Slaves "Slaves") No fully colonized province in the world produces slaves

Almost all [![Slaves.png](/images/thumb/2/25/Slaves.png/28px-Slaves.png)](/Slaves "Slaves") slave provinces are on the African continent (except Azov). [![Flag of Palembang](/images/thumb/b/b7/Palembang.png/20px-Palembang.png)](/Palembang "Palembang") [Palembang](/Palembang "Palembang") has a quick event which converts them into pirate republic, but they are Hindu and have mediocre ideas. An easier way is to start as [![Flag of Pasai](/images/thumb/a/a2/Pasai.png/20px-Pasai.png)](/Pasai "Pasai") [Pasai](/Pasai "Pasai") and hoist the black flag: Pasai has better starting provinces, better ideas, and is Muslim, which makes alliance and AE easier. Alternatively, [![Flag of Gotland](/images/thumb/2/2c/Gotland.png/20px-Gotland.png)](/Gotland "Gotland") [Gotland](/Gotland "Gotland") also becomes a pirate nation through event. Azov and the Ivory Coast are areas of contention with [![Slaves.png](/images/thumb/2/25/Slaves.png/28px-Slaves.png)](/Slaves "Slaves") slaves which need to be rushed to asap. [![Flag of Kilwa](/images/thumb/c/cb/Kilwa.png/20px-Kilwa.png)](/Kilwa "Kilwa") [Kilwa](/Kilwa "Kilwa") has the best starting location and missions in Africa. Complete Prepare the Invasion mission to secure five provinces in Madagascar. Move Kilwa's capital to Zanzibar or Madagascar. Give the remaining provinces to Sofala and release the vassal, then [Hoist the Black Flag](/Pirate_republic#Hoist_the_Black_Flag "Pirate republic")

[![Golden Century.png](/images/thumb/b/bb/Golden_Century.png/28px-Golden_Century.png)](/Golden_Century "Golden Century") _or_ [![Lions of the North.png](/images/thumb/c/cd/Lions_of_the_North.png/28px-Lions_of_the_North.png)](/Lions_of_the_North "Lions of the North")

[1.34](/1.34 "1.34")

H

[![The Grand Armada icon](/images/d/d6/The_Grand_Armada.jpg)](/File:The_Grand_Armada.jpg "The Grand Armada icon")

The Grand Armada

Have 500 heavy ships and no loans.

*   [![Heavy ship.png](/images/thumb/5/50/Heavy_ship.png/28px-Heavy_ship.png)](/Heavy_ship "Heavy ship") Have 500 heavy ships
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Have no [loans](/Loan "Loan")

Best done with a high income nation with naval force limit and ship build cost bonuses. [Netherlands](/Netherlands "Netherlands"), [Venice](/Venice "Venice"), and [Genoa](/Genoa "Genoa") are optimal but can easily be done with [England](/England "England"), [Spain](/Spain "Spain") or [Malaya](/Malaya "Malaya"). With [![Rights of Man.png](/images/thumb/5/50/Rights_of_Man.png/28px-Rights_of_Man.png)](/Rights_of_Man "Rights of Man") Rights of Man DLC, this can be done much more easily by debasing currency.

[![The Sun Never Sets on the Indian Empire icon](/images/a/af/The_Sun_Never_Sets_on_the_Indian_Empire.png)](/File:The_Sun_Never_Sets_on_the_Indian_Empire.png "The Sun Never Sets on the Indian Empire icon")

[The Sun Never Sets on the Indian Empire](/The_Sun_Never_Sets_on_the_Indian_Empire "The Sun Never Sets on the Indian Empire")

Form Hindustan or Bharat and own or have a subject own Cape, London, Hong Kong (Canton) and Ottawa (Kichessipirini).

[![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World").

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Hindustan](/images/thumb/3/3e/Hindustan.png/20px-Hindustan.png)](/Hindustan "Hindustan") [Hindustan](/Hindustan "Hindustan") or [![Flag of Bharat](/images/thumb/b/b0/Bharat.png/20px-Bharat.png)](/Bharat "Bharat") [Bharat](/Bharat "Bharat")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own or have a non-tributary subject own London (236), Cape (1177), Canton (667) and Kichessipirini (4890)

[1.9](/1.9 "1.9")

H

[![These Banners need a Saga icon](/images/d/de/These_Banners_need_a_Saga.png)](/File:These_Banners_need_a_Saga.png "These Banners need a Saga icon")

These Banners need a Saga

Starting as a Jurchen nation, have 100 regiments of Banners raised at the same time.

[![Culture icon.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Culture_icon.png/28px-Culture_icon.png)](/Culture "Culture") Started with culture _Jurchen_

[![Possible Manchu banners.png](/images/thumb/6/69/Possible_Manchu_banners.png/28px-Possible_Manchu_banners.png)](/Possible_Manchu_banners "Possible Manchu banners") Have 100 banner regiments

Make a custom Jurchen duchy holding all Jurchen provinces and the most developed states in East Asia. Set it up for high number of states, reduced culture conversion cost, and lots of diplomatic power. Start with at least 1200-1250 development, or face needing to develop or conquer more and wait for separatism to tick down. Form Manchu and then Qing, then make everyone nearby pay tribute in diplomatic power. Everything can be converted to Manchu before 1500, which is enough for 100 regiments and a few more. Admin tech 8 gives 3 more state slots but it is possible without them.

*   [![Mandate of Heaven.png](/images/thumb/7/7c/Mandate_of_Heaven.png/28px-Mandate_of_Heaven.png)](/Mandate_of_Heaven "Mandate of Heaven")
*   [![Nation designer.png](/images/a/ab/Nation_designer.png)](/Nation_designer "Nation designer")

[1.20](/1.20 "1.20")

[![Tiger of Mysore icon](/images/a/a8/Tiger_of_Mysore.png)](/File:Tiger_of_Mysore.png "Tiger of Mysore icon")

Tiger of Mysore

Starting as Mysore, Conquer the Deccan and Coromandel Regions.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Mysore](/images/thumb/c/cd/Mysore.png/20px-Mysore.png)](/Mysore "Mysore") [Mysore](/Mysore "Mysore")

*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") All provinces in Deccan and Coromandel regions are owned by the country or a non-tributary subject

Expand

[![Tiger of Mysore map.png](/images/thumb/b/b9/Tiger_of_Mysore_map.png/140px-Tiger_of_Mysore_map.png)](/File:Tiger_of_Mysore_map.png)

[](/File:Tiger_of_Mysore_map.png "Enlarge")

You need to ally Bahmanis to make it possible to defeat Vijayanagar If you can't, then you might have to restart a few times or no-cb a country in southeast Asia

[1.26](/1.26 "1.26")

H

[![Turkish Delight icon](/images/8/85/Turkish_Delight.jpg)](/File:Turkish_Delight.jpg "Turkish Delight icon")

Turkish Delight

Start as Candar and own 20 Sugar provinces between you and your subjects.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Candar](/images/thumb/5/5c/Candar.png/20px-Candar.png)](/Candar "Candar") [Candar](/Candar "Candar")

[![Sugar.png](/images/thumb/a/a9/Sugar.png/28px-Sugar.png)](/Sugar "Sugar") Have 20 provinces of sugar owned by this country and its non-tributary subjects

Fleeing to the new world is recommended, if not required for this achievement.

Since version 1.35 the provinces have to be owned by the player and the player's subjects, but in earlier versions, they had to be owned by Candar and Candar's subject which made the achievement all but impossible after forming another country. On the flip side, bringing Candar back as an AI country and giving them the provinces doesn't work anymore.

[1.18](/1.18 "1.18")

H

[![Venetian Sea icon](/images/a/a3/Venetian_Sea.jpg)](/File:Venetian_Sea.jpg "Venetian Sea icon")

Venetian Sea

Have a 75% Trade share in both the Alexandria and Constantinople nodes as Venice, owning less than 10 cities.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Venice](/images/thumb/e/e1/Venice.png/20px-Venice.png)](/Venice "Venice") [Venice](/Venice "Venice")

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Have less than 10 provinces
*   [![Trade power.png](/images/thumb/1/10/Trade_power.png/28px-Trade_power.png)](/Trade_power "Trade power") Have at least **75%** of the total trade power in the trade nodes Alexandria and Constantinople

Quickly vassalize Byzantium, feed them back their cores, ally Austria/Hungary to combat the Ottomans early game. Conquer all the centers of trade/estuaries in the Constantinople trade node and feed them to Byzantium. You can release Bulgaria and feed them as well so Byzantium does not have as high development. Repeat this by releasing Syria and feeding them back their cores and conquering/feeding Syria centers of trade in Alexandria node. Keep vassals happy by developing their provinces, placating and developing your own provinces to make yourself seem stronger. Plutocratic/Influence/Diplomatic/Innovative ideas help with keeping vassals loyal because of ideas, policies and diplomatic reputation. Take Trade idea group. You can drop Crete, Corfu and Dalmacija and pick up Milan and Ragusa. Release Croatia to help control the Ragusa trade node to ensure your wealth.

[1.7](/1.7 "1.7")

H

[![Why is the Rûm gone!? icon](/images/2/21/Why_is_the_R%C3%BBm_gone%21%3F.png)](/File:Why_is_the_R%C3%BBm_gone!%3F.png "Why is the Rûm gone!? icon")

Why is the Rûm gone!?

As Asturias, establish an Order in Rum.

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Asturias](/images/thumb/9/99/Asturias.png/20px-Asturias.png)](/Asturias "Asturias") [Asturias](/Asturias "Asturias")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own and have a [holy order](/Holy_order "Holy order") established in the [Rum area](/European_regions#Rum "European regions")

*   Easiest to do as Ottomans. First, no-CB Castile and conquer the province of Vizcaya, then release Asturias as a vassal. Next, conquer enough Iberian provinces to connect Vizcaya to the Mediterranean as well as at least one province per sea tile connecting Iberia to all provinces in the Rum area, giving Asturias the line of provinces in each peace deal as well as any of your own provinces needed to complete the snake. Integrate and re-release Asturias, selecting to play as them, and then establish the holy order needed in order to complete the achievement. A similar strategy can be used if starting as Aragon, which owns most of the connecting provinces needed.

[![Golden Century.png](/images/thumb/b/bb/Golden_Century.png/28px-Golden_Century.png)](/Golden_Century "Golden Century")

[1.28](/1.28 "1.28")

H

[![With a little help.. icon](/images/2/2f/With_a_little_help...jpg)](/File:With_a_little_help...jpg "With a little help.. icon")

With a little help..

As Ragusa, lead a Trade League of at least 5 nations and guarantee the Ottomans’ independence.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Ragusa](/images/thumb/e/e6/Ragusa.png/20px-Ragusa.png)](/Ragusa "Ragusa") [Ragusa](/Ragusa "Ragusa")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Lead a Trade League of at least 5 nations
*   [![Diplomatic relations.png](/images/thumb/5/58/Diplomatic_relations.png/28px-Diplomatic_relations.png)](/Diplomatic_relations "Diplomatic relations") Guarantee the independence of [![Flag of Ottomans](/images/thumb/8/89/Ottomans.png/20px-Ottomans.png)](/Ottomans "Ottomans") [Ottomans](/Ottomans "Ottomans")

You can only guarantee a country if you are larger than it. Ironically, taking land from the Ottomans for a vassal is probably the best way to do this. Forming [![Flag of Dalmatia](/images/thumb/d/d3/Dalmatia.png/20px-Dalmatia.png)](/Dalmatia "Dalmatia") [Dalmatia](/Dalmatia "Dalmatia") will not prevent the achievement.

[![Mare Nostrum.png](/images/thumb/f/ff/Mare_Nostrum.png/28px-Mare_Nostrum.png)](/Mare_Nostrum "Mare Nostrum")

[1.16](/1.16 "1.16")

H

[![Yarr Harr a Pirate's Life For Me icon](/images/0/00/Yarr_Harr_a_Pirate%27s_Life_For_Me.png)](/File:Yarr_Harr_a_Pirate%27s_Life_For_Me.png "Yarr Harr a Pirate's Life For Me icon")

Yarr Harr a Pirate's Life For Me

Choose to play as New Providence and conquer all of Caribbeans.

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") No more than 1 custom nation exists in the world
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") Used no more than 201 nation designer points if playing as a custom nation

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of New Providence](/images/thumb/f/f2/New_Providence.png/20px-New_Providence.png)](/New_Providence "New Providence") [New Providence](/New_Providence "New Providence")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Owns all provinces in the [Caribbean](/Caribbean "Caribbean") region.

Bermuda is in the Caribbean region also.

*   Starting as a custom nation in the Caribbean with the Bahamas as a core, and privateering in the Caribbean will allow you to spawn New Providence extremely quickly, giving you time to expand and colonize much of the Caribbean before the European colonial powers arrive. Pirate republics can declare war on colonial nations without their overlord being called as an ally, so if Europeans begin to colonize the Caribbean before you can finish, it may be easier to allow a colonial nation to form.

*   [![Golden Century.png](/images/thumb/b/bb/Golden_Century.png/28px-Golden_Century.png)](/Golden_Century "Golden Century")
*   [![Nation designer.png](/images/a/ab/Nation_designer.png)](/Nation_designer "Nation designer")

[1.28](/1.28 "1.28")

H

[![Triple the Rome icon](/images/3/34/Triple_the_Rome.png)](/File:Triple_the_Rome.png "Triple the Rome icon")

Triple the Rome

As Russia, be the Emperor of China and the HRE.

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Russia](/images/thumb/e/ee/Russia.png/20px-Russia.png)](/Russia "Russia") [Russia](/Russia "Russia")
*   [![Emperor of china icon.png](/images/thumb/2/25/Emperor_of_china_icon.png/28px-Emperor_of_china_icon.png)](/Emperor_of_China "Emperor of China") Is Emperor of China
*   [![Imperial authority.png](/images/thumb/4/46/Imperial_authority.png/28px-Imperial_authority.png)](/Imperial_authority "Imperial authority") Is the emperor of the [Holy Roman Empire](/Holy_Roman_Empire "Holy Roman Empire")

To be [Emperor of China](/Emperor_of_China "Emperor of China"), you must be in the [Pagan](/Pagan "Pagan") or [Eastern](/Eastern_denominations "Eastern denominations") religion group, whilst to be the HRE Emperor, you generally must be [![Catholicism](/images/thumb/3/39/Catholic.png/28px-Catholic.png)](/Catholic "Catholic") Catholic unless [![Protestantism](/images/thumb/0/0d/Protestant.png/28px-Protestant.png)](/Protestant "Protestant") Protestants won the league war, or sometimes other Christian denominations given specific circumstances (see [League war](/League_war "League war")), so a religion switch will be necessary to complete the achievement. Switching to a non-Christian religion as HRE Emperor will cause the emperorship to be lost unless the Erbkaisertum reform has been passed, while changing religion as Emperor of China allows you to retain the title. As such, it may be easiest to start as an atypical nation to form [![Flag of Russia](/images/thumb/e/ee/Russia.png/20px-Russia.png)](/Russia "Russia") [Russia](/Russia "Russia") such as [![Flag of Oirat](/images/thumb/2/20/Oirat.png/20px-Oirat.png)](/Oirat "Oirat") [Oirat](/Oirat "Oirat"), which starts off as [![Tengri](/images/thumb/9/9f/Tengri.png/28px-Tengri.png)](/Tengri "Tengri") Tengri and can use horde mechanics to relatively easily expand into the territories needed to form Russia. It is recommended to not seize the mandate until the needed provinces are conquered since seizing the mandate will change your government to Celestial Empire and disable horde mechanics. At this point, culture shift to [![Primary culture.png](/images/thumb/e/e1/Primary_culture.png/28px-Primary_culture.png)](/Primary_culture "Primary culture") Muscovite, Novgorodian or Ryazanian culture and form Russia once you hit admin tech 10. At some point you will need to conquer a Catholic province, perhaps from the Scandinavian or the Baltic regions, which will allow you to convert to Catholic via rebels. After seizing the Mandate of Heaven, convert to Catholicism, then ally or vassalize enough HRE electors to get yourself elected Holy Roman Emperor.

[![Mandate of Heaven.png](/images/thumb/7/7c/Mandate_of_Heaven.png/28px-Mandate_of_Heaven.png)](/Mandate_of_Heaven "Mandate of Heaven")

[A Sun God](/A_Sun_God "A Sun God")

Form Inca, embrace all Institutions and own all of South America as core provinces.

[![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World").

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Inca](/images/thumb/3/36/Inca.png/20px-Inca.png)](/Inca "Inca") [Inca](/Inca "Inca")
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Institutions.png](/images/thumb/4/43/Institutions.png/28px-Institutions.png)](/Institutions "Institutions") Have embraced all [institutions](/Institutions "Institutions")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") All provinces in [South America](/South_America "South America") are either empty, [wasteland](/Wasteland "Wasteland"), a [colony](/Colony "Colony") or owned and cored [![Flag of Inca](/images/thumb/3/36/Inca.png/20px-Inca.png)](/Inca "Inca") [Inca](/Inca "Inca").

The Falklands (1095), South Georgia (2025) and Galapagos (2002) are also part of South America. It is useful to colonize them before a strong colonizer can do it, because these provinces won't become part of a colonial nation.

[![African Power icon](/images/a/ac/African_Power.jpg)](/File:African_Power.jpg "African Power icon")

African Power

Own and have cores on all provinces in Africa as Kongo.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Kongo](/images/thumb/1/16/Kongo.png/20px-Kongo.png)](/Kongo "Kongo") [Kongo](/Kongo "Kongo")

[![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") All fully colonized provinces in [Africa](/Africa "Africa") are owned and cored by [![Flag of Kongo](/images/thumb/1/16/Kongo.png/20px-Kongo.png)](/Kongo "Kongo") [Kongo](/Kongo "Kongo")

*   Empty provinces and unfinished colonies are excluded and may be safely ignored.
*   The isolated islands required are: Comoros, Mahe, Mauritius, Île Bourbon, Sao Tome, Fernando Po, St. Helena, Cape Verde and Djerba (but not the Canarias, Madeira, Azores, Maldives, Socotra, or any other in the Mediterranean).

VH

[![An Unlikely Candidate icon](/images/b/b9/An_Unlikely_Candidate.png)](/File:An_Unlikely_Candidate.png "An Unlikely Candidate icon")

An Unlikely Candidate

Starting as Mzab, Touggourt or Djerid, reform Al-Andalus.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as _either_:

*    [![Flag of Mzab](/images/thumb/6/62/Mzab.png/20px-Mzab.png)](/Mzab "Mzab") [Mzab](/Mzab "Mzab")
*    [![Flag of Touggourt](/images/thumb/2/26/Touggourt.png/20px-Touggourt.png)](/Touggourt "Touggourt") [Touggourt](/Touggourt "Touggourt")
*    [![Flag of Djerid](/images/thumb/4/43/Djerid.png/20px-Djerid.png)](/Djerid "Djerid") [Djerid](/Djerid "Djerid")

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Andalusia](/images/thumb/0/09/Andalusia.png/20px-Andalusia.png)](/Andalusia "Andalusia") [Andalusia](/Andalusia "Andalusia")

Forming [![Flag of Algiers](/images/thumb/8/86/Algiers.png/20px-Algiers.png)](/Algiers "Algiers") [Algiers](/Algiers "Algiers"), [![Flag of Morocco](/images/thumb/e/e4/Morocco.png/20px-Morocco.png)](/Morocco "Morocco") [Morocco](/Morocco "Morocco"), [![Flag of Tunis](/images/thumb/7/79/Tunis.png/20px-Tunis.png)](/Tunis "Tunis") [Tunis](/Tunis "Tunis") or another country _will not_ prevent the achievement but instead only hide its conditions.

[Around the World in 80 Years](/Around_the_World_in_80_Years "Around the World in 80 Years")

Starting as a Custom Nation of up to 400 points in the British Region, own New York, San Francisco, Suez, Bombay, Calcutta, Hong Kong and Yokohama by 1524.11.11.

*   [![Nation designer.png](/images/a/ab/Nation_designer.png)](/Nation_designer "Nation designer") Playing as a custom nation

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") The date is before 12 November 1524
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own Manahahttan (965), T'epot'aha'l (869), Suez (2315), Thana (529), Bengal Delta (561), Canton (667), and Musashi (1028)

Provinces cannot be owned by [subject](/Subject "Subject"), so it is important not to establish colonial nations in North America. Considerably easier with the [charter company](/Charter_company "Charter company") mechanism from [![Dharma.png](/images/thumb/f/fc/Dharma.png/28px-Dharma.png)](/Dharma "Dharma") Dharma.

[![Big Blue Blob icon](/images/a/aa/Big_Blue_Blob.jpg)](/File:Big_Blue_Blob.jpg "Big Blue Blob icon")

[Big Blue Blob](/Big_Blue_Blob "Big Blue Blob")

As France, hold 100 European core provinces before 1500.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of France](/images/thumb/d/de/France.png/20px-France.png)](/France "France") [France](/France "France")

[1.12](/1.12 "1.12")

VH

[![Choson One icon](/images/b/b3/Choson_One.jpg)](/File:Choson_One.jpg "Choson One icon")

Choson One

As Korea, own or have a subject own all Shinto, Confucian and Buddhist provinces in the world.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Korea](/images/thumb/4/45/Korea.png/20px-Korea.png)](/Korea "Korea") [Korea](/Korea "Korea")

[![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") All provinces following an [Eastern religion](/Eastern_denominations "Eastern denominations") are owned by [![Flag of Korea](/images/thumb/4/45/Korea.png/20px-Korea.png)](/Korea "Korea") [Korea](/Korea "Korea") _or_ its non-tributary [subjects](/Subjects "Subjects").

The Eastern religions are Theravada, Vajrayana, Mahayana, Confucian, and Shinto. Due to [![Flag of Ming](/images/thumb/a/a5/Ming.png/20px-Ming.png)](/Ming "Ming") [Ming](/Ming "Ming")'s size and power it is best to become their tributary and go after all other nations around before attempting to attack them.

The province Kuma (2417) in the Pontic Steppe can turn [![Flag of Vajrayana](/images/thumb/f/f1/Vajrayana.png/20px-Vajrayana.png)](/Vajrayana "Vajrayana") [Vajrayana](/Vajrayana "Vajrayana") Vajrayana due to the event which spawns [![Flag of Kalmyk](/images/thumb/f/f8/Kalmyk.png/20px-Kalmyk.png)](/Kalmyk "Kalmyk") [Kalmyk](/Kalmyk "Kalmyk").

[![Cotton Kandy icon](/images/f/f3/Cotton_Kandy.png)](/File:Cotton_Kandy.png "Cotton Kandy icon")

Cotton Kandy

As Kandy be production leader in Cotton.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Kandy](/images/thumb/1/1b/Kandy.png/20px-Kandy.png)](/Kandy "Kandy") [Kandy](/Kandy "Kandy")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Kandy](/images/thumb/1/1b/Kandy.png/20px-Kandy.png)](/Kandy "Kandy") [Kandy](/Kandy "Kandy")
*   [![Cotton.png](/images/thumb/c/c3/Cotton.png/28px-Cotton.png)](/Cotton "Cotton") Be production leader of cotton

The Indian sub-continent already has the highest concentration of cotton-producing provinces in the game, so this achievement is best partnered with [The Buddhists Strike Back](/The_Buddhists_Strike_Back "The Buddhists Strike Back").

[1.26](/1.26 "1.26")

VH

[![Crossing the Finnish Line icon](/images/c/ce/Crossing_the_Finnish_Line.png)](/File:Crossing_the_Finnish_Line.png "Crossing the Finnish Line icon")

Crossing the Finnish Line

Release and play as Finland in 1444 and have a direct land connection to the Cape while your capital is in Nyland/Uusimaa.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Sweden](/images/thumb/9/98/Sweden.png/20px-Sweden.png)](/Sweden "Sweden") [Sweden](/Sweden "Sweden")

*    [![Flag of Finland](/images/thumb/c/c4/Finland.png/20px-Finland.png)](/Finland "Finland") [Finland](/Finland "Finland") has been released in 1444
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is _or_ was [![Flag of Finland](/images/thumb/c/c4/Finland.png/20px-Finland.png)](/Finland "Finland") [Finland](/Finland "Finland")
*   [![Capital.png](/images/thumb/6/6e/Capital.png/28px-Capital.png)](/Capital "Capital") Capital is Nyland(28)
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Owns Cape(1177)
*   There exists a land connection of owned provinces between the capital and Cape(1177)

The land connection can go over strait crossings (it is recommended to avoid taking Suez as to not anger the [![Flag of Ottomans](/images/thumb/8/89/Ottomans.png/20px-Ottomans.png)](/Ottomans "Ottomans") [Ottomans](/Ottomans "Ottomans")). Finland must be released in 1444, but you do not have to play as them in 1444. Consider making them a vassal, feeding them the provinces required, annexing them, the releasing and playing as them after annexing them. This gives you access to the Sweden mission tree and power base to work with.

[1.34](/1.34 "1.34")

VH

[![Empire of Mann icon](/images/2/22/Empire_of_Mann.png)](/File:Empire_of_Mann.png "Empire of Mann icon")

Empire of Mann

As Mann, conquer all Islands in the world.

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Mann](/images/thumb/9/9d/Mann.png/20px-Mann.png)](/Mann "Mann") [Mann](/Mann "Mann")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own _or_ have non-tributary subjects own all provinces which are [on an island](/Island#province_is_on_an_island "Island").

Mann can't be selected as a country in 1444, you must release it as a vassal and choose the option to play as a released vassal.

As England release Mann at the very start of the game. After 10 years you can annex them again. As the annexation progresses grant them your provinces bit by bit before the process hits 100%. You can even move your capital to continental Europe and give London to Mann. Be careful about France as they will likely attack you once you are weakened. After annexation is finished spend all your monarch points to boost provinces that Mann considers as a core. Now release Mann again and chose to play as a released vassal. Do _not_ form England again or any other country because it will prevent getting the achievement. Alternatively, sabotage England as much as possible, such as releasing all releasable nations, leaving Mann for last. Release and play as them, then ally all other released nations, plus a major like Castile. Take London, Sussex, and Kent in your first war and you should be off to a great start.

[1.25](/1.25 "1.25")

VH

  

[![First Come, First Serve icon](/images/c/c9/First_Come%2C_First_Serve.jpg)](/File:First_Come,_First_Serve.jpg "First Come, First Serve icon")

First Come, First Serve

Starting as a Western technology custom nation in North America or South America with no more than 200 points, unite the two continents.

*   [![Nation designer.png](/images/a/ab/Nation_designer.png)](/Nation_designer "Nation designer") Playing as a custom nation
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Only 1 custom nation exists in the world
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") Used no more than 201 nation designer points
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World").
*   [![Western technology group](/images/thumb/9/95/Western.png/28px-Western.png)](/Technology_group "Western technology group") Is in western technology group
*   [![Capital.png](/images/thumb/6/6e/Capital.png/28px-Capital.png)](/Capital "Capital") Capital is on the [North](/North_America "North America") or [South American](/South_America "South America") continent.

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Owns or has a core on all habitable land provinces in the continents of [North](/North_America "North America") and [South America](/South_America "South America")

There must not be any empty provinces in the Americas, but it is not necessary to finish the colonies. Let the Colonial Nations do most of the job; their overlords will not defend them in a war. Only native provinces give OE; this means you are able to annex the Colonial Nations in one war, but do the war before they break free. Provinces which you own don't have to be cored, so you can leave provinces uncored if they don't give OE.

[![El Dorado.png](/images/thumb/1/16/El_Dorado.png/28px-El_Dorado.png)](/El_Dorado "El Dorado")

[Foremost Servitor of Jagannath](/Foremost_Servitor_of_Jagannath "Foremost Servitor of Jagannath")

Start as Orissa and own or have a subject own all tropical wood provinces.

[![Tropical Wood.png](/images/thumb/f/f7/Tropical_Wood.png/28px-Tropical_Wood.png)](/Tropical_wood "Tropical wood") All provinces with tropical wood are owned by the player's country or its non-tributary [subjects](/Subjects "Subjects").

[1.9](/1.9 "1.9")

[![Frozen Assets icon](/images/2/27/Frozen_Assets.jpg)](/File:Frozen_Assets.jpg "Frozen Assets icon")

Frozen Assets

Start as Novgorod and control 90% of the trade power in the White Sea trade node while it is the highest valued trade node in the world.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Novgorod](/images/thumb/5/5e/Novgorod.png/20px-Novgorod.png)](/Novgorod "Novgorod") [Novgorod](/Novgorod "Novgorod")

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Have 90% trade share in White Sea and it's the highest valued trade node in the world.

*   Forming other nations will not prevent this achievement.
*   Note that "highest valued trade" means Total trade value _minus_ outgoing trade.
*   Not too difficult once you become powerful. You should be able to steer most asian trade towards the white sea. Trade and plutocratic ideas will be helpful.

[1.14](/1.14 "1.14")

VH

[![Gothic Invasion icon](/images/c/ce/Gothic_Invasion.png)](/File:Gothic_Invasion.png "Gothic Invasion icon")

Gothic Invasion

Start as Theodoro and conquer all Germanic culture provinces in Europe.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Theodoro](/images/thumb/1/11/Theodoro.png/20px-Theodoro.png)](/Theodoro "Theodoro") [Theodoro](/Theodoro "Theodoro")

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") All provinces with _Germanic_ culture group in Europe owned by [![Flag of Theodoro](/images/thumb/1/11/Theodoro.png/20px-Theodoro.png)](/Theodoro "Theodoro") [Theodoro](/Theodoro "Theodoro")
*   [![Culture icon.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Culture_icon.png/28px-Culture_icon.png)](/Culture "Culture") Culture is _Gothic_

Forming other nations will make this achievement much more difficult, because then all _Germanic_ cultured provinces in Europe have to be converted to another culture to fulfill the requirements. This does not apply if the formed country is a [Former colonial nation formable](/Formable_countries#Former_colonial_nations "Formable countries") and Theodoro still has provinces in the old world, because forming such a country as Theodoro keeps Theodoro alive so the achievement can still be fulfilled by feeding all _Germanic_ provinces in Europe to Theodoro if they are later vassalized. Note though that playing as a released colonial nation doesn't work, because it counts as playing as a released vassal.
