*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Perm](/images/thumb/8/8e/Perm.png/20px-Perm.png)](/Perm "Perm") [Perm](/Perm "Perm")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") All provinces in the [Canada](/North_American_regions#Canada "North American regions"), [Cascadia](/Cascadia "Cascadia"), [Hudson Bay](/Hudson_Bay "Hudson Bay"), [East Siberia](/Asian_regions "Asian regions"), [West Siberia](/Asian_regions "Asian regions"), [Scandinavia](/Scandinavia_(region) "Scandinavia (region)"), [Russia](/Russia_(region) "Russia (region)") and [Ural](/Ural "Ural") regions are owned by [![Flag of Perm](/images/thumb/8/8e/Perm.png/20px-Perm.png)](/Perm "Perm") [Perm](/Perm "Perm") _or_ its non-tributary [subjects](/Subjects "Subjects").

[1.14](/1.14 "1.14")

VH

[![I'll graze my horse here.. And here... icon](/images/d/d0/I%27ll_graze_my_horse_here.._And_here....png)](/File:I%27ll_graze_my_horse_here.._And_here....png "I'll graze my horse here.. And here... icon")

I'll graze my horse here.. And here...

As a Horde, own over 200 provinces producing grain.

[![Tab domestic government.png](/images/thumb/f/ff/Tab_domestic_government.png/28px-Tab_domestic_government.png)](/File:Tab_domestic_government.png) Government type is [![Government native.png](/images/thumb/a/a8/Government_native.png/28px-Government_native.png)](/Steppe_nomads "Steppe nomads") _Steppe Nomads_

*   [![Government native.png](/images/thumb/a/a8/Government_native.png/28px-Government_native.png)](/Steppe_nomads "Steppe nomads") Has Steppe Nomad or Great Mongol State reform
*   [![Goods produced modifier.png](/images/thumb/1/12/Goods_produced_modifier.png/28px-Goods_produced_modifier.png)](/Goods_produced_modifier "Goods produced modifier") 200 provinces produce grain _or_ livestock

[1.20](/1.20 "1.20")

VH

[![Inner Turmoil icon](/images/6/61/Inner_Turmoil.png)](/File:Inner_Turmoil.png "Inner Turmoil icon")

Inner Turmoil

Starting as The Isles, own 20 provinces by 1500, none of which are on Islands.

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of The Isles](/images/thumb/a/ae/The_Isles.png/20px-The_Isles.png)](/The_Isles "The Isles") [The Isles](/The_Isles "The Isles")
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World")

*   [![Time Icon.png](/images/7/70/Time_Icon.png)](/Time "Time") The year is before 1500
*   owns at least 20 provinces that are _not_ [on an island](/Island#province_is_on_an_island "Island")

it is allowed to have provinces on islands, but these don't count towards the 20. Islands in the context of this achievement means any province which does not have a land connection to mainland continents, meaning any province in Britain or Ireland will not count. Unfinished colonies also don't count. An easy way to achieve this is to wait until one of the berber nations is without allies and noCB them. You can core Moroccan and Sus provinces with extended range from exploration ideas and the colonial range advisor. From there, you can keep eating North Africa, or go to West Africa. The provinces do not need to be cored.

VH

[![Jihad icon](/images/e/ee/Jihad.jpg)](/File:Jihad.jpg "Jihad icon")

Jihad

As Najd, own 500 Sunni provinces.

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Najd](/images/thumb/c/c9/Najd.png/20px-Najd.png)](/Najd "Najd") [Najd](/Najd "Najd")
*   [![Tolerance of the true faith.png](/images/thumb/d/d9/Tolerance_of_the_true_faith.png/28px-Tolerance_of_the_true_faith.png)](/Tolerance_of_the_true_faith "Tolerance of the true faith") Religion is [![Sunni Islam](/images/thumb/2/2f/Sunni.png/28px-Sunni.png)](/Sunni "Sunni") Sunni

*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own **500** provinces with Sunni religion
*   [![Sunni Islam](/images/thumb/2/2f/Sunni.png/28px-Sunni.png)](/Sunni "Sunni") Is Sunni

Easier to achieve as many new provinces were added to the game since release.

KHAAAAAAN

Restore the Mongol Empire before the Age of Absolutism.

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is the [![Flag of Mongol Empire](/images/thumb/e/e4/Mongol_Empire.png/20px-Mongol_Empire.png)](/Mongol_Empire "Mongol Empire") [Mongol Empire](/Mongol_Empire "Mongol Empire")

[![Komnenoi Empire icon](/images/5/58/Komnenoi_Empire.jpg)](/File:Komnenoi_Empire.jpg "Komnenoi Empire icon")

Komnenoi Empire

As Trebizond, have the Empire government rank.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Trebizond](/images/thumb/1/1f/Trebizond.png/20px-Trebizond.png)](/Trebizond "Trebizond") [Trebizond](/Trebizond "Trebizond")

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Trebizond](/images/thumb/1/1f/Trebizond.png/20px-Trebizond.png)](/Trebizond "Trebizond") [Trebizond](/Trebizond "Trebizond")
*   [![Empire rank](/images/thumb/9/9d/Empire.png/28px-Empire.png)](/Government_rank "Empire rank") Is empire

Forming [![Flag of Byzantium](/images/thumb/9/96/Byzantium.png/20px-Byzantium.png)](/Byzantium "Byzantium") [Byzantium](/Byzantium "Byzantium") or another country _will_ prevent the achievement. Possible tactics include trying to become the emperor of the HRE or culture-shifting to Bulgarian and enact Bulgarian Tsardom government, as these will immediately make you an empire.

Meissner Porcelain

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Saxony](/images/thumb/7/74/Saxony.png/20px-Saxony.png)](/Saxony "Saxony") [Saxony](/Saxony "Saxony")
*   [![Chinaware.png](/images/thumb/9/92/Chinaware.png/28px-Chinaware.png)](/Chinaware "Chinaware") All provinces with chinaware are owned by Saxony or its non-tributary [subjects](/Subjects "Subjects").

Chinaware appears in China, Japan, Korea and the East Indies.

Never say Nevers

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Nevers](/images/thumb/9/99/Nevers.png/20px-Nevers.png)](/Nevers "Nevers") [Nevers](/Nevers "Nevers")

[1.26](/1.26 "1.26")

VH

[![New, New Deli icon](/images/7/7f/New%2C_New_Deli.jpg)](/File:New,_New_Deli.jpg "New, New Deli icon")

New, New Deli

As Deli, have your capital in the Delhi province.

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Deli](/images/thumb/0/07/Deli.png/20px-Deli.png)](/Deli "Deli") [Deli](/Deli "Deli")
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Deli](/images/thumb/0/07/Deli.png/20px-Deli.png)](/Deli "Deli") [Deli](/Deli "Deli")
*   [![Capital.png](/images/thumb/6/6e/Capital.png/28px-Capital.png)](/Capital "Capital") Capital is Delhi (522)

This achievement is only visible if the [![Leviathan.png](/images/thumb/0/0a/Leviathan.png/28px-Leviathan.png)](/Leviathan "Leviathan") Leviathan DLC is active, but it can be achieved even without the DLC.

Can be done in 5–10 years, depending on RNG. Broadly: get as many allies as you can to deter coalition. Vassalize an OPM adjacent to [![Flag of Delhi](/images/thumb/d/d5/Delhi.png/20px-Delhi.png)](/Delhi "Delhi") [Delhi](/Delhi "Delhi"), preferably [![Flag of Garhwal](/images/thumb/d/dd/Garhwal.png/20px-Garhwal.png)](/Garhwal "Garhwal") [Garhwal](/Garhwal "Garhwal") or [![Flag of Sirmur](/images/thumb/0/0e/Sirmur.png/20px-Sirmur.png)](/Sirmur "Sirmur") [Sirmur](/Sirmur "Sirmur") to even the AE. Then conquer Delhi (and some needed to connect). Give every other territories to vassals, or sell them to other countries. In a war, lose your capital Riau, after that Delhi will be the new capital.

[1.31](/1.31 "1.31")

VH

[![Norwegian Wood icon](/images/a/ad/Norwegian_Wood.jpg)](/File:Norwegian_Wood.jpg "Norwegian Wood icon")

Norwegian Wood

Own or have a subject own all naval supplies provinces as Norway.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Norway](/images/thumb/0/0f/Norway.png/20px-Norway.png)](/Norway "Norway") [Norway](/Norway "Norway")

[![Naval supplies.png](/images/thumb/f/f1/Naval_supplies.png/28px-Naval_supplies.png)](/Naval_supplies "Naval supplies") All provinces with naval supplies are owned by [![Flag of Norway](/images/thumb/0/0f/Norway.png/20px-Norway.png)](/Norway "Norway") [Norway](/Norway "Norway") _or_ its direct [subjects](/Subject "Subject"), but _no_ [tributary states](/Tributary_state "Tributary state").

As Norway, or Norway's non-tributary subjects, needs to own all the naval supply provinces, forming another nation is not recommended.

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Quizquiz](/images/thumb/b/b3/Quizquiz.png/20px-Quizquiz.png)](/Quizquiz "Quizquiz") [Quizquiz](/Quizquiz "Quizquiz")
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World")

[1.31](/1.31 "1.31")

VH

[![Rags and Riches icon](/images/0/0d/Rags_and_Riches.jpg)](/File:Rags_and_Riches.jpg "Rags and Riches icon")

Rags and Riches

Have the highest income in the world while neither owning nor starting with a province with a development level higher than 10.

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") No owned province has more than [![Development.png](/images/thumb/a/a4/Development.png/28px-Development.png)](/Development "Development") 10 development at the start of the game

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") No owned province has more than [![Development.png](/images/thumb/a/a4/Development.png/28px-Development.png)](/Development "Development") 10 development
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") No other country has a higher income than this country

One possible start is [![Flag of Norway](/images/thumb/0/0f/Norway.png/20px-Norway.png)](/Norway "Norway") [Norway](/Norway "Norway"). Stay as a vassal under [![Flag of Denmark](/images/thumb/6/69/Denmark.png/20px-Denmark.png)](/Denmark "Denmark") [Denmark](/Denmark "Denmark") for protection, rush expansion ideas, then get exploration after you reach diplomatic tech 7, and colonize Newfoundland from there, triggering the Grand Banks Fisheries which will power your colonial nation of Vinland. After Vinland forms, you can release and choose to play as them well within the time-frame of Denmark beginning integration, bypassing the PU. From there, expand and build as many manufactories as possible, swapping into Canada or Quebec's ideas, or even the USA. An important thing to note is that you can have a 10+ development province after the start of the campaign, but not during the month you're trying to count the highest income.

A great alternative start is [![Flag of Wolgast](/images/thumb/f/f6/Wolgast.png/20px-Wolgast.png)](/Wolgast "Wolgast") [Wolgast](/Wolgast "Wolgast"). Play the regular HRE game, expanding into Denmark and Russia. Exploit all provinces within 10-20 development (requires [![Cradle of Civilization.png](/images/thumb/2/23/Cradle_of_Civilization.png/28px-Cradle_of_Civilization.png)](/Cradle_of_Civilization "Cradle of Civilization") Cradle of Civilization), boost development of all provinces below 10. Eventually, your income from flat 10 dev provinces will be the highest in the world, especially if you consider expanding into the west and taking control over the Channel. Keep all high dev provinces like Lübeck under vassals.

Another good variant is [![Flag of Kilwa](/images/thumb/c/cb/Kilwa.png/20px-Kilwa.png)](/Kilwa "Kilwa") [Kilwa](/Kilwa "Kilwa"). Having Feudalism makes your country a dominant power in region, and you can easily expand. Almost all conquered provinces have development below 11 dev, so you will not need to exploit them (it takes much time). You can get 5 provinces with gold at the start and another 2 in Ethiopia. Other provinces also have good resources like ivory. Also your home trade nodes (Zanzibar and Cape) are convenient for collecting – you can increase income by steering trade from India and Malacca. At the start you should rush to admin tech 5 and get colonists for colonizing coasts (especially Cape) before the Europeans.

The game does its check for highest income on every monthly tick meaning you could release nations from all your provinces with more than ten development and still get the achievement even if the next monthly tick would see your income drop tremendously as long as on the previous month tick, you had the highest income.

Raja of the Rajput Reich

Conquer all of Germany as Nagaur.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Nagaur](/images/thumb/e/e4/Nagaur.png/20px-Nagaur.png)](/Nagaur "Nagaur") [Nagaur](/Nagaur "Nagaur")

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") All provinces in [North Germany](/North_Germany "North Germany") and [South Germany](/South_Germany "South Germany") regions are owned by the player's country _or_ its non-tributary [subjects](/Subjects "Subjects").

Expand

[![Raja of the Rajput Reich map.png](/images/thumb/5/5e/Raja_of_the_Rajput_Reich_map.png/140px-Raja_of_the_Rajput_Reich_map.png)](/File:Raja_of_the_Rajput_Reich_map.png)

[](/File:Raja_of_the_Rajput_Reich_map.png "Enlarge")

Forming other nations won't prevent getting the achievement, including [![Flag of Mughals](/images/thumb/e/e6/Mughals.png/20px-Mughals.png)](/Mughals "Mughals") [Mughals](/Mughals "Mughals"), [![Flag of Hindustan](/images/thumb/3/3e/Hindustan.png/20px-Hindustan.png)](/Hindustan "Hindustan") [Hindustan](/Hindustan "Hindustan"), and [![Flag of Delhi](/images/thumb/d/d5/Delhi.png/20px-Delhi.png)](/Delhi "Delhi") [Delhi](/Delhi "Delhi").

[![Saladin's Legacy icon](/images/f/fb/Saladin%27s_Legacy.png)](/File:Saladin%27s_Legacy.png "Saladin's Legacy icon")

Saladin's Legacy

Playing as Hisn Kayfa, reforge the Ayyubid Empire.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Hisn Kayfa](/images/thumb/4/4c/Hisn_Kayfa.png/20px-Hisn_Kayfa.png)](/Hisn_Kayfa "Hisn Kayfa") [Hisn Kayfa](/Hisn_Kayfa "Hisn Kayfa")

[![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own the following provinces:

Expand

[![Saladin's Legacy map.png](/images/thumb/2/20/Saladin%27s_Legacy_map.png/140px-Saladin%27s_Legacy_map.png)](/File:Saladin%27s_Legacy_map.png)

[](/File:Saladin%27s_Legacy_map.png "Enlarge")

Forming [![Flag of Mughals](/images/thumb/e/e6/Mughals.png/20px-Mughals.png)](/Mughals "Mughals") [Mughals](/Mughals "Mughals"), [![Flag of Persia](/images/thumb/0/01/Persia.png/20px-Persia.png)](/Persia "Persia") [Persia](/Persia "Persia"), [![Flag of Mamluks](/images/thumb/c/ca/The_Mamluks.png/20px-The_Mamluks.png)](/Mamluks "Mamluks") [Mamluks](/Mamluks "Mamluks") or another country will _not_ prevent getting the achievment.

You will most likely not be able to ally the [![Flag of Ottomans](/images/thumb/8/89/Ottomans.png/20px-Ottomans.png)](/Ottomans "Ottomans") [Ottomans](/Ottomans "Ottomans") at start. One strategy is to restart until [![Flag of Aq Qoyunlu](/images/thumb/6/67/Aq_Qoyunlu.png/20px-Aq_Qoyunlu.png)](/Aq_Qoyunlu "Aq Qoyunlu") [Aq Qoyunlu](/Aq_Qoyunlu "Aq Qoyunlu") is friendly, and allying them along with. Try to ally [![Flag of Ajam](/images/thumb/d/df/Ajam.png/20px-Ajam.png)](/Ajam "Ajam") [Ajam](/Ajam "Ajam"), [![Flag of Mamluks](/images/thumb/c/ca/The_Mamluks.png/20px-The_Mamluks.png)](/Mamluks "Mamluks") [Mamluks](/Mamluks "Mamluks") and attack [![Flag of Qara Qoyunlu](/images/thumb/9/99/Qara_Qoyunlu.png/20px-Qara_Qoyunlu.png)](/Qara_Qoyunlu "Qara Qoyunlu") [Qara Qoyunlu](/Qara_Qoyunlu "Qara Qoyunlu") together. You can ally these two at start. If they pick QQ as a rival, and you pick "Lenient taxation" Iqta ability (that gives +1 diplomatic reputation; requires [![Cradle of Civilization.png](/images/thumb/2/23/Cradle_of_Civilization.png/28px-Cradle_of_Civilization.png)](/Cradle_of_Civilization "Cradle of Civilization") Cradle of Civilization).

[![Spanish Fly icon](/images/6/6e/Spanish_Fly.png)](/File:Spanish_Fly.png "Spanish Fly icon")

Spanish Fly

Starting as Offaly, secure a Personal Union over an Iberian nation.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Offaly](/images/thumb/3/3a/Offaly.png/20px-Offaly.png)](/Offaly "Offaly") [Offaly](/Offaly "Offaly")

*   [![Personal union.png](/images/thumb/3/39/Personal_union.png/28px-Personal_union.png)](/Personal_union "Personal union") Lead a [personal union](/Personal_union "Personal union") over a country whose [![Capital.png](/images/thumb/6/6e/Capital.png/28px-Capital.png)](/Capital "Capital") capital fulfills both of the following conditions:
    *   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") is in the [Iberia region](/Iberia "Iberia")
    *   [![Culture icon.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Culture_icon.png/28px-Culture_icon.png)](/Culture "Culture") has a province culture in the [Iberian culture group](/Iberian "Iberian")

Forming [![Flag of Ireland](/images/thumb/4/4b/Ireland.png/20px-Ireland.png)](/Ireland "Ireland") [Ireland](/Ireland "Ireland") or another country _will not_ prevent the achievement but instead only hiding its conditions. Take a single Spanish province with a core of another tag and release that tag as a vassal. Place dynasty member on the throne (needs the [![Common Sense.png](/images/thumb/e/e4/Common_Sense.png/28px-Common_Sense.png)](/Common_Sense "Common Sense") Common Sense DLC) and annex the vassal. Return their core via the province screen to release them as an independent nation with your dynasty ruling. Claim their throne, immediately declare with restoration of union CB and enforce union for the achievement.

[1.28](/1.28 "1.28")

VH

[![Sunset Invasion icon](/images/a/a2/Sunset_Invasion.jpg)](/File:Sunset_Invasion.jpg "Sunset Invasion icon")

Sunset Invasion

Own and have cores on Lisbon, Madrid, Paris, London, Amsterdam and Rome as the Aztecs.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Aztec](/images/thumb/e/ef/Aztec.png/20px-Aztec.png)](/Aztec "Aztec") [Aztec](/Aztec "Aztec")

[![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own and core the provinces of Lisboa, Madrid, Paris, London, Amsterdam, and Roma.

Expand

[![Sunset Invasion map.png](/images/thumb/b/b4/Sunset_Invasion_map.png/140px-Sunset_Invasion_map.png)](/File:Sunset_Invasion_map.png)

[](/File:Sunset_Invasion_map.png "Enlarge")

As a New World country European overlords will not automatically join defensive wars against their colonies by you, establish a power base in North America, then you can either get allies (unlikely as most will desire your gold provinces too much) or an effective strategy is try to trigger a defensive war, or attack a colonial province still controlled by the overlord. In the following peace treaty take European provinces from them, that way you can easily ship over your elite troops in peace time without the need to also build up a large armada. With the Unrestricted Conquest [ability from the Age of Revolutions](/Ages#Abilities_4 "Ages") you can take any province making it easy to take capitals without the need of conquering a lot of adjacent provinces.

[1.2](/1.2 "1.2")

VH

[![The Buddhists Strike Back icon](/images/0/0e/The_Buddhists_Strike_Back.jpg)](/File:The_Buddhists_Strike_Back.jpg "The Buddhists Strike Back icon")

[The Buddhists Strike Back](/The_Buddhists_Strike_Back "The Buddhists Strike Back")

As Kotte or Kandy, own all of India and convert it to Theravada Buddhism.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as _either_:

*    [![Flag of Kotte](/images/thumb/3/3e/Kotte.png/20px-Kotte.png)](/Kotte "Kotte") [Kotte](/Kotte "Kotte")
*    [![Flag of Kandy](/images/thumb/1/1b/Kandy.png/20px-Kandy.png)](/Kandy "Kandy") [Kandy](/Kandy "Kandy")

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own and core all of the provinces in the [Indian sub-continent](/India_(sub-continent) "India (sub-continent)").
*   [![Theravada.png](/images/thumb/5/52/Theravada.png/28px-Theravada.png)](/Theravada "Theravada") All of the provinces in the [Indian sub-continent](/India_(sub-continent) "India (sub-continent)") are Theravada

Taking the province of Pataliputra will give an extra missionary. The monuments [Bagan Temples](/Bagan_Temples "Bagan Temples") and [Buddha Statues](/Buddha_Statues "Buddha Statues") give additional missionaries. If playing as Kandy, you'll likely also get the achievement [Cotton Kandy](/Cotton_Kandy "Cotton Kandy").

[![Trade power.png](/images/thumb/1/10/Trade_power.png/28px-Trade_power.png)](/Trade_power "Trade power") Have at least 90% trade power in Katsina, Safi, Timbuktu and Tunis trade nodes

[The Great Khan](/The_Great_Khan "The Great Khan")

Starting as Mongolia or Great Horde, own or have a subject own the Chinese, Russian and Persian regions.

Expand

[![EU4TheGreatKhanRequirements.png](/images/thumb/8/88/EU4TheGreatKhanRequirements.png/140px-EU4TheGreatKhanRequirements.png)](/File:EU4TheGreatKhanRequirements.png)

[](/File:EU4TheGreatKhanRequirements.png "Enlarge")

The [Caucasia](/Caucasia "Caucasia") region is not needed even though it gets highlighted by the in-game achievement list.

Forming [![Flag of Golden Horde](/images/thumb/6/62/Golden_Horde.png/20px-Golden_Horde.png)](/Golden_Horde "Golden Horde") [Golden Horde](/Golden_Horde "Golden Horde"), [![Flag of Mongol Empire](/images/thumb/e/e4/Mongol_Empire.png/20px-Mongol_Empire.png)](/Mongol_Empire "Mongol Empire") [Mongol Empire](/Mongol_Empire "Mongol Empire"), [![Flag of Yuan](/images/thumb/a/a8/Yuan.png/20px-Yuan.png)](/Yuan "Yuan") [Yuan](/Yuan "Yuan") or any other country does not prevent the player from getting the achievement.

[1.6](/1.6 "1.6")

VH

[![The Pheasant Strut icon](/images/7/72/The_Pheasant_Strut.png)](/File:The_Pheasant_Strut.png "The Pheasant Strut icon")

The Pheasant Strut

As Gorkha form Nepal and defeat Prussia with at least 100,000 Prussian casualties in a war (both have to be primary targets of war).

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Gorkha](/images/thumb/f/f8/Gorkha.png/20px-Gorkha.png)](/Gorkha "Gorkha") [Gorkha](/Gorkha "Gorkha")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Nepal](/images/thumb/3/3a/Nepal.png/20px-Nepal.png)](/Nepal "Nepal") [Nepal](/Nepal "Nepal")
*    [![Flag of Prussia](/images/thumb/2/28/Prussia.png/20px-Prussia.png)](/Prussia "Prussia") [Prussia](/Prussia "Prussia") must have lost at least 100,000 men in battles against [![Flag of Nepal](/images/thumb/3/3a/Nepal.png/20px-Nepal.png)](/Nepal "Nepal") [Nepal](/Nepal "Nepal") in one war with both as primary participants

The game only counts the losses in battles which show [![Flag of Prussia](/images/thumb/2/28/Prussia.png/20px-Prussia.png)](/Prussia "Prussia") [Prussia](/Prussia "Prussia")'s flag in the battle list at the bottom of the war overview screen. If there are other countries on Prussia's side, battles which show their flag are not counted. But their losses are counted in battles which show Prussia's flag.

 [![Flag of Brandenburg](/images/thumb/e/e3/Brandenburg.png/20px-Brandenburg.png)](/Brandenburg "Brandenburg") [Brandenburg](/Brandenburg "Brandenburg") or [![Flag of Teutonic Order](/images/thumb/2/2f/Teutonic_Order.png/20px-Teutonic_Order.png)](/Teutonic_Order "Teutonic Order") [Teutonic Order](/Teutonic_Order "Teutonic Order") can form Prussia even when subjects, though they'll still need to be Protestant or Reformed. If Prussia doesn't form naturally, you can create them by vassalizing one of the above tags and giving them the required provinces, helping them grow large enough to field a lot of troops and declaring war on them once they form Prussia.

[1.26](/1.26 "1.26")

VH

[![The Re-Reconquista icon](/images/9/99/The_Re-Reconquista.jpg)](/File:The_Re-Reconquista.jpg "The Re-Reconquista icon")

The Re-Reconquista

As Granada, form Andalusia and reconquer all of Iberia.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Granada](/images/thumb/a/a7/Granada.png/20px-Granada.png)](/Granada "Granada") [Granada](/Granada "Granada")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Andalusia](/images/thumb/0/09/Andalusia.png/20px-Andalusia.png)](/Andalusia "Andalusia") [Andalusia](/Andalusia "Andalusia")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own and core all provinces of [Iberia](/Iberia "Iberia")

Optimal strategy is to start expanding to north Africa by picking weak targets like [![Flag of Tlemcen](/images/thumb/b/b2/Tlemcen.png/20px-Tlemcen.png)](/Tlemcen "Tlemcen") [Tlemcen](/Tlemcen "Tlemcen") and [![Flag of Tunis](/images/thumb/7/79/Tunis.png/20px-Tunis.png)](/Tunis "Tunis") [Tunis](/Tunis "Tunis"). After the initial expansions, secure an alliance with either [![Flag of Ottomans](/images/thumb/8/89/Ottomans.png/20px-Ottomans.png)](/Ottomans "Ottomans") [Ottomans](/Ottomans "Ottomans") or [![Flag of Mamluks](/images/thumb/c/ca/The_Mamluks.png/20px-The_Mamluks.png)](/Mamluks "Mamluks") [Mamluks](/Mamluks "Mamluks") as soon as possible. Colonizing North America early can boost your income and drastically weaken the economy of [![Flag of Spain](/images/thumb/5/58/Spain.png/20px-Spain.png)](/Spain "Spain") [Spain](/Spain "Spain").

[1.4](/1.4 "1.4")

VH

[![The Third Way icon](/images/2/27/The_Third_Way.jpg)](/File:The_Third_Way.jpg "The Third Way icon")

[The Third Way](/The_Third_Way "The Third Way")

Start as an Ibadi nation and eliminate all rival schools of Islam (do not convert to another religion).

[![Tolerance of the true faith.png](/images/thumb/d/d9/Tolerance_of_the_true_faith.png/28px-Tolerance_of_the_true_faith.png)](/Tolerance_of_the_true_faith "Tolerance of the true faith") Religion is [![Ibadi Islam](/images/thumb/0/02/Ibadi.png/28px-Ibadi.png)](/Ibadi "Ibadi") Ibadi

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ playing as a [released vassal](/Vassal#Release_a_nation "Vassal")
*   [![Ibadi Islam](/images/thumb/0/02/Ibadi.png/28px-Ibadi.png)](/Ibadi "Ibadi") Is Ibadi
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") No province is [![Sunni Islam](/images/thumb/2/2f/Sunni.png/28px-Sunni.png)](/Sunni "Sunni") Sunni or [![Shiite Islam](/images/thumb/5/5c/Shiite.png/28px-Shiite.png)](/Shiite "Shiite") Shia.

Possible starts are [![Flag of Mzab](/images/thumb/6/62/Mzab.png/20px-Mzab.png)](/Mzab "Mzab") [Mzab](/Mzab "Mzab"), [![Flag of Oman](/images/thumb/2/27/Oman.png/20px-Oman.png)](/Oman "Oman") [Oman](/Oman "Oman"), and [![Flag of Pate](/images/thumb/e/e8/Pate.png/20px-Pate.png)](/Pate "Pate") [Pate](/Pate "Pate"). Uncolonized provinces with Muslim religion (south of Morocco, Tunis and Ethiopia) must also be colonized and converted to Ibadi. With [![Golden Century.png](/images/thumb/b/bb/Golden_Century.png/28px-Golden_Century.png)](/Golden_Century "Golden Century") Golden Century, European countries like [![Flag of Spain](/images/thumb/5/58/Spain.png/20px-Spain.png)](/Spain "Spain") [Spain](/Spain "Spain") and [![Flag of Portugal](/images/thumb/1/12/Portugal.png/20px-Portugal.png)](/Portugal "Portugal") [Portugal](/Portugal "Portugal") can convert provinces in the colonial regions to Islam by expelling minorities. Those provinces must be converted to Ibadi as well.

 [![Flag of Persia](/images/thumb/0/01/Persia.png/20px-Persia.png)](/Persia "Persia") [Persia](/Persia "Persia") can be formed by a nation whose primary culture is in the Iranian culture group, or by [![Flag of Aq Qoyunlu](/images/thumb/6/67/Aq_Qoyunlu.png/20px-Aq_Qoyunlu.png)](/Aq_Qoyunlu "Aq Qoyunlu") [Aq Qoyunlu](/Aq_Qoyunlu "Aq Qoyunlu").

Ultimate Military

As Songhai, have Prussia and Nepal as marches!

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Songhai](/images/thumb/2/24/Songhai.png/20px-Songhai.png)](/Songhai "Songhai") [Songhai](/Songhai "Songhai")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Songhai](/images/thumb/2/24/Songhai.png/20px-Songhai.png)](/Songhai "Songhai") [Songhai](/Songhai "Songhai")
*   [![March icon.png](/images/thumb/1/1d/March_icon.png/28px-March_icon.png)](/March "March") Have [![Flag of Prussia](/images/thumb/2/28/Prussia.png/20px-Prussia.png)](/Prussia "Prussia") [Prussia](/Prussia "Prussia") _and_ [![Flag of Nepal](/images/thumb/3/3a/Nepal.png/20px-Nepal.png)](/Nepal "Nepal") [Nepal](/Nepal "Nepal") as marches.

This achievement is only visible if the [![Origins.png](/images/thumb/8/8e/Origins.png/28px-Origins.png)](/Origins "Origins") Origins DLC is active, but it actually needs the [![Art of War.png](/images/thumb/0/0f/Art_of_War.png/28px-Art_of_War.png)](/Art_of_War "Art of War") Art of War DLC to create marches.

 [![Flag of Songhai](/images/thumb/2/24/Songhai.png/20px-Songhai.png)](/Songhai "Songhai") [Songhai](/Songhai "Songhai") has a strong starting position, the main difficulty is making sure both [![Flag of Prussia](/images/thumb/2/28/Prussia.png/20px-Prussia.png)](/Prussia "Prussia") [Prussia](/Prussia "Prussia") and [![Flag of Nepal](/images/thumb/3/3a/Nepal.png/20px-Nepal.png)](/Nepal "Nepal") [Nepal](/Nepal "Nepal") exist. Note that only [![Flag of Prussia](/images/thumb/2/28/Prussia.png/20px-Prussia.png)](/Prussia "Prussia") [Prussia](/Prussia "Prussia") can be formed by a subject nation, so you are better off giving a Nepali minor the required provinces by calling them to war as ally before subjugating them.

Where the heart is

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Dahomey](/images/thumb/f/f1/Dahomey.png/20px-Dahomey.png)](/Dahomey "Dahomey") [Dahomey](/Dahomey "Dahomey")

Expand

[![Niger and Sahel map.png](/images/thumb/d/d7/Niger_and_Sahel_map.png/140px-Niger_and_Sahel_map.png)](/File:Niger_and_Sahel_map.png)

[](/File:Niger_and_Sahel_map.png "Enlarge")

*   The owner must be Fetishist, not the province. Possible to do by feeding lots of land to a Sunni vassal and then enforcing religion.

[1.20](/1.20 "1.20")

VH

[![World Conqueror icon](/images/7/7d/World_Conqueror.jpg)](/File:World_Conqueror.jpg "World Conqueror icon")

World Conqueror

Own or have a subject own the entire world.

[![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World").

The only existing countries are the player's country and its direct non-tributary [subjects](/Subject "Subject") and their non-tributary [subjects](/Subject "Subject").

*   Subjects of subjects count as long as they are not tributaries (e.g., Colonies of a client state or Vassals of a personal union). But colonial nations of a vassal of a junior partner don't count, because they are subjects of a subject of a subject.

[1.1](/Patch_1.1.X "Patch 1.1.X")

VH

[![All Blue icon](/images/a/a8/All_Blue.png)](/File:All_Blue.png "All Blue icon")

All Blue

As Portugal, all Europe is owned by you or blue European countries that exist in 1444.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Portugal](/images/thumb/1/12/Portugal.png/20px-Portugal.png)](/Portugal "Portugal") [Portugal](/Portugal "Portugal")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Portugal](/images/thumb/1/12/Portugal.png/20px-Portugal.png)](/Portugal "Portugal") [Portugal](/Portugal "Portugal")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") All provinces in [europe](/Europe "Europe") are owned by one of the following countries:
    
    *    [![Flag of Portugal](/images/thumb/1/12/Portugal.png/20px-Portugal.png)](/Portugal "Portugal") [Portugal](/Portugal "Portugal")
    *    [![Flag of Avaria](/images/thumb/4/47/Avaria.png/20px-Avaria.png)](/Avaria "Avaria") [Avaria](/Avaria "Avaria")
    *    [![Flag of Bavaria](/images/thumb/b/b3/Bavaria.png/20px-Bavaria.png)](/Bavaria "Bavaria") [Bavaria](/Bavaria "Bavaria")
    *    [![Flag of Bourbonnais](/images/thumb/5/5d/Bourbonnais.png/20px-Bourbonnais.png)](/Bourbonnais "Bourbonnais") [Bourbonnais](/Bourbonnais "Bourbonnais")
    *    [![Flag of Bremen](/images/thumb/c/c4/Bremen.png/20px-Bremen.png)](/Bremen "Bremen") [Bremen](/Bremen "Bremen")
    *    [![Flag of Dithmarschen](/images/thumb/3/34/Dithmarschen.png/20px-Dithmarschen.png)](/Dithmarschen "Dithmarschen") [Dithmarschen](/Dithmarschen "Dithmarschen")
    *    [![Flag of Dortmund](/images/thumb/0/08/Dortmund.png/20px-Dortmund.png)](/Dortmund "Dortmund") [Dortmund](/Dortmund "Dortmund")

[1.35](/1.35 "1.35")

VH

[![From Frankfurt to the Andes icon](/images/7/72/From_Frankfurt_to_the_Andes.png)](/File:From_Frankfurt_to_the_Andes.png "From Frankfurt to the Andes icon")

[From Frankfurt to the Andes](/From_Frankfurt_to_the_Andes "From Frankfurt to the Andes")

Starting as Frankfurt, form Jerusalem, and then form the Inca while owning Mallorca.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Frankfurt](/images/thumb/7/75/Frankfurt.png/20px-Frankfurt.png)](/Frankfurt "Frankfurt") [Frankfurt](/Frankfurt "Frankfurt")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Was [![Flag of Frankfurt](/images/thumb/7/75/Frankfurt.png/20px-Frankfurt.png)](/Frankfurt "Frankfurt") [Frankfurt](/Frankfurt "Frankfurt")
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Was [![Flag of Jerusalem](/images/thumb/e/ef/Jerusalem.png/20px-Jerusalem.png)](/Jerusalem "Jerusalem") [Jerusalem](/Jerusalem "Jerusalem")
*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Inca](/images/thumb/3/36/Inca.png/20px-Inca.png)](/Inca "Inca") [Inca](/Inca "Inca")
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Own Mallorca (333)

*   Hardest part of this achievement is finding and fulfilling conditions for different tag formation.
*   To form [![Flag of Jerusalem](/images/thumb/e/ef/Jerusalem.png/20px-Jerusalem.png)](/Jerusalem "Jerusalem") [Jerusalem](/Jerusalem "Jerusalem"), you need to get into coring range of Jerusalem area (vassalize an Italian minor and conquer a province next to it), own and state Jerusalem area, move capital to Arabia, Egypt or Mashriq and switch from [![Government republic.png](/images/thumb/5/5d/Government_republic.png/28px-Government_republic.png)](/Republic "Republic") Republic to [![Government monarchy.png](/images/thumb/4/4d/Government_monarchy.png/28px-Government_monarchy.png)](/Monarchy "Monarchy") Monarchy. And this has to be done before the Age of Reformation ends, because Frankfurt can't form Jerusalem later.
*   To form [![Flag of Inca](/images/thumb/3/36/Inca.png/20px-Inca.png)](/Inca "Inca") [Inca](/Inca "Inca") you need to move your capital to the New World, own cores on required provinces, [![Culture icon.png](/images/thumb/2/29/Culture_icon.png/28px-Culture_icon.png)](/Culture "Culture") culture shift to Andean culture and change your religion to a pagan faith via rebels.
*   Switching to play as a released vassal will invalidate the achievement.

[1.35](/1.35 "1.35")

VH

[![Eat your Greens icon](/images/6/61/Eat_your_Greens.png)](/File:Eat_your_Greens.png "Eat your Greens icon")

Eat your Greens

Control all Grasslands in Asia as Kale before the age of Absolutism.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Kale](/images/thumb/d/d1/Kale.png/20px-Kale.png)](/Kale "Kale") [Kale](/Kale "Kale")

*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") It is _not_ the [![Age of Absolutism.png](/images/thumb/e/ec/Age_of_Absolutism.png/28px-Age_of_Absolutism.png)](/Age_of_Absolutism "Age of Absolutism") Age of Absolutism or the [![Age of Revolutions.png](/images/thumb/5/59/Age_of_Revolutions.png/28px-Age_of_Revolutions.png)](/Age_of_Revolutions "Age of Revolutions") Age of Revolutions
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Every province in Asia with Grasslands terrain is owned by the player's country _or_ its non-tributary [subjects](/Subjects "Subjects")

Expand

[![](/images/thumb/d/dc/Eat_your_greens_map.png/140px-Eat_your_greens_map.png)](/File:Eat_your_greens_map.png)

[](/File:Eat_your_greens_map.png "Enlarge")

All grassland provinces in Asia

It is not required to keep playing as [![Flag of Kale](/images/thumb/d/d1/Kale.png/20px-Kale.png)](/Kale "Kale") [Kale](/Kale "Kale") to earn the achievement, but changing tag will hide it from the achievement tab.

Start by subjugating and allying all Shan minors to complete the mission "Unite the Shan" to inherit them all and gain free cores (don't conquer any province from them as these would needlessly have to be cored; best to fully annex [![Flag of Ava](/images/thumb/d/df/Ava.png/20px-Ava.png)](/Ava "Ava") [Ava](/Ava "Ava") and inherit all their tributaries). To limit AE and help with the endless conquests to come it is recommended you switch to horde government first, which is you should form [![Flag of Tibet](/images/thumb/0/03/Tibet.png/20px-Tibet.png)](/Tibet "Tibet") [Tibet](/Tibet "Tibet") and do the "Steppe Politics" mission. After choosing to invite one of the two Mongols switch culture back to Shan. Conquer enough of Indochina to form [![Flag of Siam](/images/thumb/7/7e/Siam.png/20px-Siam.png)](/Siam "Siam") [Siam](/Siam "Siam") for the ideas.

Take Horde Ideas then Expansion then Diplomatic Ideas, don't delay colonizing Siberia, you need to finish 3 colonies to reach the farthest province (2 if you conquer from [![Flag of Mongolia](/images/thumb/b/bc/Mongolia.png/20px-Mongolia.png)](/Mongolia "Mongolia") [Mongolia](/Mongolia "Mongolia").

[1.26](/1.26 "1.26")

I

[![One Faith icon](/images/e/ef/One_Faith.jpg)](/File:One_Faith.jpg "One Faith icon")

One Faith

Have all non-wasteland land provinces in the world be of your religion.

[![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") No colonized non-wasteland province has a different religion than this country.

*   Using the random new world will drastically reduce the number of provinces, especially inland ones, making this easier than with the true new world.
*   Uncolonized provinces may still be of a different religion.

 [![Flag of Najd](/images/thumb/c/c9/Najd.png/20px-Najd.png)](/Najd "Najd") [Najd](/Najd "Najd") is a recommended starting nation, since its ideas are religiously focused, including access to +2 missionaries and +2% missionary strength, as well as its starting religion of [![Sunni Islam](/images/thumb/2/2f/Sunni.png/20px-Sunni.png)](/Sunni "Sunni") [Sunni](/Sunni "Sunni") granting [![Local missionary strength.png](/images/thumb/0/08/Local_missionary_strength.png/28px-Local_missionary_strength.png)](/Local_missionary_strength "Local missionary strength") **−2%** local missionary strength which would make these provinces harder to convert.

[1.14](/1.14 "1.14")

I

[![The Three Mountains icon](/images/e/e1/The_Three_Mountains.jpg)](/File:The_Three_Mountains.jpg "The Three Mountains icon")

The Three Mountains

Own or have a subject own the entire world as Ryukyu.

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as [![Flag of Ryukyu](/images/thumb/6/64/Ryukyu.png/20px-Ryukyu.png)](/Ryukyu "Ryukyu") [Ryukyu](/Ryukyu "Ryukyu")
*   [![No](/images/thumb/5/56/Ledger_no_crop.png/28px-Ledger_no_crop.png)](/File:Ledger_no_crop.png "No") _Not_ using a [random New World](/Random_New_World "Random New World").

*   The only existing countries are:
    *   the player's country,
    *    [![Flag of Ryukyu](/images/thumb/6/64/Ryukyu.png/20px-Ryukyu.png)](/Ryukyu "Ryukyu") [Ryukyu](/Ryukyu "Ryukyu") and its [subjects](/Subject "Subject"), but _not_ [tributary states](/Tributary_state "Tributary state").

[1.1](/Patch_1.1.X "Patch 1.1.X")

I

[![True Heir of Timur icon](/images/8/8c/True_Heir_of_Timur.png)](/File:True_Heir_of_Timur.png "True Heir of Timur icon")

True Heir of Timur

Starting as a Timurid subject, form the Mughals and conquer India by 1550.

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as one of the following:
    *    [![Flag of Afghanistan](/images/thumb/7/7d/Afghanistan.png/20px-Afghanistan.png)](/Afghanistan "Afghanistan") [Afghanistan](/Afghanistan "Afghanistan")
    *    [![Flag of Sistan](/images/thumb/f/f5/Sistan.png/20px-Sistan.png)](/Sistan "Sistan") [Sistan](/Sistan "Sistan")
    *    [![Flag of Transoxiana](/images/thumb/c/c3/Transoxiana.png/20px-Transoxiana.png)](/Transoxiana "Transoxiana") [Transoxiana](/Transoxiana "Transoxiana")
    *    [![Flag of Khorasan](/images/thumb/1/1d/Khorasan.png/20px-Khorasan.png)](/Khorasan "Khorasan") [Khorasan](/Khorasan "Khorasan")
    *    [![Flag of Fars](/images/thumb/a/ab/Fars.png/20px-Fars.png)](/Fars "Fars") [Fars](/Fars "Fars")

*   [![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Is [![Flag of Mughals](/images/thumb/e/e6/Mughals.png/20px-Mughals.png)](/Mughals "Mughals") [Mughals](/Mughals "Mughals")
*   [![Time Icon.png](/images/7/70/Time_Icon.png)](/Time "Time") The year is before 1550
*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") Every province in India superregion is owned by the country or a subject other than a tributary

[1.26](/1.26 "1.26")

I

[![Mehmet's Ambition icon](/images/2/2e/Mehmet%27s_Ambition.png)](/File:Mehmet%27s_Ambition.png "Mehmet's Ambition icon")

Mehmet's Ambition

Starting as The Ottomans, own or have Core Eyalets own all the provinces required to form the Roman Empire before 1500.

[![Yes](/images/thumb/d/da/Ledger_yes.png/28px-Ledger_yes.png)](/File:Ledger_yes.png "Yes") Playing as the [![Flag of Ottomans](/images/thumb/8/89/Ottomans.png/20px-Ottomans.png)](/Ottomans "Ottomans") [Ottomans](/Ottomans "Ottomans")

*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") All provinces in the following regions are owned by this country or a subject of type Core Eyalet:
    
    *   [Italy](/Italy_(region) "Italy (region)")
    *   [France](/France_(region) "France (region)")
    *   [Iberia](/Iberia "Iberia")
    *   [Balkans](/Balkans "Balkans")
    *   [Anatolia](/Anatolia "Anatolia")
    *   [Mashriq](/Mashriq "Mashriq")
    

*   [![Province icon.png](/images/thumb/1/13/Province_icon.png/28px-Province_icon.png)](/Province "Province") The following provinces are owned by this country or a subject of type Core Eyalet:
    
    *   Fez (343)
    *   Tunis (341)
    *   Cairo (361)
    *   London (236)
    *   York (245)
    *   Zeeland (96)
    *   Wien (134)
